<I,1>

{0}

[I,1,i]

namo buddhāya ॥

[I,1,ii]

	jayati sugataḥ kṛpātmā dharmo nairyāṇikaḥ sadā jayati /
	sakalatribhuvanapūjyaḥ prathitaguṇo jayati cāryagaṇaḥ //
	param anugṛhṇanprāptaiḥ parato 'pi hi vastubhiḥ satāṃ ślāghyaḥ /
	labdhair anyamatair api tatkartuṃ parahitaṃ yuktam //
	tad atīva viprakīrṇānyācāryāṇāṃ matānyaśaknuvataḥ /
	ālocayituṃ samyagjanasya matto 'pi mandamateḥ //
	āhṛtya dharmakīrter anyeṣāṃ caiva khalu matāt kiñcit /
	tad darśitayā ca diśā svayam abhyūhya prayatnena //
	udbhāvitārthatattvasvāduraso 'yaṃ mayopakārāya /
	diṅnāganītiśāstravyākhyānakarambakaḥ kriyate //

{1.1}

[I,1,iii]

pramāṇabhūtāyetyādi । yathā —
	tvaṃ merus tvaṃ samudro 'si nātha tvaṃ kalpapādapaḥ /
	tvaṃ suvaidyaḥ pradīpas tvaṃ tvam eva paramaḥ plavaḥ //
<I,2>
ity atrevaśabdaprayogam antareṇāpi tadartho gamyate, tathehāpīti bhagavān pramāṇam iva pramāṇam । yathā hi pratyakṣādipramāṇaṃ puruṣārthopayogino 'nadhigatasyārthasya prakāśakam avisaṃvādakaṃ ca, tathā bhagavān api yatra paraḥ puruṣārthaḥ pratibaddhaś caturāryasatyalakṣaṇe tattve tadviṣayaṃ jñānam āsādya niḥśreyasārthināṃ tasyānadhigatasya prakāśako 'visaṃvādakaś ca । tasmāt pramāṇasādharmyāt pramāṇam । bhūto jātaḥ, utpanna ity arthaḥ । bhūtavacanam abhūtasya nityasyeśvarādeḥ pramāṇasya paraparikalpitasya pratiṣedhārtham । pramāṇaṃ cāsau bhūtaś ceti pramāṇabhūtaḥ, tasmai pramāṇabhūtāya ॥

[I,2,i]

nanu ca dvitīyayātra bhavitavyam, yathāsyaiva vivaraṇe — evaṅ guṇaṃ śāstāraṃ praṇamyeti । satyam, śiṣṭaprayogānusāritvād vivakṣāyā yadā karmakārakaṃ vivakṣyate । yadā tu prārthanādhyavasāyakriyābhyām āptum iṣṭamatvāl labdhakarmavyapadeśayā praṇatikriyayābhipreyamāṇasya sampradānatvaṃ vivakṣyate, tadā caturthyeva nyāyyā । yathā tathiva prāptakarmasañjñena śayanenābhipreyamāṇatvātpatyuḥ sampradānavivakṣāyāṃ patye śeta ity atra caturthyeva bhavati । tathehāpīty adoṣaḥ ॥

[I,2,ii]

jagaddhitaiṣiṇa iti । jagad dhitaṃ heyopādeyayoḥ sābhyupāyayor ātyantike hānopādāne, tadeṣaṇaśīlāya । praṇamyeti manovāl lāyaiḥ praṇāmaṃ kṛtvā । asya ca <I,3> samuccayaḥ kariṣyata ity anena sambandhaḥ । etena praṇāmataḥ pūjā jihitā ॥ śāstra iti । iṭo 'trābhāvaḥ, tṛntṛcau śaṃsikṣadādibhyaḥ sañjñāyāṃ cāniṭau । bahulam anyatrāpīti vacanāt । duḥkhakṣayopāyopadeśaḥ śāsanam । tasya kartā śāstety ucyate phalāv asthāyām । iha tu tasyaiva śāsanasya hetau mārgābhyāse phalopacārācchāsanaśabdo vartate । tacchāsanaṃ kurvan bhagavān bodhisattvāvasthāyāṃ śastṛśabdenoktaḥ ॥

[I,3,i]

sugatāyeti । suṣṭhu gataḥ prāptaḥ sarvathā sarvapraheyaprahāṇam iti sugataḥ ॥ tāyina iti । tāyate 'neneti tāyaḥ । sa punaḥ svadṛṣṭamārgopadeśaḥ । so 'syāstīti tāyī ॥

[I,3,ii]

sarvaprekṣāpūrvakāriṇāmārambhasya prayojanena vyāptatvāt tan nivartamānam ārambham api nivartayati । tac cāsya nāsti । tasmān nārabdhavyam idam । yasya prayojanaṃ nāsti, na tat prekṣāvatārabdhavyam । tad yathānanuṣṭheyaviṣayajñānaparīkṣaṇam upadeṣṭari । nāsti cāsya tat । vyāpakānupalambhaḥ । asyāsiddhim udbhāvitum āha — pramāṇasiddhyā iti । pramāṇasiddhiḥ pramāṇavyutpattiḥ । tadartham idam । tasmād ārabdhavyam । yat saprayojanam, tat prekṣāvatārabdhavyam । tad yathānuṣṭheyaviṣayajñānaparīkṣaṇam upadeṣṭari । saprayojanaṃ cedam । svabhāvaḥ ॥

<I,4>

[I,4,i]

yadi tarhy etad artham idam ārabhyate, nārabdhavyam, pramāṇasiddher nyāyamukhādinaiva svamatena tvayā prāg eva sādhitatvāt । yat sādhitam, na tat siddhaye prekṣāvatārambhaḥ kartavyaḥ । tad yathā sādhitasyaudanasya । sādhitā ca pramāṇasiddhiḥ । vyāpakaviruddhaḥ । asya nirāsāyāha — svamatād viprasṛtād iti । hetāv iyaṃ pañcamī । prasṛtaṃ prasaraṇaṃ vistara iti yāvat । punas tantreṇāvṛtter anekaśakter vāsyaivāyam aparo 'rthaḥ । sarve gatyarthā jñānārthā iti sṛtam avagamaḥ parijñānam । prakṛṣṭaṃ sṛtaṃ prasṛtam । vigataṃ prasṛtaṃ yataḥ, tad viprasṛtam । svamataṃ nyāyamukhādivigataprasṛtapramāṇavyutpattikam । tathā hi tatra pratyakṣaṃ kalpanāpoḍham ity asya pratyakṣalakṣaṇasya nāpavādaḥ kṛtaḥ । tataś ca dvicandrādijñānasyāpi pratyakṣatāprasaṅgaḥ । vigatavistaraṃ ca tatsaṅkṣiptam । tena ya evoddhaṭitajño diṅmātradarśanenāpy anuktam abhyūhitum arthaṃ samarthaḥ, tasyaiva vyutpattir bhavati, netarasya । tathā hi tatraiva mukhamātram idaṃ sadarthanīter ityādeḥ ślokasya pūrvārdhena sudhiya eva saṅkṣiptarucer upakārāyedaṃ kṛtam iti sūcitam, kusṛtīr ityādinā tūttarā<I,5>rdhena netareṣāmanenānugraho bhavatīti । tīrthyatarkabhramitā mandadhiyo vistareṇa pratipādyāḥ kṛsṛtīr apavidhya katham arthatattvabhājaḥ syuḥ, naivetyarthagateḥ । kathaṃśabdena hy atrāsambhavo dyotyate । ye tūddhaṭitadhīviṣayam āsaṃsārthaṃ vyācakṣate — kathaṃ nāmoddhaṭitadhīviṣāḥ kumārgamapāsya tīrthyatarkabhramitā bhūyāsūr arthatattvabhāja iti, teṣāṃ tad ayuktam । sthavīyāṃso hi doṣās tīrthyatakārṇāṃ te tathāvidhaiḥ sukham evopalakṣyante । ye 'nuktam api nāma duravabodham arthaṃ diṅmātradarśanena svayam utprekṣituṃ kṣamāḥ, te sūpalakṣyasthūlataradoṣais tīrthyatarkair unmārgeṇa tīyanta ity asambhāvanīyam etat । tad evam evaṃvidhaṃ yataḥ svamatam, na tena sarveṣāṃ pramāṇavyutpattiḥ kṛtā । tasmāt svamatāt saṅkṣiptād akṛtaprakṛṣṭapramāṇavyutpatter hetor mandadhiyām api vastararucīnām upakārāya sotsargaḥ sāpavādaḥ savistaraḥ prakṛṣṭaḥ pramāṇavyutpattaye pramāṇasamuccayaḥ kariṣyate ॥

[I,5,i]

tat kiṃ tatraiva nyāyamukhādāv ekaikasmin prakaraṇe 'paragranthaprakṣepeṇa samuccayaḥ kariṣyata iti praśnāvasara āha — ihaikata iti । ihāsminn ekasmin prakaraṇe sukhāvabodhārthaṃ samuccayaḥ kariṣyate । viprakīrṇo hi granthaḥ prakaraṇabhedena na sukham ālocayituṃ śakyate । ekata ityādyāditvāt tasiḥ । tathā hi śiṣṭaprayogaḥ carakasaṃhitāyām —
<I,6>
	yānīha karmāṇyuktāni visarpāṇāṃ praśāntaye /
	ekatas tāni sarvāṇi raktamokṣaṇam ekataḥ //
iti ॥

[I,6,i]

atreti śloke । bhagavata iti bhagaśabdo 'yam aiśvaryādiṣu vartate, yathoktam —
	aiśvaryasya samagrasya vairyasya yaśasaḥ śriyaḥ /
	jñānasyātha prayatnasya eṇṇāṃ bhaga iti śrutiḥ //
iti । etac ca samagraṃ tathāgata evāstīti sa eva bhagavān । māracatuṣṭayaṃ vā bhagnavān iti bhagavān nair uktena vidhinā । tasya stotrābhidhānam । stūyate 'neneti stotraṃ sadbhūtaguṇodbhāvanavacanama । abhidhānam iha vivakṣitasyārthasya śabdena pratyāyanam abhisaṃhitam । stotreṇābhidhānaṃ stutipadena guṇavattayā prakāśanam ity arthaḥ । kena guṇena tathāprakāśanam ity āha — pramāṇabhūtatveneti । sa punar guṇaḥ kena hetunety āha — hetuphalasampattyeti । hetuphalayoḥ sampattiḥ prakarṣaḥ, tena hetunā । yat pramāṇabhūtatvam asādhāraṇo guṇaḥ, tena karaṇena hetunā vā stotrābhidhānam, stutipadena bhagavato guṇavattayā śrotṛbhyaḥ pratipādanam iti yāvat ॥

<I,7>

[I,7,i]

tatpunaḥ kim artham ity āha — prakaraṇādau gauravotpādanārtham iti । kathaṃ punar bhagavataḥ stotrābhidhānena prakaraṇārambhe gauravaṃ bhavati । yataḥ satsvapyanyeṣu guṇeṣu prāmāṇyena guṇena stuvataitat sūcitam ācāryeṇa — yad etat pratyakṣādipramāṇalakṣaṇam, tad bhagavad upadeśād eva siddham, nedānīṃ savayam utprekṣya mayā vyavasthāpyata iti । ata evābhidharme 'py uktam ity uktam । yuktaṃ tāvat pratyakṣasya tataḥ siddhiḥ, tadupadeśadarśanāt । anupadiṣṭasya tv anumānasya katham । tasyāpi prayogadarśanād vihitam eva lakṣaṇaṃ gamyate । yathā yat kiñcit samudayadharmakam, tan nirodhadharmakam ity ādayo 'numānaprayogā bhagavato dṛśyante । katham evam ucyamāne 'numānasya lakṣaṇam uktaṃ bhavati । yasmād anumānasyāśrayo 'vinābhāvi liṅgam । anena ca prayogena sādhyena nirodhenotpādasya liṅgasya sphuṭam evāvinābhāva ukto bhagavatā । ato 'numānalakṣaṇam api bhagavad upadeśād eva siddham । tasmād bhagavad upadeśāsiddhapramāṇalakṣaṇānuvidhāyy etat prakaraṇam iti jātaniśccayānāṃ prasiddhaśāstṛkāṇāṃ tatra gauravaṃ jāyate । tataś cādyatya śravaṇādau pravartante ॥

[I,7,ii]

atha vātra prakaraṇādau bhagavataḥ stotrābhidhānaṃ stutye bhagavati gauravotpādanārtham । katham anena tatra gauravaṃ jāyate । yasmād anena ślokena sopapattaikaṃ pramāṇabhūtatvaṃ bhagavato guṇa udbhāvitaḥ, tasmāt prāg aprasiddhaśāstṛkā<I,8>ṇām api tatra gauravam utpadyate, kiṃ punar itareṣām । tad gauravāc copacitapuṇyasambhārāṇāṃ prakaraṇodgrahaṇāya pravṛttānāṃ na vinayakāḥ prabhavantīti tad gauravam api saprayojanam eva ॥

[I,8,i]

nanu ca kaiś cittathāvidhapuruṣapratiṣedhāya puruṣatvādisādhanānīkaṃ prayuktam । tat kathaṃ tatra stotrābhidhānena gauravaṃ bhavati । yatas tadagamakam, pratikṣepasāmānyasādhanayor asambhavāt । na hy atīndriyeṣv atad darśinaḥ pratikṣepaḥ sambhavati, satām apy eṣām ajñānāt, ata eva virodhāsiddher avirodhinā ca sahabhāvāvirodhāt । nāpītarapuruṣasāmānyasiddhiḥ, viśeṣāsambhavasya jñātum aśakyatvāt, īdṛśeṣu cānupalabdher hetutvāyogāt, puṃstvādisāmānye 'pi kasyacin medhāder guṇaviśeṣasya darśanāt tadvat sati saṃskāre 'nyasyāpi sambhāvāt sambhavadviśeṣe ca sāmānyāsiddheḥ । tasmāc cheṣavad anumānam etat, vyatirekasya sandehād asamartham adarśane 'pi vipakṣavṛtteḥ । na ca tasya tathāvidhajñālakṣaṇaṃ prāmāṇyam asambhāvanīyam, tatsādhanānuṣṭhānasambhavāt । yo yat sādhanam avipa<I,9>rītam anutiṣṭhati, tasya sambhavati tatprāptiḥ । tad yathārogyasādhanam aviparītam anutiṣṭhavāṃś ca bhagavān । svabhāvaḥ ॥

[I,9,i]

yat sādhanānuṣṭhānāc ca prāmāṇyaprāptiḥ sambhavati, tad darśayann āha — tatra heturāśayaprayogasampad iti । āśayaṃ darśayati — āśayo jagaddhitaiṣiteti । sā punaḥ sakalajagadātyantikaduḥkhaviyogaprārthanākārānalpakalpābhyāsena sātmībhūtā karuṇā । śloke jagaddhitaiṣiṇa ity anena darśitā । tadyogād dhi jagaddhitaiṣī bhavati । abhyāsāc ca sātmībhāvas tasyāḥ sambhavati । ye manoguṇāḥ, te 'tyantābhyāsasambhave sati sātmībhavanti, śrotriyajoṭiṅganair ghṛṇyavat । manoguṇaś ca karuṇā । svabhāvaḥ । sa tayā parārthaṃ prati preryamāṇaḥ svayam asākṣāt kṛtya na pāryate parebhyo deśayituṃ duḥkhapraśamopāya iti svaduḥkhoparamopāyabhāvanārthaṃ tāvat prayujyata iti darśayann āha — prayogo jagacchāsanād ityādi । yasya yatra dayā, sa tayā yathā tasyārtho bhavati tathā prayujyate, yathā mātuḥ putre dayā, sā ca yathā tasyārtho bhavati tathā prayujyate । āsīc ca bhagavato jagati dayā । svabhāvaḥ । jagacchāsanaṃ mukhyaṃ svadṛṣṭaduḥkhopaśamopāyopadeśaḥ । iha tu kāraṇe kāryopacāraṃ kṛtvopāyābhyāso jagacchāsanaśabdonoktaḥ, tasya sattvaśāsanayogyopāyatvena tad anyopāyābhyāsād viśiṣṭatvajñāpanārtham ॥

<I,10>

[I,10,i]

jagacchāsanād iti lakṣṇahetur ayam । tena yathā kāṭhinyāt pṛthivīty ukte kāṭhinyasvabhāvā pṛthivīti gamyate, tathā jagacchāsanāc chāstṛtvam ity ukte tatsvabhāvaṃ śāstṛtvam iti । sa pañcopādānaskandhalakṣaṇaṃ duḥkhaṃ kādācit katvena hetunānityam । ata eva cānityahetukam । śakyam etad dhetukṣayeṇa kṣapayityuṃ nidānakṣayeṇa vyādhir iva nānyatheti ca niścitya ko 'sya hetur iti vicārayan duḥkhahetum ātmasnehavatastṛṣṇām eva prādhānyenaivam avagatavān । yo 'nanyasatvaneyas yābhir atipūrvako hīnasthānaparigrahaḥ, sa ātmasnehavato duḥkhasukhatyāgāptivāñ chāpūrvakaḥ । tad yathā makṣikāṇām abhiratipūrvako 'śucisthānaparigrahaḥ । ananyasattvaneyas yābhir atipūrvakaś ca garbhādihīnasthānaparigrahaḥ prāṇina iti kāryam । saiva ca tṛṣṇā prādhānyena śāstre samudayasatyam ity ucyate । prādhānyaṃ punas tatsamutthāpitaprayatnavaśenotpattideśagamanād ānantaryāc ca । saty api hy ajñāne vāñ chāntareṇa pravṛtter asambhavāt karmaṇo 'pi tṛṣṇaiva pradhānam । tathā hi sad api karma yāvad avidyāpaṃ svavacchāditaṃ na bhavati tṛṣṇāsrehābhiṣyanditaṃ ca, na tāvat phalavad bhavati, yathārhatām । tatas tasyā api tṛṣṇāyā<I,11>s tadanyeṣāṃ ca doṣāṇām ātmadarśanam eva prabhavam evaṃ vyavasitavān । na hi nāhaṃ na mameti paśyataḥ parigraham antareṇa kvacit snehaḥ, na cāsnehavataḥ kvacid dveṣaḥ, ātmātmīyānuparodhiny uparodhapratighātini ca tadabhāvāt । tatsamānajātīyābhyāsajamātmadarśanam ātmīyasrehaṃ prasūte, sa dveṣādīn iti satkāyadarśanajāḥ sarve tṛṣṇādayo doṣāḥ । tad eva cājñānam ity ucyate, jñānavipakṣatvāt tasya । tad evātmadarśanam । yato doṣahetuḥ, tataḥ sambhavati tatkṣayāt tṛṣṇāyās tadanyeṣāṃ ca doṣāṇāṃ kṣaya iti matvātmadarśanapratipakṣaṃ parīkṣate sma, yad abhyāsena tat prahātavyam । parīkṣamāṇaś cātmadarśanasya tadviparītākāratvān nairātmyadarśanam eva pratipakṣam evam avajagāma । yo yad viparītasvabhāvaḥ, sa tasya pratipakṣaḥ । tad yathā vāyuviparītasvabhāvaṃ tailaṃ vāyoḥ । ātmadarśanaviparītasvabhāvaṃ ca nairātmyadarśanam iti svabhāvaḥ । ātmadarśanaviruddhaṃ ca nairātmyadarśanaṃ tatpūrvakasyātmasnehāder api doṣagaṇasya viruddham evety evam ajñāsīt । yo yan nidānaviruddhaḥ, sa tasya bādhakaḥ । yathā vātikasya vyādhes tan nidānaviruddhaṃ tailam । <I,12> ātmasnehādinidānātmadarśanaviruddhaṃ ca nairātmyadarśanam iti svabhāvaḥ । evaṃ jñātvā tasya tan nairātmyadarśanaṃ bahuśo bahudhā dīrghaṃ ca kālam abhyasyatas tatra tadvipakṣe ca sarvathā guṇadoṣāḥ prakāśatāmīyuḥ । yo yat prājño bahuśo bahudhā dīrghaṃ ca kālam, abhyasyati, tasya tatra tadvipakṣe ca guṇadoṣā prakāśībhavanti । tad yathā kasyacit prājñasya kvacic chilpaviśeṣe 'bhiyuktasyābhyasyataḥ । abhyastavāṃś ca bhagavān nairātmyadarśanaṃ bahuśo bahudhā dīrghaṃ ca kālam । svabhāvaḥ । ayam eva copāyābhyāso mārgasatyam ity ucyate । tasyaivaṃvidhād upāyābhyāsād ananyasādhāraṇād duḥkhahetor vāsanāpi nāvaśiṣyate । ayam eva ca bhagavataḥ khaḍgāder viśeṣaḥ । parārthapradhānavṛttinā cānenāvaśyam evaṃvidho 'bhyāsaḥ kartavyaḥ, aparijñātasakalavipakṣapratipakṣeṇa parebhyo vipakṣapratipakṣayor upadeṣṭum aśakyatvād ity ayam upāyābhyāsaḥ pūrvanirdiṣṭā ca karuṇā hetusampat ॥

[I,12,i]

asyāḥ phalaṃ svaparārthasampat । tatra svārthasampat — yathoktād upāyābhyāsāduḥkhahetoḥ pūrvasya svarasaṃ nirodhe nairātmyadarśanasātmye 'vasthitasyottaraduḥkhahetvanutpattilakṣṇo 'vasthāviśeṣaḥ, yasya nirodhasatyam ity ākhyā, sa eva viśeṣaṇatrayaviśiṣṭaṃ sugatatvam ity ucyate । tāṃ svārthasampadaṃ darśayann āha — svārthasampatsugatatvenetyādi । suśabdo 'yam iha praśastatvāder arthasya dyotako veditavyaḥ, yad āha — trividham artham upādāyetyādi ॥

<I,13>

[I,13,i]

praśastaṃ gataḥ prāptaḥ sugataḥ । praśastatvaṃ punar duḥkhasyāpunarāśrayatvena । loke hi sukhaṃ tadanubandhi ca praśastam ity ucyate । tac ca duḥkhānāśrayaṇaṃ nairātmyadṛṣṭeḥ svabhyastatvāt । atha vānantaroktenopāyena yuktidṛṣṭena gamanāt praśastaṃ gataḥ । loke hi yo yuktipūrvakaṃ pravartate, sa praśasyate ॥

[I,13,ii]

apunarāvṛttigamanāt sugataḥ । apunarāvṛttis tu janmadoṣānutpādaḥ । sa ca taddhetoḥ pūrvakasyābhāvāt । yasyātmadarśanasnehau na staḥ, na tasya janmarāgādidoṣotpādaḥ । tad yathākāśasya । na staś cātmadarśanasnehau sātmībhūtanairātmyadarśanasya । kāraṇābhāvaḥ ॥

[I,13,iii]

niḥśeṣaṃ gataḥ sugataḥ । nirgataṃ śeṣam asyeti vigrahaḥ । śeṣaṃ punaḥ kāyādivaiguṇyam । tat punar yathākramam acāpale 'py abhyāsād utplutyagamanādi, aham mānābhāve 'pi vṛṣalīvādādi nityāsamādhānenāsamāhitacittāvasthānaṃ ca । atha vā tathāvidhasya mārgābhyāsasyābhāvenātyartham aparijñānān mārgatadvipakṣayoḥ, adhigatasyāpi mārgasya vibhajyāprakāśanapāṭavaṃ śeṣam । tad api bhagavataḥ prahīṇam ity ato 'sau sugataḥ ॥

[I,13,iv]

arthatrayaṃ caitad ityādi । tatra bāhyavītarāgā ātmadarśanānupātena duḥkhāśrayeṇa mārgeṇa gamanāt, tadvaśenaiva punar duḥkham āśrayante, na ca yuktidṛṣṭena mārge<I,14>ṇa gatā ity atas te na praśastaṃ gatāḥ । tathā hi loke yo duḥkham āśrayatyayuktipūrvakaṃ ca pravartate, sa na praśasyate, api tu nindyata eva । śaikṣās tu yady api duḥkhānāśrayeṇa yuktiniścitena ca mārgeṇa praśastaṃ gatāḥ, tathāpi teṣāṃ doṣāṇāṃ janmanaś ca punarutpāda iti te 'pi na dvitīyenārthena sugatāḥ । aśaikṣāḥ punaḥ kāmam arthadvayena sugatāḥ, na tu niḥśeṣārthena, yathoktasya śeṣasyāprahāṇāt ॥

[I,14,i]

parārthasampattāraṇārthenety anena tāyaśabdasyārtham ācaṣṭe । tāryante saṃsārasāgaram anena sattvā iti tāraṇaḥ svadṛṣṭamārgopadeśaḥ । sa evārtho 'rthyate mokṣopāyakāmair iti kṛtvā so 'syāstīti tenārthena bhagavatas tāyitvam । ayam eva hi tāyateḥ paraḥ pālanārtho yad uta saṃsārasāgaratāraṇam ॥

[I,14,ii]

na ca tasya viparītopadeśatā sambhāvyate, tatkāraṇābhāvāt kṛpātmakatvān mārgasya ca supratividdhatvāt । rāgādayo hi doṣā mithyābhidhānagetavaḥ । prayojanaṃ vā kiñcit । tac ca nāsti । sātmībhūtakṛpaś ca parārtham eva duḥkhakṣayopāyaṃ sādhayitvā katham anyathā brūyāt । yasya yadānṛtavacanakāraṇāni na santi, na sa tadānṛtaṃ vakti । tad yathānyaḥ kaścit satyavacanakāle । na santi ca sugatāvasthākāle tasyānṛtakāraṇāni । kāraṇābhāvaḥ । yo yad arthakaraṇāya yat kṛpa<I,15>yā yam arthaṃ sādhayati, na sa tad arthaniṣpattāv aparityaktatadviṣayadayastaṃ tatra vañcayati । tad yathā sutapathyabhijanāya prasādhitāhārā mātā । sattvārthakaraṇāya sattvakṛpayā duḥkhakṣayopāyaṃ sādhitavān aparityaktatadviṣayadayaś ca bhagavān । vyāpakaviruddhaḥ । tasmāt pramāṇam । yo yad arthine tad arthopāyam aviparītaṃ kathayati, sa tasya tatra pramāṇam । tad yathārogyārthina ārogyopāyam aviparītaṃ kathayann āturasya tatra vaidyaḥ । duḥkhakṣayārthine duḥkhayopāyam aviparītaṃ kathitavāṃś ca bhagavān । svabhāvaḥ ॥

[I,15,i]

tad evaṃ pramāṇabhūtāyety etad eva stutipadam । anena hi bhagavato jñānalakṣaṇaṃ prāmāṇyam asādhāraṇo guṇa udbhāvitaḥ, yatas tadyogāt sa pramāṇaṃ bhavati । sa tu guṇo na vinā hetunā niṣpadyata iti darśayatā hetusampad uktā ॥

[I,15,ii]

sugataśabdena tu tasya jñānasya vipakṣaprahāṇaviśeṣaḥ phalasampatsaṅgṛhīta uktaḥ । tasminn asaty utplutyādigamanavad vākyaprāpaṇīyasyārthasyāyuktasyāpi sūcakaṃ kāyaceṣṭitaṃ kuryāt, vṛṣalīvādādivadanyad apy asatyaṃ kadācid abhidadhyāt, nityāsamāhitatvena vāvyākyākṛtāvasthāyāṃ na sakalasattvārthakaraṇasamarthaḥ syāt, <I,16> na vā pāṭav avipakṣasya savāsanasyāprahāṇād asyādhigatamārgaprakāśanapāṭavaṃ syāt । tasmiṃs tu saty ete doṣā na bhavatīti darśayituṃ prahāṇaviśeṣa uktaḥ ॥

[I,16,i]

tāyin ity anena tu tasyaiva jñānasya kāryaviśeṣo yathādṛṣṭamārgopadeśo darśitaḥ । sa yadi na syāt, tatprāmāṇyam eva na syāt । tathāvidhaṃ hi yadi tasya kāryaṃ bhavati, evaṃ tadyogād bhagavān anadhigatasyārthasya prakāśako bhavati tatra vāvisaṃvādakaḥ, nānyathety ataḥ kāryaviśeṣo darśitaḥ ॥

[I,16,ii]

karuṇā tu bodhisattvāvasthāyām eva yā svarasavāhinyabhūt, sā sugatāvasthāyām anuktasiddhaiveti noktā । tayā hi vinā naiva hitam upadeṣṭum utsaheteti sāpi tasya parāthaṃ prati sahāyabhūtā veditavyā । tad evaṃ bhagavato jñānalakṣaṇaṃ prāmāṇyaṃ tāvad ānulomyena vyākhyā, yatra kṛpādibhiḥ śāstṛtvādīnāṃ sambhavo 'numīyate ॥

[I,16,iii]

idānīṃ prātilomyena vyākhyā kriyate । atha vā tāyo 'viparītasatyopadeśaḥ । taṃ duḥkhopaśamahetuṃ sattvebhyo deśitavān bhagavān iti sa teṣāṃ tadarthināṃ tatra pramāṇam । yo yad duḥkhapraśamārthine yasmai tad duḥkhasvabhāvaṃ ca tad duḥkhahetuṃ ca tad duḥkhapraśamaṃ ca tad duḥkhapraśamopāyaṃ ca yathābhūtaṃ kathayati, sa tasya tatra <I,17> pramāṇam । tad yathā vyādhiduḥkhapraśamārthina āturāya vyādhiduḥkhasvabhāvabhāvādikaṃ yathābhūtaṃ kathayan tasya tatra vaidyaḥ । saṃsāraduḥkhapraśamārthine puruṣāya saṃsāraduḥkhasvabhāvādikaṃ yathābhūtaṃ kathitavāṃś ca bhagavān । svabhāvaḥ ॥

[I,17,i]

tāni ca satyāni leśato darśitāni । yathā duḥkhaṃ pañcopādānaskandhalakṣaṇam । tasya ca samudayas tṛṣṇā । tataś ca duḥkhasyotpattir yathā prayujyate । nirodho mārgasātmye 'vasthitasya pūrvaduḥkhahetunirodhe saty uttaraduḥkhahetvanutpattilakṣaṇo 'vasthāviśeṣaḥ । mārgo nairātmyadarśanābhyāsaḥ । yathā ca tato nirodhaprāptir bhavati । tat sarvaṃ prāg eva saṅkṣepato darśitam । tasmād bhavati saty acatuṣṭayadarśanān muktiḥ । tataś ca tadupadeśaḥ saṃsārārṇavottaraṇasādhanatvāt tāyaḥ । etāvad eva ca parahitaiṣiṇā kāryam, yad uta heyopādeyatattvasya sābhyupāyasya upadeśaḥ । sa ca bhagavatā kṛtaḥ । tad etasmāt kāryāt praśastatvādiviśeṣaṇatrayaviśiṣṭaṃ jñānam anumīyate, gamer bodhārthastehāśrayaṇāt । pūrvaṃ prāptyarthaṃ gamim āśritya prahāṇasampatphalam uktam ॥

[I,17,ii]

samprati jñānasampat — praśastam avabuddhavān yāvad aśeṣam avabuddhavān ity evaṃ sugatatvaṃ veditavyam । tatra praśastatvaṃ tasya jñānasya tattvaviṣayatvāt । tat punaḥ pramāṇasaṃ<I,18>vādāt taddeśitasya mārgasyānumīyate । apunarāvṛttitvaṃ sthiratvāt । tatpunarmārgasya tanniścitasya pramāṇāntareṇābādhanād avasīyate । avicalasya vā pūrvāparavacanāvyāhatyā sarvatra pravacane caturāryasatyadeśanāyā ekavākyatvāt । śeṣaṃ punar atra catuṣv āryasatyeṣv adhigateṣv api jñānasya pratipādanākauśalam । tadabhāvaśeṣajñānam anumīyate citrair upāyaiḥ satyaprakāśanāt । śrāvakāṇāṃ tu kiñcinmātraṃ kauśalam । tad api tadanuśikṣaṇataḥ । atas tattvasthiratvāśeṣatvaviśeṣaṇaviśiṣṭena jñānena bāhyavītarāgebhyo 'dhikaḥ । tathā hi na teṣāṃ pramāṇasaṃvādiheyopādeyaviṣayaṃ jñānam । sthiratvaviśeṣaṇaviśiṣṭena śaikṣebhyaḥ, teṣām anabhisaṃskārikāyāḥ satkāyadṛṣṭer aprahāṇāt, tatsamudācārakaleṣu parāvṛttisambhavāt । aśeṣatvaviśeṣaṇaviśiṣṭenāśaikṣebhyaḥ, teṣāṃ yathoktaśeṣasambhavāt । evaṃvidhajñānāt parārtho mārgābhyāso 'vasīyate, yatas tadadhigamyāpi noparatavyāpāro 'bhūt pratyekajinavat, kiṃ tarhi yathādhigatamārgākhyānatatpara evāsīt । yo yasminn adhigate 'py aviratavyāpāraḥ, na sa tanmātraphalābhikāṅkṣī । tad yathānnadhigame 'py aviratavyāpāro bhojanāya pravṛttaḥ । adhigate 'pi ca yathokte <I,19> jñānaviśeṣe na tāvatoparatavyāpāro 'bhūd bhagavān । vyāpakaviruddhaḥ । sa eva ca mārgābhyāsaḥ śastṛtvam upacārād ity uktam etat ॥

[I,19,i]

tato 'pi dayānumīyate । dayāvān iha parārthe prayujyate, nānyaḥ ॥

[I,19,ii]

tad evaṃvidhayā hetuphalasampadā bhagavān pramāṇam । tathā hi kṛpayārtham evopadeṣṭum icchati । niṣkaruṇas tu jānann apy anyathā kathayed iti kṛpāyāḥ prāmāṇye 'ṅgabhāvaḥ । dayāvān apy ajñānāt tattvam evopadeṣṭum akṣamaḥ । jñānāt tu bhūtam evopadiśatīti jñānāsyāpi prāmāṇyaṃ prati sādhanabhāvaḥ । tac ca prāmāṇyaṃ sahetukam । tato 'sya yuktaḥ sadbhāva iti hetusampad uktā । na tu tathāvidhāyāṃ phalasampadi satyāṃ tasyāḥ kaścanopayogaḥ । yadi hi vināpi hetusampadā sā phalasampat syāt, syād eva prāmāṇyam । sā tu tayā vinā na sambhavatīti tadanupādānam ॥

[I,19,iii]

tāyitvenāvaśyam abhiyogavān parāvabodhanaṃ pratīty etad darśitam । tad evaṃ yataḥ śreyobhūtam ācaṣṭe tadākhyāne ca yatnavān, tasmāt pramāṇam । yo yasmai śreyobhūtam ācaṣṭe tadākhyāne ca yatnavān, sa tena viduṣā pramāṇayitavyaḥ । tadyathā yathoktair guṇaiḥ śiṣyāyopadiśann upādhyāyo viduṣā śiṣyeṇa । sattvebhyaḥ śreyobhūtam ācaṣṭe ca tadākhyāne ca yatnavān bhagavān । svabhāvaḥ ॥

<I,20>

[I,20,i]

atra vyākhyāprakāre codyate — yadi jñānam api prāmāṇyasya sādhanatvena vyavasthāpyate, tat kiṃ punas tatprāmāṇyaṃ yasya karuṇādayaḥ sādhanam iti vaktavyam । ucyate — sāmarthyaviśeṣaḥ, yasmin sati bhagavān anadhigatam arthaṃ gamayati tatra cāvisaṃvādako bhavati । sa tu sāmarthyaviśeṣaḥ karuṇādibhir yuktasya bhavati, netarasyeti tasya sādhanatvena vyavasthāpyate ॥

[I,20,ii]

svaprakaraṇebhya ity etat svamatād ity asya vyākhyānam । mukhaśabdenaiva ca pūrvoktaḥ prasṛtaśabdasyārthaḥ sphuṭam eva gamyata iti na vibhaktaḥ । mukhaṃ hi dvāraṃ diṅmātradarśanaṃ saṅkṣiptam । na ca tena vistarapratipādyānāṃ vyutpattir bhavatīti prasiddham evaitat । bahuṣv api matasāmānyāc chloke svamatād ity ekavacanam । vṛttau tu bhedavivakṣāyāṃ svaprakaraṇebhya iti bahuvacanam ॥

[I,20,iii]

samāhṛtyetyādi । pūrvakṛtaṃ ca kiñcid anyac cāpūrvaṃ buddhisthaṃ samyagānīya pramāṇānāṃ samuccayaḥ samuccitiḥ kariṣyate । atra ca sarva eva pramāṇaprameyatadābhāsādinimittāḥ sandarbhāḥ pramāṇaprasaṅgenāyātatvāt pramāṇaśabdenoktāḥ ॥

[I,20,iv]

parapramāṇapratiṣedhadhāyetyādinā pramāṇasiddhiśabdasyārtham ācaṣṭe । svapramāṇaṃ cātra mukhyam । parapramāṇaṃ tu pareṣāṃ tatra pramāṇābhiniveśa iti pramāṇam i<I,21>ty uktam । tayor yathāsvaṃ svarūpaparijñānaṃ pramāṇasiddhiḥ । tatra parapramāṇasyāpramāṇasya sato 'py āropitapramāṇasvabhāvasya naitat pramāṇasvabhāvam iti yad utpādanaṃ sa pratiṣedhaḥ । saiva ca tasya siddhiḥ । svapramāṇam eva guṇaḥ, arthakāmair guṇyata iti kṛtvārthāv āhakatāc ca । tasyodbhāvanam aviparītalakṣaṇābhidhānena vyutpādanam । saiva ca tasya siddhiḥ ॥

[I,21,i]

yasmād ityādinā puruṣārthopayogitvaṃ pramāṇasya darśayati । anyathā tadanupayogino vyutpādanaṃ vyarthopayogitvaṃ pramāṇasya darśayati । anyathā tadanupayogino vyutpādanaṃ vyartham ity akartavyam eva syāt । prameye punar atra heyam upādeyaṃ ca । tatpratipattir yataḥ pramāṇāyattā, tasmāt pramāṇasiddhaye yatnaḥ saphala ity abhiprāyaḥ ॥

[I,21,ii]

atra kecid āhuḥ — svata eva siddhāni pramāṇānīti । tanmatānusāriṇaś cāpare ślokaṃ paṭhanti —
	prasiddhāni pramāṇāni vyavahāraś ca tatkṛtaḥ /
	pramāṇalakṣaṇasyoktau jñāyate na prayojanam //
iti ॥

[I,21,iii]

atas tan nirākaraṇāyāha — bahavaś cātra vipratipannā iti । bahavaś cātra vipratipannā iti । caśabdena yasmād ity etad anukṛṣyate । viruddhaṃ pratipannā vipratipannāḥ, parasparaviruddhalakṣaṇapraṇayanāt yadi hi pramāṇam idam iti niścayalakṣaṇā siddhiḥ svataḥ pramāṇasya <I,22> syāt, na parasparavirodhalakṣaṇaṃ lakṣaṇakāraiḥ praṇīyet । pramāṇotpattāv eva pramāṇasvarūpasiddher ekākāram eva lakṣaṇapraṇayanaṃ syāt । vyavahartāro 'pi vipratipannā viparītaṃ pratipannāḥ, apramāṇaṃ pramāṇatvenādhyavasitā ity arthaḥ । tathā hi pramāṇābhāsena pravṛttāḥ kecid vipralabhyamānā dṛśyante । yadi tu siddhāny eva sarveṣāṃ pramāṇāni syuḥ, na kaścid vipralabhyet ॥

[I,22,i]

tasmāt svataḥ pramāṇasya savasaṃvedanāt svarūpasiddhimātraṃ bhavati । īpsitārthakriyāsamarthavastuprāpaṇasāmarthyalakṣaṇaṃ tu yat prāmāṇya, tasya sata eva pramāṇaparidṛṣṭavastusādhyārthakriyāviṣayapramāṇāntaravṛttyā viścayo bhavati prathamam । utttarakālaṃ tu punaḥ punaruttarapramāṇavṛttyā kāsāñcij jñānavyaktīnāṃ prāmāṇyaṃ niścinvann abhyāsād anyāsām uttarapramāṇavṛttim antareṇāpi prājñas tathāvidhānāṃ svarūpasaṃvedanamātrād eva prāmāṇyaṃ vyavasyati, abhyāsena maṇyādīnām ivākṛtrimādibhedam । tad evaṃ yato bahavaḥ pramāṇaṃ prati vipratipannāḥ, tasmāt teṣāṃ vipratipattinirāsāya śāstram iti ॥

{1.2–1.3a}

[I,22,ii]

tatra phalatvarūpaviṣayasaṅkhyāvipratipattipattayaś catastraḥ ॥

[I,22,iii]

tāsāṃ saṅkhyāvipratipattiṃ nirākartum āha — pratyakṣam anumānaṃ cetyādi ॥

[I,22,iv]

pramāṇavyutpādane kartavye saṅkhyādivyutpattir apārthiketi cet, na, pramāṇā<I,23>pramāṇavipratipattinivartanaparatvāt prakaraṇasya । tatra yadi saṅkhyādipratipattir na nirākriyeta kevalaṃ pratyakṣānumānayoḥ svarūpaṃ vyutpādyeta, tadā pareṣām evaṃ syāt । nūnam etad viṣayaivāsmākaṃ vipratipattiḥ, yāni tu pramāṇāntarāṇyasmābhir abhyupetāni na tadviṣayeti । nanu ca teṣām api doṣodbhāvanāt kuta iyam āśaṅkhā । evaṃ tarhi yathā pratyakṣānumānayor asmad abhimatāt svarūpād anyad eva svarūpam, tathā teṣām apy astitve tad anena na vyutpāditam ity āśaṅkā syāt । ataḥ saṅkhyāvyutpattiḥ ॥

[I,23,i]

gocarāvyutpādane tvaviṣaye gṛhītaṃ pramāṇaṃ yadā bhavati, tadā tatra tasya visaṃvāde tadvatsvaviṣaye 'py aprāmāṇyam avagacchet pratipatteti viṣayavyutpattiḥ ॥

[I,23,ii]

pramāṇāt phalam avyatiriktam iti yadā na vyutpādyate, tadā pramāṇasya pramāṇasvarūpataiva hīyate । tathā hi phalasya tāvad arthādhigamarūpatvaṃ niyamato 'bhyupeyam, anyathā phalatvāyogāt । tasmād adhigamarūpatvaṃ phalam । tato jñānarūpād vyatiriktaṃ yadā pramāṇam, tadā tenājñānarūpeṇa bhāvyam । ajñānarūpasya ca pramāṇasvarūpatā na syād rūpādivad iti phalavyupattiḥ । tannāpārthikā saṅkhyādivyutpattiḥ ॥

[I,23,iii]

dvayor api svaviṣaye tulyabalatākhyāpanāya samuccayavacanaś caśabdaḥ ॥

[I,23,iv]

kaḥ punar asya vākyasyārthaḥ । kiṃ pratyakṣa anumānaṃ ca pramāṇe ity anena pratyakṣānumānayoḥ pramāṇayor dvitvaṃ pratipādyate pratyakṣam anumānaṃ caite pramāṇe eva na <I,24> pramāṇaṃ pramāṇāni ceti । atha prāmāṇyaṃ pratyakṣānumānayoḥ pratipādyate pratyakṣam anumānaṃ ca pramāṇe eva nāpramāṇe iti । kiṃ cātaḥ । yadi pūrvaḥ kalpaḥ, niṣphalaṃ vacanam, tayor dvitvasya siddhatvāt । na hi pratyakṣānumānayor dvitvaṃ prati kasyacid vipratipattiḥ । atha dvitīyaḥ, saṅkhyāvadhāraṇaṃ na kṛtaṃ syāt । tataś ca dvividham eva pramāṇam iti yat pratipipādayiṣitam, tad eva na pratipāditaṃ syāt, siddhasādhyatā ca tayoḥ prāmāṇyasya siddhatvāt । atha vā cārvākaṃ praty etad ucyate, tathāpi pratyakṣāpekṣayā siddhasādhanam eva ॥

[I,24,i]

naiṣa doṣaḥ । atra hi dve vākye । pratyakṣam anumānaṃ cety ekavākyam, pramāṇe iti dvitīyam । evaṃ ca vyākhyeyam । pramāṇe eva, na pramāṇāni pramāṇaṃ cety arthaḥ । ata eva vṛttāv avadhārayati dve eveti । vyavacchedaphalatvād vākyasya vināpyevaśabdaṃ tadartha upalabhyate । evam anena vākyena dve eva pramāṇe iti pratipāditam । ke punas te dve iti saṃśayitasya paśnāvasara idam ucyate — pratyakṣam anumānaṃ ceti, pratyakṣānumāne eva te dve pramāṇe, na tv anye eva kecid dve iti । atra vyākhyāne na bhavati yathoktadoṣāvakāśaḥ ॥

[I,24,ii]

atha kathaṃ gamyate naikatvaṃ pramāṇasya bahautvaṃ veti । ekatvaṃ tāvan na bhavati, anumānasyāpi prāmāṇyāt । anyathedaṃ pramāṇam idam apramāṇam ity eṣā vyavasthā na <I,25> syāt । tathā hi kāsāñcij jñānavyaktīnāṃ pravṛttau saṃvādaṃ visaṃvādaṃ copalabhya tajjātīyatayāny asyāpi jñānasya saṃvād etarau niścinvan pramāṇetaravyavasthāṃ kuryāt, nānyathā । tac ca yathādṛṣṭasādharmyāt tathā paricchidyamānaṃ nānumeyatām atipatati । kiṃ cānumānasyāprāmāṇye śāstrapraṇayanaṃ na syāt । parāvabodhārthaṃ hi śāstraṃ kriyate । sa ca parāvabodho nānumānād anyato 'vasīyate, pratyakṣasya śarīramātraviṣayatvāt ॥

[I,25,i]

na ca śarīram eva buddhiḥ, tatsiddhāv api buddhivikalpe saṃśayāt । nainam anyasambandhinaṃ puruṣamātrapratyakṣam anveti ॥

[I,25,ii]

pratiṣedhaṃ cāyam anumānāpavādīkurvan paralokārdena pratyakṣeṇa kartum arhati, tasya bhāvaviṣayatvāt । tat punar arthasāmarthyāpekṣaṇāt, anapekṣāyāṃ vyavadhānādibhāve 'pi bhāvaprasaṅga iti । ato 'numānasyāpi prāmāṇyam abhyupeyam । tasmān naikatvaṃ pramāṇasya ॥

[I,25,iii]

bahutvaṃ tu syāt । tac ca viṣayabahutvād vā, ekasminn api viṣaye 'nekapramāṇāvatārād vā । na tāvad viṣayabahutvāt । atra kāraṇam āha — yasmāl lakṣaṇadvayaṃ prameyam iti । etad vivṛṇoti — na hītyādinā । tatra svalakṣaṇam, yad arthakriyāsamastham । tad eva vastu । sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ punas tadviparītam ॥

<I,26>

[I,26,i]

yady evam, taimirikādyupalabdhāḥ keśādayo na svalakṣaṇam, keśādisādhyārthakriyāyām arthatvāt, nāpi sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ, spaṣṭapratibhāsitvād iti teṣāṃ prameyāntaratvaṃ syāt ॥

[I,26,ii]

naiṣa doṣaḥ । yatra hi vyavahartṛṇāṃ viṣayatvādhyavasāyaḥ, tatreyaṃ cintā । na ca taimirikādibhirupalabdhāḥ keśādayas taiḥ svajñānapratibhāsino viṣayatvenādhimucyante । abhāvas tarhi sāmānyaṃ mā bhūt । na hi tadviṣayatvenādhyavasīyata iti cet, na, jñeyatvenādhyavasāyād asti tatrāpi viṣayādhimokṣaḥ । yadā punar abhāvav ataimirikādidṛṣṭānāṃ keśādīnāṃ jñānāntareṇa jñeyatvena grahaṇam, tad eṣṭam eva sāmānyarūpatvam । kevalaṃ yasmiñ jñāne te pratibhāsante, tasya jñeyatvena te na gṛhyanta iti teṣām asāmānyarūpatvam ucyate ॥

[I,26,iii]

yadi te na vastu kathaṃ sphuṭaṃ pratibhāsante । jñānarūpatayā svalakṣaṇatvāt । yadā tu praty avamarśajñānena viṣayīkriyante keśādivat keśādīdam iti, tadā sāmānyākāreṇāsphuṭena praty avabhāsamānānāṃ sāmānyarūpatvaṃ vyavasthāpyate ॥

[I,26,iv]

yadi teṣāṃ jñānarūpatvād vastutvam, sāmānye 'pi prasaṅgaḥ । tathā tad api svalakṣaṇam iṣṭam ity adoṣaḥ ॥

<I,27>

[I,27,i]

sāmānyarūpatvaṃ tu tasya viṣayāpekṣayā vyavasthāpyate । arthāntaravyāvṛttapadārthasamāśrayeṇotpadyamānā praty avamarśabuddhir abhinnākārā teṣv abhinnam evākārāṃ darśayatīti sa buddhigata ākāro 'rthānāṃ vyavasthāpyate । avastutvam apy asyāt eva, bāhyarūpeṇādhyavasitasyātadrūpatvāt ॥

[I,27,ii]

yadi tarhi sāmānyaṃ sarvasāmarthyarahitaṃ tanmānārham eva na bhavatīty aprameyam eva, tat katham ācāryeṇa viṣayadvaividhyam uktam, tat tasyaiva svarūpapararūpābhyām adhigateḥ । tasyaiva hi vastunaḥ pratyakṣeṇa svarūpādhigamāt, ekaṃ prameyaṃ svalakṣaṇam । tasyaivānumānena sāmānyākārānuraktagrāhyāṃśātmakena pararūpeṇādhyavasitatadbhāvatayādhigamāt, dvitīyaṃ sāmānyalakṣaṇam ॥

[I,27,iii]

kathaṃ punar etad gamyate — pararūpeṇa svalakṣaṇam evādhigamyata iti । yasmād anumānavikalpasya bāhyatayā praty avabhāsamānam aṃśamasvalakṣaṇam api svalakṣaṇatvenādhyavasāya puruṣo 'rthakriyārthī svalakṣaṇa eva pravartate । anyathā yadi <I,28> sāmānyam anumānena paricchinnaṃ syāt, arthakriyārthī tatraiva pravartate । na hi ghaṭaṃ paricchidya ghaṭaṃ paricchidya ghaṭāv asāye 'vasthitas tadarthakriyārthī ghaṭe pravartate naiva vā pravartate, sāmānyasya kvacid anupayogāt । pravartate ca svalakṣaṇe tatsādhyārthakriyāprāptaye 'numānāt । tenādhyavasitatadbhāva iti gamyate । pratyakṣeṇāpi pararūpeṇaivādhigatiḥ । ayaṃ tu viśeṣo 'numānena sādhāraṇabhūtena pararūpeṇārthasya grahaṇam, pratyakṣeṇa tv asādhāraṇabhūteneti । tasmāt sādhāraṇāsādhāraṇabhūtābhyāṃ pararūpābhyām adhigateḥ prameyadvayam uktam । na hi vijñānavad arthasya svataḥ saṃvittiḥ । yad eva tv arthākārasya jñānasya svasaṃvedanaṃ saivārthasaṃvittiḥ । arthapratibhāse hi jñāne 'nubhūte 'dhigata iti manyate । ata eva bāhye 'py arthe prameye svasaṃvittiṃ phalatvena vyavasthāpayiṣyatīty apare ॥

[I,28,i]

gatam etat । idaṃ tu vaktavyam — kathaṃ prameyadvitvāt pramāṇadvitvam ity āha — svalakṣaṇaviṣayaṃ cetyādi । caśabdo 'vadhāraṇārthaḥ, svalakṣaṇaviṣayaṃ pratyakṣam eva, sāmānyalakṣaṇaviṣayam anumānam eva, na pramāṇāntaram । ayaṃ cārtho vistareṇa svalakṣaṇam anirdeśyaṃ grāhyabhedād ityādinā pratipādayiṣyamāṇa iti darśayann āha — pratipādayiṣyāma iti ॥

[I,28,ii]

atha vānena prameyadvayadarśanenaikatryādipramāṇanirāsaḥ kṛṭaḥ । svalakṣaṇād anyad api prameyaṃ darśayatāpratyakṣam api pramāṇam astīty ekapramāṇanirāsaḥ kṛtaḥ । tṛtīyasya prameyasyābhāvaṃ darśayatā tryādipramāṇanirāsaḥ ॥

<I,29>

[I,29,i]

yat tarhītyādi । yadi prameyaniyamaḥ svasāmānyalaṣaṇābhyām anyat prameyaṃ nāsty evety abhyupeyate, evaṃ tarhi nīlādīnāṃ kṛtakatvādiliṅgadarśanād anityaṃ rūpam ity evamādi grahaṇaṃ na syāt । tathā hi nīlādi svalakṣaṇam, anityatā sāmānyam । anayoḥ saṅkareṅa grahaṅān na tatsāmānyam eva svalakṣaṇam eva vā । ato viśeṣasāmānyarūpaṃ prameyāntaram evaitan na pramīyate । pramīyate ca । tasmād anityaṃ rūpam ityādiviśeṣasāmānyaviṣayaṃ grahaṇaṃ pramāṇāntaram । tathā hi na tatpratyakṣam, sāmānyasyāpi grahaṇāt, nāpy anunmānam, viśeṣasyāpi grahaṇāt, vināpi liṅgena tathāpratīteḥ sambhavāc ca । tat katham iti tadgrahaṇaṃ kathaṃ na pramāṇāntaram ity arthaḥ ॥

[I,29,ii]

asakṛd vety anenāpi — viśeṣadṛṣṭākhyaṃ yad anumānam, tat pramāṇāntaram iti darśayati । tad yathā pratyakṣeṇaikadā paricchinne vahnau dhūme ca punaḥ paryāyeṇa <I,30> tenaiva dhūmena yadā sa evāyaṃ vahnir iti paricchinatti, tadā tadviśeṣadṛṣṭākhyam agrigrahaṇaṃ pramāṇāntaraṃ sāmānyato dṛṣṭād anumānāt । tad eva cātrānumānam iṣṭaṃ tallakṣaṇaṃ ca viśeṣadṛṣṭe na sambhavati, viśeṣeṇa liṅgasya sambandhāyogāt । tad evaṃ dvābhyāmākārābhyāṃ pramāṇabahutvaṃ sambhavet, prameyabahutvād vā, ekasminn eva vā viṣaye 'nekapramāṇāvatārāt । tadubhayathāpi pareṇa darśitaṃ yat tarhītyādinā granthena ॥

[I,30,i]

ekānekapramāṇanirāso vā prameyadvayadarśanādyaḥ prāg uktaḥ, sa nāstīti pratipāditam । na tāvad ekasaṅkhyānirāso viṣayāniyamāt । yadā na sāmānyaviṣayam evānumānam, kiṃ tarhi pramāṇāntaraviṣaye 'pi pravartate, tadā pratyakṣasyāpi sāmānye pravṛttyavirodhān nāpratyakṣaviṣaye pratyāyanāyānumānaṃ kalpayitavyam ity ekam eva pramāṇaṃ syāt । nāpi tryādisaṅkhyānirāsaḥ, prameyāntarasambhavāt । prameyadvitvena hi pramāṇadvitvam uktam । yadā tu prameyāntaraṃ sambhavati, tadā tasya pratyāyakaṃ pramāṇāntaraṃ syād iti na dve eva pramāṇe ॥

[I,30,ii]

asty etad grahaṇam iti । nedam apahnūyate, kiṃ tu tasya saṃdhāne na pramāṇāntaram ॥

<I,31>

[I,31,i]

ayaṃ tāvat pūrvasya parihāraḥ । tasyety anityāder varṇādeś ca । sandhānaṃ yojanam । yat tat sandhāne pravartate tan nimittaṃ jñānam, na tatpramāṇāntaram । kathaṃ punas tatsandhānam ity āha — svasāmānyalakṣaṇābhyām ityādi । prāk tāv adrūpādikam avyapadeś yena svalakṣaṇena gṛhṇāti pratyakṣeṇa । paścāt tad eva varṇatvādinā sāmānyalakṣaṇena savikalpena manovijñānena । tataḥ sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ cānityatvādi yat kiñcit kṛtakam, tat sarvam anityam ity evaṃ gṛhītvā tataḥ kṛtakaṃ cedaṃ varṇādi tasmād anityam ity evaṃ manasā sandhatte yojayati varṇatvādisāmānyaṃ sāmānyenaivānityatvena । tasmān na pramāṇāntaram, api tv anumānam eva । kiṃ kāraṇaṃ viśeṣeṇa na yojayati । tasya tenāgrahaṇāt ॥

[I,31,ii]

syād etat — yadi varṇasāmānyenānityatvādīn yojayati, evaṃ sati sāmānyasyaivāvastuno 'nityatvādayo dharmoḥ prāpnuvanti, na svalakṣaṇasya, tatrāvṛttteḥ । ye hi vastuni na vartate, na te vastudharmāḥ । tad yathānutpādādaya, tatrāvṛtteḥ । ye hi vastuni na vartate, na te vastudharmāḥ । tad yathānutpādādaya iti । nāyaṃ doṣaḥ, vastuna evānityādibhirākārais tathāsādhanāt । yady api vikalpapratibhāsinaḥ sāmānyasyaiva tathā vastvadhyavasāyena grahaḥ, tathāpi tasya vastunaḥ kṣaṇikatvādayo vidyamānā evākārā anumānavikalpe pratibhāsante । sa hi <I,32> yathāsthitavastupratyāyakaliṅgāśrayeṇotpanno vastunaḥ sata evākārānadhyavasyati । ato varṇasāmānye 'nityatādisādhane 'pi tatra tadākārasiddhyā vastuna eva sa ākāraḥ sidhyatīty avagantavyam, sāmagrīviśeṣajanmano mukhapratibimbajñānasya viṣaye lakṣmyādisiddhyā mukhalakṣmyādisiddhivad arthaḥ ॥

[I,32,i]

sa tv ayam anumānavikalpo yady api sambhavina evākārān arthasyādhyavasyati, tathāpi svalakṣaṇasya rūpam agṛhītam eva tena । anyathā darśanavat spaṣṭaṃ pratibhāseta tatra vastuno rūpam । na ca parasparavilakṣaṇāv ākārāv ekasya vastunaḥ staḥ, yenāspaṣṭaṃ gṛhyeta netareṇa । tasmād viśeṣasyāgrahaṇān na sa tam anityatayā yojayati, api tu varṇasāmānyam eva svaviṣayam । ato na pramāṇāntaram । evam idam anumānena varṇāder anityatāgrahaṇam adhikṛtyoktam ॥

[I,32,ii]

yadā tv antyakṣaṇadarśino naṣṭo 'yam iti, tadā pratyakṣeṇānityatāsvabhāvapratipatter gṛhītam eva niścinotīty etat pramāṇam eva na bhavati । tadā <I,33> cāsakṛd vāty anenāsya sādhāraṇaḥ parihāro vakṣyamāṇo 'niṣṭhāsakter ity ayaṃ veditavyaḥ ॥

[I,33,i]

kathaṃ punaḥ pratyakṣeṇa gṛhītam eva pūrvaṃ paścān niścayajñānaṃ gṛhṇāti । yasmān nānityatā nāmānyā kācic calād vastunaḥ । tenāntyaṃ kṣaṇaṃ sadṛśāparāpratisandhāyinaṃ pratyakṣeṇa paricchin dan naśvaratām api tasya svabhāvaṃ pratyetīti saiva cānityateti pratyakṣasiddhā sā । atha punar anityatā bhāvād arthān taram, tadā na svabhāvo naśvaraḥ syāt । na hy anyasya bhāve 'nyo naṣṭo nāma । tato nāśitāsvabhāvāpattir bhāvasyeti cet, ayuktam etat । na hi svayam acalasvabhāvasyānyena svabhāvāntaram ādhātuṃ śakyate । prakṛtyā ca calātmake viphalānyānityatā । tattvānyatvābhyām avācyatve 'py avastutvān na sa svabhāvo bhāvika iti saṃvṛtyānityaḥ syāt, na paramārthataḥ । tasmād bhāva evānityatā । tataś ca dharmiṇi rūpādau gṛhīte 'nityatāpi gṛhītaiveti gṛhītagrahaṇān nedaṃ pramāṇam ॥

[I,33,ii]

yadi nānyo 'nityatādiko dharmiṇo dharmaḥ, nanv evam anumānam api na pramāṇaṃ syāt । tathā hi nāsiddhe dharmiṇi dharmaḥ śakyaḥ sādhayitum, tatsiddhau ca tadātmatayā dharmasyāpi siddhatvād iti cet, na, aniścayāt । sadṛśāparotpattyā hi sa evāyam iti bhrāntasya na tatra pratyakṣaṃ niścayaṃ janayati । aniśca<I,34>yāc cāvyavahārayogyo 'gṛhītakalpa eva sa iti na tatra tasya prāmāṇyam, api tu yatrākāre niścayamādadhatsmṛtidvāreṇa pravartayati tatraiva । kutaḥ । pravṛttiphalatvāt pramāṇasya । tasmād aniścit eṣv ākāreṣu niścayam utpādayat tatra pravartanāyānumānaṃ pramāṇam ity asamānam ॥

[I,34,i]

atha dvitīye kalpe na pramāṇāntaram iti kathaṃ granthe nīyate । yāvatā pramāṇam evedaṃ na bhavati, tato nedaṃ pramāṇam iti yuktaṃ vaktuṃ syāt । satyam etat, kiṃ tu pareṇa pramāṇāntaram iti kṛtvāpanyastam । atas tathaiva pratiṣiddham ity adoṣaḥ ॥

[I,34,ii]

na ca punaḥ punar abhijñāna ity abhijñāne phale kartavye yaj jñānaṃ viśeṣadṛṣṭam, tan na pramāṇam ity arthaḥ । yady api jñānābhijñānayor vastuto na bhedaḥ, tathāpi pramāṇaphalavad bheda utprekṣyate । abhijñeyārthākārotpattyā jñānaṃ pūrvagṛhītārthagrahaṇād abhijñānam iti । caśabdena pratyakṣeṇa gṛhītasyaiva punar anityaṃ varṇādīti yad grahaṇam, tad api na pramāṇam iti darśayati । punaḥ punar ity anenāsakṛd ity asyārtham ācaṣṭe ॥

[I,34,iii]

nanu ca pūrvagṛhītasyārthasya sakṛd api grahaṇe na pramāṇam, tat kim ucyate asakṛd iti । paramatopapradarśanārthatvād adoṣaḥ । sāṅkhyena hi viśeṣadṛṣṭānumāna<I,35>sya lakṣaṇam uktam — yadā tenaiva dhūmena tasyaivāgreḥ punaḥ punar astitvaṃ pratipadyata iti ॥ atas tanmataṃ darśayitum evam uktam, na punaḥ sakṛdgrahaṇāt pramāṇāt pramāṇam iti kṛtvā ॥

{1.3bcd}

[I,35,i]

vivādās padībhūtaṃ vastu kāraṇam antareṇa na pratīyata ity ataḥ pṛcchati — kiṃ kāraṇam iti । ācāryas tv adhigataviṣayatvam apramāṇye kāraṇam upadarśayiṣyann āha — aniṣṭhāsakter iti । sāṅkhyāto lakṣaṇataś ca pramāṇām iyattāparicchedo niṣṭhā । tadabhāvaḥ prasajyata ity arthaḥ । anadhigatārthādhigantṛ pramāṇam iti sāmānyena pramāṇalakṣaṇam । saṅkhyā dve trīṇi vety evamādi tan na prāpnoti । yadi sarvaṃ jñānaṃ pramāṇatveneṣyata ity anena prāk pakṣavirodham āha, anavasthayā vyavasthāyā nirākaraṇāt । smṛtādivad iti dṛṣṭāntam āha । dṛṣṭāntam āha । viṣaye 'py evan nirdeśo 'stīty āha — smṛtir eva smṛtim iti bhāve ktavidhānāt । tad yathety evamādinā hetoḥ sādhyenānugamaṃ dṛṣṭānte darśayati, tadvad iti pramāṇaphalam । yat pūrvādhigatārthaviṣayam, na tat pramāṇam, smṛtyādivat । tathā ca viśeṣadṛṣṭam । vyāpakaviruddhaḥ ॥

[I,35,ii]

syād etat — na sa yathādṛṣṭa eva viśeṣas tena gṛhyate, kiṃ tu tatsāmānyam iti । na tarhi viśeṣadṛṣṭaṃ tadanumānam, api tu pūrvadṛṣṭasāmānyenottarasya <I,36> grahaṇāt sāmānyato dṛṣṭam eva । syād etat — na tatrāgnisāmānyamātragrahaṇaṃ kevalam, pratiniyatadeśavartino grahaṇād iti । neyatā viśeṣasamāśrayeṇa samānatā hīyate । tathā hy agurudhūmādinā tajjananaṃ vahniṃ pratipannam apy agnisāmānyam eva pratyeti, na tu pratiniyataṃ bhedam iti yat kiñcid etat ॥

[I,36,i]

syād etat — yatra bhinnau dṛṣṭāntadārṣṭāntikau, tatra tayoḥ sāmānyenānumānaṃ sambhavati । iha punar ya eva dṛṣṭāntaḥ, sa eva dārṣṭāntikaḥ, sa evāyam iti pradarśanāt । ato na sāmānyenānumānam iti । yadi yad eva sādhyaṃ sa eva dṛṣṭāntaḥ, evaṃ tarhi tena gṛhītāvismṛtena bhavitavyam । na hy anyathā dṛṣṭānto bhavitum arhati । tataś cādhigataviṣayatvāt sa eva doṣaḥ । atha manyase — naivedam adhigataviṣayam, yato 'dhigatasya dharmiṇaḥ pūrvadṛṣṭārthabhāvo dharmo 'nadhigato 'nenādhigamyata iti । ayuktam etat । yadi tāvat  pūrvāparakāladṛṣṭāv arthau bhinnau, evaṃ saty atasmiṃs tadbhāvādhyāropo viparyāsa eva, na pramāṇam । athābhinnau, adhigataviṣayam, yato 'dhigatasya dharmiṇaḥ pūrvadṛṣṭārthabhāvas tasyānadhigato 'dhigamyata ity uktam । tad ayuktam uktam, yato nāyaṃ kacid arthasya dharmo yaḥ prāṅ nāsīt paścād bhavati । yadi syāt sa eva tayoḥ svabhāvabhedāsraya iti nānābhavaḥ syāt । tatra cokto doṣaḥ ॥

<I,37>

[I,37,i]

tasmāt tad evedam iti niścayo viśeṣadṛṣṭatvenābhimato na smṛter bhidyate । idaṃ hi smṛteḥ svarūpaṃ yad utābhrāṣṭadarśanasaṃskārasya tad evedam iti pūrvadṛṣṭākārādhyavasāyaḥ । tas asyāpy astīti smṛtir eva ॥

[I,37,ii]

svabhāvavipratipattinirākaraṇātāha — pratyakṣam ityādi । pratigatam akṣaṃ pratyakṣaṃ prādisamāsaḥ । etal lakṣyam । kalpanāpoḍham iti lakṣaṇam । kalpanāyā apoḍham apagataṃ kalpanayā vāpoḍhaṃ rahitaṃ kalpanāpoḍham । kalpanāpoḍhanirdeśāc ca jñānātmakaṃ tad iti gamyate । yato jñānasyaiva kalpanāsaṃsargo 'sti, atas tatpratiṣedhena tad eva pratīyate ॥ tad yathā dhenurānīyatāmavatseti vatsapratiṣedhena godhenur eva nānyā ॥

[I,37,iii]

atha keyaṃ kalpanā nāmeti । kalpanānāṃ bahutvātkātra kalpanā vivakṣiteti saṃśayānasya paśnaḥ । nāmajātyādiyojaneti । namno jātyādibhir atulyakakṣatvād ādiśabdena parigrahe 'pi । parikalpitā hi jātyādayo na tattvataḥ santi । nāmajātyādīnāṃ yojanā nāmajātyādiyojanā । kṛdyogā ca ṣaṣṭhī samasyata iti samāsaḥ sādhanaṃ kṛteti vā । kā punar asau । nāmādīni tadvatārthena yayā yojyante saṃsṛjyante, sā pratītiḥ kalpanā । na cātra yojanaṃ prati vyāpṛtaiva pratītiḥ kalpanā vivakṣitā, kiṃ tarhi yāpi yojanaṃ prati na vyāpṛtā <I,38> tatra ca yogyapratibhāsā sāpi । yo hi yatra yogyaḥ, sa tad akurvāṇo 'pi tenavyapadeśam arhati, pācakavat pākena । tena stanapānādiṣu bāladārakāder yat kalpanājñānam, tan nāmādisaṃsargābhāve 'pi savikalpakaṃ siddhaṃ bhavati ॥

[I,38,i]

yadṛcchāśabdeṣv ityādi । anapekṣitajātyādipravṛttinimittā yadṛcchāśabdāḥ । jñānadharmo hi kalpanā, na śabdadharmaḥ । tato nāmnā viśiṣṭo 'rtho gṛhyata iti vaktavya abhilāpena kalpanāyās tulyaviṣayatāṃ darśayitum — ucyata ity āha । tat punar abhilāpavat kalpanājñānam api na svalakṣaṇaviṣayam, ato na tat pratyakṣatvenābhimatam iti jñāpanārtham । ḍittha iti ḍitthaśabdasvarūpātmanā kila so 'rthas tad abhinnarūpatayā pratīyate । evaṃ jātyādibhis tadabhedopacārāpannās te 'rtho ucyante । daṇḍī viṣaṇīti saṃyogisamavāyidravyabhedenodāharaṇadvayam ॥

[I,38,ii]

atreti kriyādravyaśabdeṣu । kriyādravyābhyāṃ tadvatāṃ yaḥ sambandhaḥ, sa śabdapravṛttinimittam । tathā hi kārakatvaṃ daṇḍitvam iti bhāvapratyayaḥ kriyākārakādisambandhe bhavati । yathoktam — samāsakṛttaddhiteṣu sambandhābhidhānam iti । śabdapravṛttinimitte ca bhāvapratyayo bhavati । tathā cāhur — yasya guṇasya hi bhāvādravye śabdaniveśaḥ, tadabhidhāne tv atalāv iti । pācako daṇḍīti ca kṛttad dhitau । tasmād atra sambandhe bhāvapratyayaḥ ॥

<I,39>

[I,39,i]

anye tv arthaśūnyair iti svamataṃ darśayati । arthena jātyādinā viśeṣaṇena rahitair ity arthaḥ । yathā yadṛcchāśabdā jātyādiviśeṣaṇavṛttinirapekṣā eva saṅketavaśāt svārtham abhidadhati, tathā gavādiśabdā api । icchāmātrāyattavṛttayo hi śabdās te puruṣair icchayā yatra yatra yathābhūte niyujyante, taṃ tam arthaṃ tathābhūtaṃ pratyāyayantaḥ kena cāryante । jātyādayas tv asiddhā iti kutas teṣāṃ śabdapravṛttinimittabhāva ity abhiprāyaḥ ॥

{1.4}

[I,39,ii]

atha kasmād ityādi । anyatarābhāve 'bhāvād dvayādhīnā vṛttiḥ । tat kasmād dvayādhīn ajanma jñānam aindriyam indriyeṇaivocyate, na viṣayeṇa । ālokas tu na sarvendriyajñānimittam, cakṣurvijñānasyāpi keṣāñcin na bhavatīti nopanyastaḥ । manaskārasya tu loke viṣayavac cakṣurvac ca kāraṇatvaṃ na prasiddham ity anupanyāsaḥ । kāraṇāntaropalakṣaṇamātraṃ vā viṣayagrahaṇam । atra yathā kathañcit pratyakṣaśabdaṃ vyutpādya so 'vikalpe sarvatra samyagjñāne sañjñātvena paribhāṣyata ity ācāryam atam । paras tv ataj jānānaḥ — akṣanimitto 'yam asañjñāśabda iti matvā pṛṣṭavān । ācāryas tv abhyupagamya parihāram āha — asādhāraṇahetutvād iti । akṣāṇi hi svasantatipatitasyāpi manovijñāsyendriyāntaravijñānasya ca nāśrayībhavanti । ato rūpīndriyavijñānanirdeśas tair iva nyāyyaḥ, tadasādhara<I,40>ṇahetutvāt । evaṃ hi cakṣurādivijñānam eva pratipādayituṃ śakyate, na tu viṣayair nirdeśena, tasya tatrāgamakatvāt, tat punaḥ sādhāraṇakāraṇatvāt । tathā hi viṣayā manovijñānānyasantānavijñānasādhāraṇāḥ, navacandrādiprekṣāsvan ekasantānacakṣurādivijñānakāraṇatvāt tatpṛṣṭhalabdhamanovijñākāraṇatvāc ca । aya, atrābhiprāyaḥ । lokena hy asya śabdasyāsminn abhidheye pratyāyanasāmarthyam astīti gamakatvam abhisamīkṣya śabdaḥ prayujyate । tac ca gamakatvam indriyavijñāne 'kṣavyapadeśasyāsti na viṣayavyapadeśasya । gamakatvena ca śabdaniyogārhatā vyāptā । atas tadgamakatvaṃ viṣayavyapadeśān nivartamānaṃ tanniyogārhatām api nivartayati । ato na viṣayair vyapadiśyata iti ॥

[I,40,i]

nanu ca icchādhīn avṛttayaḥ śabdāḥ sarvārthapratyāyanayogyā ity uktam । satyam, saiva tv icchā lokas yāsādhāraṇena vyapadeśe 'sti, na sādhāraṇena । tathā hi loko 'sādhāraṇenaiva vyapadiśati, yad darśayati — asādhāraṇena ca vyapadeśo dṛṣṭa ityādi । vyavahāratā ca loke tadvyavasthātra vidheyā, tasya pratyāyanatvād iti manyate ॥

[I,40,ii]

upapannam etad iti yuktam, yasmāt pratyakṣaṃ kalpanāpoḍhaṃ pratyakṣeṇaiva sidhyati । kim atrānyayā yuktyety abhiprāyaḥ । pratyātmavedyo hi svasaṃvedanena jñānāntareṇa vā sarveṣām abhilāpasaṃsargayogyo vikalpaḥ । asaṃsṛṣṭavikalpaṃ <I,41> ca pratyakṣaṃ vikalparahitam evātmānaṃ paricchindad utpadyate । tathā hi sarvaviṣayebhyo vikalpānapanīya pratyastam itāśeṣavikalpena manasā sthito 'pi cakṣurvijñānena rūpam īkṣate prāṇī । tac ca kalpanārahitaṃ pratyakṣam eva । santy evendriyadhiyaḥ kalapanāḥ, kiṃ tu tā nopalakṣyanta iti cet, vārttam etat । tathā hy avikalpāvasthāyā ūrdhvaṃ kiñcid vikalpayan sa cittadhārāṃ saṅkalaty evaṃ caivaṃ ca kalpanā mamāsīd iti । tad iyaṃ kalpanopalakṣyasvarūpaiva । tad yadīndriyavijñāne syāt prāg apy upalakṣyeta, na ca saṃhṛtavikalpāv asthāyām upalakṣyate । tena sā tatra nāstīti gamyate ॥

[I,41,i]

syād etat — yad etad vyāpṛtendriyasya jñānaṃ manovijñānatvena vo 'bhimatam āviṣṭābhilāpam ahir ahir iti dhārāvāhi yojakaṃ cābhidhānābhidheyayor darśakaṃ cārthasya, tadvikalpakam apy avikalpajñāvat yakṣam eveṣṭavyam । anyathā vicchinnaṃ darśanaṃ syād vikalpaś ca, vikalpenādarśānād darśanena vāvikalpanāt tayor asahavṛtteś ca । asti cāvicchinnaṃ darśanam । tasmād indriyajamevedaṃ savikalpam i<I,42>ti । vikalpakapratyakṣavādino 'pi tarhi gavādau san nihite viṣaye tatra ca pratyakṣa pravṛtte 'rthāntaranāmānusmṛtavikalpāntarasammukhībhāve ca sati pratyupasthitaviṣayagrāhi vikalpakaṃ jñānaṃ pratyakṣatvenābhimataṃ kathaṃ na vyavahitam, vyavadhāne vā katham avicchinnaṃ darśanaṃ bhavatīti tulyaṃ codyam ॥

[I,42,i]

syād etat — vijātīyavikalpakāle nāsti darśanam, tathāpi tan naiva vicchinnam avasīyate, laghutaravṛttinā darśanāntarodayena tacchūnye kāle pratisandhīyamānatvād alātavat । alātaṃ hi pūrvapūrvadeśaṃ hitvāntarāntaradeśavarti na sakalacakrābhāsāṃ deśaṃ vyāpnotīti tatra viniyatadeśapratibhāsy eva vijñānaṃ syāt, na sarvadiganugatapratibhāsam । atha ca cakrābhāsaṃ darśanaṃ bhavati । ataḥ pratisandhānāc cakraṃ paśyāmīti matir yathā tathehāpīti । tad etan nirvikalpapratyakṣavādino 'pi tulyam । yad uktam — laghutaravṛttinetyādi, tat kramabhāvinor api darśanavikalpayor avicchinnadarśanādhyavasāyasādhanāya paryāptam eva nirvikalpapratyakṣavādino 'pi । atha vā savikalpam avikalpaṃ ca yugapadve vijñāne vartete, tayoḥ svabhāvabhedam anavadhārayan pratipattā mohādaikyam adhyava<I,43>syati । tasmān manovijñānam evaitat savikalpakam, indriyajñānaṃ tu tena sahabhāvi kramabhāvi vā nirvikalpakam eveti sthitam etat ॥

[I,43,i]

pratyakṣaṃ kalpanāpoḍhaṃ pratyakṣeṇaiva sidhyatīty atra kaścid āha —
	yadi pratyakṣaśabdena pratyakṣam abhidhīyate /
	kathaṃ tatkalpanāpoḍham anuktaṃ gamyate katham //
iti । tad etat kalpanāsvarūpasaṃvarṇanenaiva nirastam । na hy abhidheyatā kalpanā, yato 'bhidhīyamānasya kalpanāpoḍhatā nivarteta, kiṃ tarhi pratītiviśeṣa ity uktam ॥

[I,43,ii]

na kevalaṃ pratyakṣeṇaiva kalpanāpoḍhatvaṃ siddham, api tv āgamenāpīti darśayann āha — abhidharme 'pītyādi । samaṅganaṃ samaṅgaḥ saṅgatir ity arthaḥ । cakṣurvijñānena samaṅgaḥ so 'syāstīti cakṣurvijñānasamaṅgī, cakṣurvijñānena saṅgata iti yāvat । nīlaṃ vijānātīti nīlam arthasvarūpeṇa jānāti, no tu nīlam iti na tan nāmato nīlam etad iti jānāti । etad evottareṇa padadvayena spaṣṭayati । na tv arthe dharmasañjñīti nārthe nāmasañjñīty arthaḥ ॥

[I,43,iii]

kathaṃ tarhītyādi । sañcitālambanāḥ pañca vijñānakāyā iti yo 'yaṃ siddhāntaḥ, sa kathaṃ yujyate, yadi tad ekata ekatvenālambanaṃ na vikalpayanti । <I,44> evaṃ manyate — sañcitaśabdena samudāya ucyate, bhāve niṣṭhavidhānāt । sañcitaṃ sañcayaḥ samudāya iti hi paryāyāḥ । sa ca sañcayo naikasyaiva paramāṇoḥ, api tu bahūnāṃ sādhāraṇo dharmaḥ । tatra sāmānye yady akṣadhīḥ pravarteta, tadāsau vikalpikā syāt । sāmānyabuddhir hi niyataṃ vikalpenānubadhyate । na hi sāmānyaṃ vastusatsiddhānta iṣyate । tasmāt saiva tadvikalpayatīti kṛtvā yac cetyādi । āyatanasvalakṣaṇaṃ cakṣurvijñānagrāhyatvādi, tat pratyete svalakṣaṇaviṣayāḥ pañca vijñānakāyāḥ, na dravyasvalakṣaṇam iti । dravyaṃ nīlādibhedāḥ । nīlādidravyasvalakṣaṇaviṣayatvapratiṣedhena sāmarthyāt teṣāṃ yat sāmānyam abhinnam, sa viṣaya ity uktaṃ bhavati । ataś ca kalpanāpoḍhatvaṃ nirudhyate tat kathaṃ tacchāstram anyathā netuṃ śakyata iti bhāvaḥ ॥

[I,44,i]

tasyobhayasyāpy ekaparihāram āha — tatrānekārthajanyatvād ityādi । tatreti śāstre, anekārthajanyatvād ity anekaparamāṇujanyatvād ity arthaḥ । svahetupratyayebhyo ye paramāṇavo jāyante, te 'nyonyasannidhānāvasthāprāptā eva santaḥ pratyekaṃ vijñānopajananasamarthāḥ sañcitaśabdenoktāḥ । sañjātaṃ citaṃ cayapa<I,45>ryāyam eṣā iti sañcitāḥ । prādibhyo dhātujasya veti bahuvrīhir uttarapadalopaś ca, praparṇa iti yathā । naiva vātra ktapratyayo bhāve vihitaḥ, kiṃ tarhi karmaṇy eva । parasparopasarpaṇapratyayair hi te sañcitāḥ saṃhīkṛtāḥ । tais tathāvidhair anekaiḥ svapratibhāsā janyanta iti sañcitālambanā ity uktāḥ, sarvāṃs tān sañcitākhyānaviśeṣeṇālambante, naikam eva dravyam iti kṛtvā ॥

[I,45,i]

yac coktam — āyatanasvalakṣaṇaṃ pratyeta ityādi, atrāpi tair eva yathoktaiḥ paramāṇubhiḥ sahitenaiva cakṣurādivijñānaṃ janyate, na svakenaiva । tasmād anekārthajanyatvāt svārthe sāmānyagocaram ity uktam । sāmānyaṃ gocaro 'syeti vigrahaḥ । nanu ca sāmānyam abhinnakalpitam, indriyajñānasya ca viṣayaḥ paramāṇvākhyam anekaṃ vastu । tat kathaṃ sāmānyagocaratvam upapadyate । naiṣa doṣaḥ । yat tat sañcitaśabdenāyatanasvalakṣaṇaśabdena coktam anekaṃ paramāṇuvastu tad eva pratiniyatavijñānajananasāmarthyena sādharmyeṇa parasparāpekṣayā samānam । samānam eva sāmānyam, svārthe taddhitavidhānāc cātur varṇyavat । tad etad uktaṃ bhavati — sañcitagocaram āyatanasvalakṣaṇagocaraṃ coktam iti । na tu bhinneṣv abhedakalpanād iti sāmānyaviṣayam uktam ity anena sambandhaḥ । na tu bhinne<I,46>ṣv abhedakalpanayā sañcitaviṣayam āyatanasvalakṣaṇaviṣayaṃ coktam ity arthaḥ । na dravyasvalakṣaṇam ity anenāpy ekaparamāṇudravyaniyamanirākaraṇaṃ śāstraṃ kṛtaṃ draṣṭavyam, na sāmarthyākṣiptaṃ sāmānyaviṣayatvam ity aviruddham ॥

[I,46,i]

ye tu — ekendriyavijñānakāryatvenaikarūpāyatanādisaṅgrahe 'pi nānekaṃ dravyaṃ yugapadgṛhyate, api tu krameṇaivety āhuḥ, ta idaṃ vaktavyāḥ — yadi yugapadbahūnāṃ dravyāṇāṃ grahaṇaṃ nāsti, kathaṃ tarhi tilam āṣādīnāṃ vicchinnadeśāvasthitānāṃ sakṛdgrahaṇam iti । na hi tair asaṃyuktatvād vijātīyatvāc ca dravyāntam ekam ārabdham, yasya grahaṇaṃ syāt । darśanasya laghuvṛttitvād bhrāntyā kramavaty api tatrākramādhyavasāya iti cet, kramapātiṣv api tarhi teṣu lāghav asya tulyatvāt, sakṛd eva gṛhṇāmīty adhyavasāyaḥ syāt । kiṃ ca rephasakārādiṣu varṇeṣu laghuvṛttitvād darśanasyākramagrahaṇādhyavasāyaḥ syāt । tataś ca kramabhedāc chrutibhedo na syād rasaḥ sara ity evamādiṣu śabdeṣu । āśubhramaṇodakabindupātādiṣu ca darśanasya lāghavāt krameṇa gṛhṇāmīti bhāve grahaṇādhyavasāyo na syāt । tasmād yāvad gocarībhūtaṃ tat sarvaṃ yugapad eva pratīyata iti ॥

{1.5}

[I,46,ii]

āhuś ceti । viṣayavipratipattiṃ nirākurvaṃs tad eva nirvikalpatvaṃ samarthayate — dharmiṇo 'nekarūpasyeti । arthāntaravyāvṛttisamāśrayeṇa kalpitā ye dharma<I,47>bhedāḥ sāmānyarūpā jñeyatvādayaḥ, tadapekṣayān ekarūpasyety uktam । na punar aṃśavān asau viṣayā, netarasyeti darśayann āha — nendriyāt sarvathā gatir iti । indriyād iti hetau pañcamī lyablope vā । indriyād dhetor indriyaṃ vā prāpya sarveṇa prakāreṇa svasāmānyalakṣaṇābhyāṃ grahaṇaṃ na bhavatīty arthaḥ ॥

[I,47,i]

tasya tarhi kīdṛśam ālambanam ity āha — svasaṃvedyam ityādi । svasaṃvedyam anāgamikam । anirdeśyam anākhyeyam । atha vā svasaṃvedyam ity ukte kiṃ svabhāvaṃ tad iti vaktavyam ity āha — anirdeśyam iti । anirdeśyatvaṃ tu tasya jñānayo rūpabhedād iti manyate । tathā hi yac ca śābdaṃ jñānaṃ yac caindriyam, anayor bhinnaḥ pratibhāsaḥ, spaṣṭāspaṣṭtvāt । na hi yathā vyāpṛtendriyasyārtharūpam indriyajñāne sphuṭenākāreṇa pratibhāsate tathā śābde । yadi punar indriyagocara eva nirdeśyaḥ syāt, śābde 'pi tathaiva pratibhāseta, na caivam ।

<I,48>

[I,48,i]

na ca yaḥ śābde na pratibhāsate sa śabdārthaḥ । tasmād bhinnarūpajñānagrāhyatvān nendriyaviṣayaḥ sitatvād nirdeśya iti । yady eto bhinnarūpajñānagrāhyam, na tat tad eva । tad yathāśvād bhinnajñānagrāhyo mahiṣaḥ । indriyaviṣayād bhinnarūpajñānagrāhyaś ca śabdaviṣayaḥ sitatvādiḥ । vyāpakaviruddhaḥ ॥

[I,48,ii]

syād etat — aindriyasya jñānasya cakṣurādir āśrayaḥ, śābdasya tu manaḥ । tasmād āśrayabhedād ekaviṣayatve 'pi tayoḥ pratibhāsabheda iti । yady evam, katham idānīṃ cakṣurvijñānādīni bhinnārthānīti vo niścayaḥ । tatrāpi hi śakyate vaktum — eka eva teṣāṃ viṣayaḥ, pratibhāsabhedas tv āśrayabhedād iti । kasyacid arthākārasyānukārāc chābdasyaivaikaviṣayatvaṃ na cakṣurvijñānādīnām । na hi tāni parasparam arthasya kañcanākāram anukurvantīti cet, na, tatrāpi jñeyatvādy anukāritvam asty eva ॥

[I,48,iii]

yāpīyaṃ kalpanā yadi śābdendriyajñānayor naiko viṣayo yaḥ sāstrādimānsa gaur ity upadeśād gāṃ pratipadya paścād vyaktiviśeṣaṃ paśyan katham evam avasyati yo 'sau mayā śruto 'yam asāv iti, kathaṃ ca gāmānayety ukta indriyaviṣaya eva pravartate । na hy anyam upalabdhavato 'nyatra sa evāyam iti pratyayo bhavati । nāpy anyatra codite 'nyatra pravṛttir yuktā । bhavati ca tathā pratyayaḥ pravartate ca śabdād i<I,49>ndriyaviṣaye । tasmād ekas tayor viṣaya iti sāpyakalpanaiva । tattvavicāravyāpṛtā hi vyākhyātāraḥ khalv evaṃ viṣayavivekaṃ kurvanti, na vyavahartāraḥ । te tu tattvādhyavasāyena dṛśyavikalpyāv arthāv ekīkṛtya vyavakarantīty alam atiprasaṅgena । evaṃ svasaṃvedyam anirdeśyaṃ rūpaṃ pratyakṣasya viṣayo na caivaṃvidhe kalpanā pravartate, tasyāḥ śābdenaikaviṣayatvād iti viṣayanirdeśenāpi pratyakṣasyāvikalpatā samarthitā bhavati ॥

[I,49,i]

kathaṃ tarhīdānīm aniścayātmanaḥ pratyakṣād vyavahāraḥ । niścinvan hīdan tayā sukhaduḥkhasādhanayoḥ prāptiparihārāya pravartate । naiṣa doṣaḥ । arthālocanamātre 'pi hi pratyakṣe 'nubhavāhitasāmarthyabhāvismaraṇapūrvakābhyām abhilāṣetarābhyāṃ vyavahāro bhavati । vastudharmo hy eṣa yad anubhavaḥ paṭīyān smṛtibījam ādhatte yādṛśaṃ ca sukhasādhanaṃ duḥkhasādhanaṃ vānubhūtam, tādṛśadarśanād asya prabodhe sati tad evedam iti smṛtir bhavati । tato 'bhilāṣetarayor anyataraḥ । tato 'pi puruṣasya yathārhaṃ pravṛttir iti ॥

[I,49,ii]

evaṃ tāvad ityādi nigamanam । ihaivaṃ tāvat pañcendriyajam iti vacanāt tāvac chabdenānyad apy apañcendriyajam asti tasya ca lakṣaṇaviśeṣaḥ pṛthagvakṣyamāṇa ity etat sūcitam । tac ca sarvaṃ nirvikalpam eveti nyāyamukha eva parigatam ।

<I,50>

[I,50,i]

ataḥ kasyacin nipuṇamateś codyam āśaṅkate । tatredaṃ codyam — nanu sarva evāmī pratyakṣabhedā nirvikalpā eva, tataś ca pratyakṣaṃ kalpanāpoḍham ity anenaiva saṅgṛhītāḥ । tathā hi nyānamukhenaiṣāṃ pṛthaglakṣaṇaṃ praṇītam ।  tatra kim artho 'yam iha pṛthaglakṣaṇabheda ucyata iti । ato 'sya parihārāyāha — paramatāpekṣaṃ cātra viśeṣaṇam iti viśeṣaṇam viśeṣo bheda iti paryāyāḥ । tac ca prakṛtatvāt pratyakṣalakṣaṇasyeti gamyate । atreti prakaraṇe । yo 'yaṃ pṛthaglakṣaṇaviśeṣaḥ sa pareṣāṃ vipratipattilakṣaṇaṃ yan mataṃ tadapekṣaḥ ॥

[I,50,ii]

tatra manovijñāne pratyakṣa indriyajñānānubhūtatam eva tam arthaṃ gṛhṇātīti keṣāñcid vipratipattiḥ । rāgādisaṃvedane nāsty eva tad iti । yogijñāne 'py eṣaiva । yata evaṃ pareṣāṃ vipratipattir atas tadapekṣaḥ pratyakṣaṃ kalpanāpoḍham ity anena saṅgṛhītasyāpy apañcendriyajasya pratyakṣasya pṛthaglakṣaṇabheda ucyate । paravipratipattinirāsāyeti bhāvaḥ ॥

[I,50,iii]

apare tu — kiṃ punaḥ pañcendriyajaṃ savikalpam apy asti, yata etad viśeṣaṇam ity āha — paramatāpekṣaṃ cetyādi । pareṣām indriyajaṃ jñānaṃ kiñcit savikalpakaṃ yad vyutpannavyavahārasya, kiñcid avikalpakaṃ yad itarasyeti matam । atas tadapekṣam indriyajñānasya kalapanāpoḍham ity etad viśeṣaṇaṃ paraparikalpitasavikalpe<I,51>ndriyajñānavyavacchedārtham iti vyācakṣate । teṣāṃ yadi paramatāpekṣam etad viśeṣaṇam uktam, evaṃ saty akriyamāṇe 'smin paramatāpekṣe svamatena lakṣaṇam anuktam eva syāt । tataś ca lakṣaṇaṃ pratyakṣasya kiṃ syāt । etac codyamasamāhitaṃ syād ity uktam etat ॥

[I,51,i]

sarve tv avikalpakā eveti tuśabdena na svamatāpekṣo 'yaṃ pṛthaglakṣaṇaviśeṣa ucyate, vipratipatter abhāvād ity arthaṃ dyotayati । viśeṣaṇena pratyakṣaṃ kalpanāpoḍham ity anenaiva sarvalakṣyasaṅgrahaḥ ॥

{1.6}

[I,51,ii]

mānasaṃ cetyādi । caśabdaḥ samuccayārthaḥ । arthaśabdo 'yaṃ jñeyaparyāyaḥ । rāgādīnāṃ svaṃ rāgādisvam । svaśabdo 'yam ātmavacanaḥ । arthaś ca rāgādisvaṃ ca, tasya saṃvittir artharāgādisvasaṃvittiḥ । saṃvedyate jñāyate 'nayeti saṃvittiḥ । saṃvitteḥ pratyekam abhisambandhaḥ । sāvikalpikā mānasaṃ pratyakṣam ॥

[I,51,iii]

tatra manovijñānam indriyagṛhītam evārthaṃ gṛhṇāti tato vānyam iti dvayī kalpanā । yadi pūrvā, tatas tasya prāmāṇyam eva na syāt, gṛhītagrahaṇāt smṛtyādivat । atha dvitīyā, tadāndhāder apy arthagrahaṇaṃ syāt । indriyajñānanirapekṣaṃ hi mano<I,52>vijñānaṃ yadi bāhye 'rthe pravartate, tadā cakṣurādivikalasyāpi darśanaṃ prāpnoti । tadvaktavyaṃ kīdṛśaṃ tad ity āha — mānasam apītyādi । rūpādayaś ca te viṣayāś ceti karmadhārayaḥ ॥

[I,52,i]

nanu ca rūpādayo viṣayā eva, tat kim arthaṃ viṣayagrahaṇam । anālambyamānarūpādivyavacchedārtham, na hy avijñāyamānaviṣayā bhavanti । kasya punas te viṣayāḥ । anantaram indriyajñānasya prakṛtatvāt tasyaiva rūpādiviṣayāṇāṃ vikāro rūpādiviṣayavikāraḥ, sa ālambanaṃ yasya tat tathoktam । samudāyavikāraṣaṣṭhyāś ca bahuvrīhir uttarapadalopaś ceti vacanāt samāsa uttarapadalopaś ca suvarṇālaṅkāra iti yathā । kaḥ punar viṣayasya vikāraḥ । yas tena janita uttarakṣaṇaviśeṣaḥ, sa tasya vikāra iti vyavahriyate, na tv avasthite dharmiṇi dharmāntaranivṛttau dharmāntarāv abhāvaḥ, sāṅkhyaparikalpitasya pariṇāmasya niṣiddhatvāt । tad etad uktaṃ bhavati — indriyajñānaviṣayajanitasamantararūpādikṣaṇālambanam iti । anenāprāmāṇyadoṣaḥ pratikṣiptaḥ । kutaḥ punas tasya niyataviṣayateti cet, yatas tasya yaḥ samanantarapratyayaviśeṣaḥ sa svaviṣayopajanitānantararūpādikṣaṇasahakāryeva taj janayati, atas tad yathoktaviṣayam evety avagaccha ॥

<I,53>

[I,53,i]

anubhavākārapravṛttam iti । anubhūyate 'nenety anubhavaḥ । ākāra ābhāsaḥ । sa punar ananubhavarūpo 'py asti, yaḥ smṛtyādīnām ity atas tadvyavacchedāyānubhavagrahaṇam । anubhava ākāro yasya, tat tathoktam । kiṃ punas tat । pūrvoktanyāyenendriyajñānam eva । tenānubhavākāreṇa pravṛttam utpannam anubhavākārapravṛttam । etad uktaṃ bhavati — indriyajñānāt samanantarapratyayād utpannam iti । anena yad uktam — andhāder apy arthagrahaṇaṃ syād iti, tan nirastam । yasmān na tadbāhyeṣv artheṣu svatantraṃ pravartate, kiṃ tarhīndriyapratyayāpekṣam, andhādeś cendriyajñānaṃ nāstīti nāsti tat ॥

[I,53,ii]

rāgādiṣu ca svasaṃvedanam iti । svasya saṃvedanaṃ svasaṃvedanam । saṃvedyate 'neneti saṃvedanam । grāhakākārasaṅkhyātam anubhavasvabhāvatvam । anubhavasvabhāvatvād eva hi rāgādayo 'nubhavātmatayā prakāśamānā ātmānaṃ saṃvedayante, ātmasaṃvedanā iti ca vyapadiśyante । atas tadanubhavātmatvam eṣāṃ pramāṇam । yat punarbhāvarūpaṃ saṃvedanaṃ svādhigamātmakam, tat tasya phalaṃ veditavyam । ātmā tu teṣāṃ prameyaḥ । rāgādigrahaṇaṃ spaṣṭasaṃvedanadarśanārtham । sarvajñānānāmā<I,54>tmasaṃvedanasya pratyakṣatvāt । avikalpakatvaṃ tu tasyāśakyasamayatvāt । viṣayīkṛte hi samayaḥ śakyate kartum । na cānutpannaṃ rāgādyātmānaṃ saṃvittir viṣayīkaroti, rāgādyātmarūpatayā tasyā apy anutpannatvāt । utpanne 'pi rāgādyātmani saṃvittir abhilāpaṃ na yojayati । tathā hi sābhilāpamādāya tatra yojayet । abhilāpagrahaṇe ca kṣaṇikatvān na sā, nāpi rāgādaya iti kiṃ kena yojyeteti । aśakyasamayatvād rāgādīnāṃ saṃvittir nāviṣṭābhilāpā yena yatra śabdasya samayo na gṛhītaḥ, na tacchabdena taṃ saṃyojya gṛhṇāti । tad yathā cakṣurvijñānaṃ gandham । na gṛhītaś ca rāgādyātmani tatsaṃvedanena śabdasamayaḥ । kāraṇābhāvaḥ ॥

[I,54,i]

atra kecid āhuḥ — āśrayāsiddhiḥ । tathā hi svasaṃvitter nirvikalpakatvaṃ sādhyam । sā ca jñānasyāpi tāvan na samasti । kutaḥ punaḥ sukhādīnām ajñānarūpāṇām । te hy ekasminn ātamani jñānena saha samavāyāt tenaikārthasamavāyinā gṛhyanta iti svayaṃ <I,55> prameyarūpā eva । atas te parasyāpi na saṃvedakāḥ, kutaḥ punar ātmana iti । tais tajjñānam avaśyaṃ sukhādyākāram abhyupeyam, anyathā tasya te vedyā eva na syuḥ । na hi jñānasattaivārthānāṃ saṃvedanā yuktā, tasyāḥ sarvatrāviśeṣāt sarvārthagrahaṇaprasaṅgāt । yaj jñānaṃ yadākārarahitam, na tat tasya saṃvedakam । gojñānam ivāśvasya । sukhādyākārarahitaṃ ca sukhādijñānam । vyāpakavirudddhaḥ ॥

[I,55,i]

bhavatu jñānaṃ tadākāram, tataḥ kim iti cet, idaṃ tato yat tad eva hlādaparitāpādyākārānugataṃ sukhādīti siddhaṃ sukhādi jñānarūpam । bodharūpaṃ hi vastu sātādirūpaṃ teṣām api siddham । tatra jñānaṃ sukhaṃ duḥkham ityādikā yatheṣṭaṃ sañjñāḥ kriyantām । nātra kaścin nivārayitā । yathā jñātahlādādika ākāro 'jñānarūpasukhādikṛto na bhavati, tathānyatra pratipāditam । iha tu bahugranthabhayān na pratanyate ॥

[I,55,ii]

yo 'py āha — nāntārāḥ sukhādayo nāpi cetanāḥ, kiṃ tarhi tadviparītasvabhāvāḥ prameyā eveti, tasyāpi yathoktanītyā hlādādyākārabodhātmalkaṃ vastu <I,56> siddham । tasyaiva ca svasaṃvedanaṃ pratyakṣam uktam, na tadvyatiriktasya sukhādeḥ paraparikalpitasya । tac ca svasaṃvedanaṃ sādhayiṣyamāṇam iti nāsty āśrayāsiddhiḥ ॥

[I,56,i]

nanu sarvasyaiva jñānasyendriyajasyāpi mana āśraya ity apy ete pañca vijñānakāyā indriyadvayāśrayā iti vacanāt, tatkasmād idam eva mānasam ucyata ity āha — indriyānapekṣatvād iti । rūpīndriyanirapekṣatvād iti bhāvaḥ । yasya mana evāśrayo na rūpīndriyam, tanmānasam abhisaṃhitam । ye tarhi pañca vijñānakāyās tatsamprayoginaś ca rāgādayaḥ, teṣāṃ svasaṃvedanaṃ kathaṃ mānasaṃ pratyakṣam । svasaṃvittisāmānyena tajjātīyatvāt । kathaṃ punar indriyānapekṣatve pratyakṣaśabdo yujyate । yāvatākṣanimittaḥ pratyakṣavyapadeśaḥ, uktam etaj jñānaviśeṣasya pāribhāṣikīyaṃ sañjñeti । atha vā manaso 'py akṣatvāt pakṣāntare 'py adoṣaḥ ॥

[I,56,ii]

tathā yoginām iti । yathā mānasam avikalpakaṃ pratyakṣam, tathā yoginām api । yogaḥ samādhiḥ । sa yeṣām asti, te yoginaḥ । gurunirdeśāvyavakīrṇam iti । tenāvyavakīrṇaṃ rahitam ity arthaḥ । etena spaṣṭāvabhāsitvam api tasya labdham, nirvikalpasya spaṣṭatvāvyabhicāritvāt । mātraśabdo 'dhyā<I,57>ropitārthavyavacchedārthaḥ । tena yad bhūtārthaviṣayam āryasatyadarśanavat, tad eva pramāṇam, nābhūtārthaviṣayaṃ viplutaṃ pṛthivīkṛtsnādi । nanu cāyam artho vakṣyamāṇād evāpavādāl labhyate, tat kiṃ mātragrahaṇena । satyam etat, tathāpi prādhānyajñāpanārtham asya lakṣaṇavākya evāyam arthaḥ paridīpitaḥ । prādhānnyaṃ punar mokṣahetutvāt । nirvikalpakatvaṃ punas tasya spaṣṭāvabhāsitvaṃ ca bhāvanāniṣpattiphalatvāt । yad bhāvanāniṣpattiphalaṃ jñānam, tan nirvikalpaṃ spaṣṭāvabhāsi ca bhavati । tad yathā kāmaśokādy upaplutānāṃ priyāviṣayaṃ jñānam । tathā ca yogijñānam । svabhāvaḥ ॥

{1.7–1.8ab}

[I,57,i]

kalpanājñānam api nāmeti । asyāyam arthaḥ — yat svasaṃvedyam, tat svādhigamaṃ prati pratyakṣam, rāgādijñānavat । tathā ca kalpanājñānam iti svabhāvaḥ । satyam etad ityādineṣṭasiddhiṃ darśayati । evaṃ manyate — yatra viṣaye yaj jñānaṃ śabdasaṅketagrāhi, tat tatra śabdadvāreṇa tasya viṣayagrahaṇāt savikalpakaṃ bhavati, svarūpaṃ cāśakyasamayaṃ yathoktaṃ prāk । atas tatrādhigantavye sarvaṃ jñānaṃ pratyakṣam eveti ॥

[I,57,ii]

evaṃ tāvat pratyakṣam iti tāvac chabdaḥ krame । pratyakṣam uktvā tadābhāsābhidhānam iti kramaḥ ॥

<I,58>

[I,58,i]

nanu ca — pratyakṣaṃ kalapanāpoḍham iti bruvatā — savikalpaṃ pratyakṣābhāsam ity uktaṃ bhavati । tac ca prāg evoktaṃ nāmajātyādiyojanena, tat kim arthaṃ punas tasya vacanam । yad artham, tad utttaratrāviṣkariṣyāmaḥ ॥

[I,58,ii]

bhrāntisaṃvṛtisajjñānam ityādi । anena caturvidhaṃ pratyakṣābhāsam uktam । tatra bhrāntijñānam ity anenānyārthakalpanājñānam ekaṃ tāvad uktam । tathā hy asad evodakādikam arthāntaraṃ saṅketasamāśrayān mṛgatṛṣṇādiṣv adhyāropayanty upadyate kalpanā । saṃvṛtisatsv ityādinā saṅketasamāśrayasamāropakalpanāpravṛttaṃ dvitīyam । kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ saṃvṛtisatsu yaj jñānaṃ tat pratyakṣābhāsam ity āha — arthāntarādhyāropād iti । tad dhi prajñaptivastuṣu rūpādiṣv arthāntarabhūtān ghaṭādīn adhyāropayati, na prajñaptivastumātraṃ pratipadyate । kathaṃ punar etaj jñāyata ity āha — tadrūpakalpanāpravṛtttatvād iti । tad dhi tān saṃvṛtisato 'rthāntaratvena kalpayad upadyate । adhyāropitārthākārakalpanayā pravṛttatvāt saṃvṛtijñānaṃ ghaṭādīn adhyāropayati, na tu tatprajñaptivastumātraṃ pratyeti ॥

[I,58,iii]

tatra tāvad rūpādīnām udakāharaṇādyekakāryatayā tadanyebhyo bhinnānāṃ sakṛtsamuditānāṃ svakārye niyojanārthaṃ tatra lokasya yaḥ śabdasaṅketaḥ, tam āśrayaṃ <I,59> kṛtvārthāntareṇa ghaṭādinā rahiteṣv api rūpādiṣu bhāvato 'rthāntaramadhyāropayantī pravartate kalpanā ghaṭaḥ paṭa ityādikā । tathā samuccayādivyavacchedaphalaśabdaniveśasamāśrayeṇaikatvādiveśinī । tathā deśāntarotpādiṣu evaṃ satsu, tathā bahuṣv ekakāryeṣu samudāyeṣu, evaṃ nairantaryādyavastheṣu, atathābhūtatavyavacchedāya śabdasamayam āśrityārthāntarabhūtaṃ karma sattāṃ ghaṭatvādi saṃyogādi ca yathākramam adhyāropayanty upajāyate kalpanā । tad evaṃ prabhedataḥ śabdakalpaiva saṅketamātrasamāśrayam । dvitīyam etat kalpanājñānam ॥

[I,59,i]

mṛgatṛṣṇādiṣu yā toyādikalpanā, sā nānudakavyavacchedāyodake kṛtaṃ saṅketamātrāśritya pravartate, yena saṅketasamāśrayāyam evāntarbhāvān na pṛthagvacanaṃ tasyāḥ syāt, kiṃ tarhy asad evodakādikaṃ tatra bhūtasaṅghāte saṅketasamāśrayāt pūrvadṛṣṭam anyad evārthamadhyāropayanty utpadyate । ata evāha — toyādikalpanāpravṛttatvād iti । ghaṭādayas tu svopādānād anye na santy eva । saṅketamātranimittaiva tadadhyāropiṇī kalpaneti pūrvasyāḥ pṛthag uktā ॥

[I,59,ii]

anumānatatphalādijñānam iti । anumīyate 'nenety anumānam, liṅgam । tatra sa evāyaṃ dhūma iti sambandhakālānubhūtārthakalpanāpravṛttaṃ jñānam । tatphale 'pi liṅgijñāne pūrvānubhūtakalpanāsti, sa evātrāgnir iti sāmānye<I,60>nānumānāt । smārte 'pi pūrvānubhūtākāro vikalpa itthaṃ tanmayānubhūtam iti । ābhilāṣikam api pūrvānubhūtakalpanāṃ nātivartate, vinā tyābhilāṣābhāvāt । ādiśabdena saṃśayajñānagrahaṇam । tatrāpi kiṃ tad evedam āhosvidanyad ity evam ākārā pūrvānubhūtakalpanā jāyata itīdaṃ pūrvānubhūtārthakalpanājñānaṃ tṛtīyam ॥

[I,60,i]

sataimiram  ity anenendriyopaghātajaṃ ca taimirādijñānaṃ caturthaṃ pratyakṣābhāsam uktam iti ॥

[I,60,ii]

tatra dve pūrvake kalpanājñāne na pratyakṣe iti khyāpanārtham ukte । kutaḥ punas tayoḥ pratyakṣāśaṅkā yena tannivṛttaye yatnaḥ kriyate । te hi pratyakṣasya saṃvṛttinī । tasmāt sūkṣmam utpādakālavibhāgaṃ duravadhāratvād anupalakṣayataḥ pratyakṣe evaite iti kasyacin matiḥ syāt । dṛśyate ca keṣāñcid vipratipattiḥ । yathā ghaṭādiṣu jñānaṃ saṃvṛtisatsu mṛgatṛṣṇādiṣu codakādijñānaṃ pratyakṣam eveti । tathā hi tasyaiva mṛgatṛṣṇādau toyādijñānasya vyavacchedāyāvyabhicārīti pratyakṣalakṣaṇe viśeṣa<I,61>ṇam upāttam । akṣopaghātajajñānanivṛtty arthaṃ tad iti cet, na, arthasan nikarṣagrahaṇād evān arthasambhūtasya dvicandrādijñānasya nivṛtteḥ । anyathendriyajam ity eva vācyaṃ syāt ॥

[I,61,i]

anumānādijñānaṃ tu siddham eva yathāpūrvānubhūtasamayasmṛtibalapravṛttam apratyakṣaṃ ceti tasyāpratyakṣatve siddhe 'pi yad ihopādānām, tat pūrvayor eva kalpanājñānayor apratyakṣatvasādhanāya । yat pūrvānubhūtasamayasmṛtibalabhāvi, na tat pratyakṣam । yathedam anumānādijñānam । tathā ca pūrvake jñāne । vyāpakaviruddhaḥ । tad evaṃ trividham eva kalpanājñānaṃ lakṣaṇavacanenārthāpattito nirastam ॥

[I,61,ii]

caturthas tu yaḥ pratyakṣābhāsaḥ, so 'pavādo 'tra draṣṭavyaḥ, na tu lakṣaṇavacanenārthāpattyā nirākṛtasyodāharaṇam । anyathā lakṣaṇavyabhicāraḥ syāt । tasmāt tenāpavādavacanena bāhyābhyantaropaghātapratyayopahatendriyajñānaṃ kalpanāpoḍhatve 'pi pratyakṣābham ucyate । sataimiram ity atra tu timiraṃ sarvendriyopaghātapratyayopalakṣaṇamātraṃ kila draṣṭavyam ॥

[I,61,iii]

yas tv āha — dvicandrādijñānaṃ naivendriyajam, api tu mānasam eveti, tena vaktavyam — kim indriyajasya lakṣaṇam iti indriyabhāvābhāvānuvidhānam iti <I,62> cet, tad ihāpi tulyam । tadvikāravikāritvam iti cet, atrāpy etad evottaram । api cecchayā sarpādibhrāntivad eva tan nivartyeta । śakyante hi kalpanāḥ pratisaṅkhyānabalena nivartayitum । kiṃ ca vikṛtākṣasya vikāranivṛttau kalpayato 'pi na nivarteta । na caidam । tasmād idam apy aindriyam eva । uktaṃ cācāryeṇa te 'pi hi paramārthato 'nyathā vidyamānā dvicandrādyābhāsasya nīlādyābhāsasya ca jñāsya kāraṇaṃ bhavantīti । nātrābhiniveṣṭavyam । yata evam indriyajam api viplutam asti, ata eva bhrāntītyādinoktād vikalpavargād itikaraṇavyavacchinnāt pṛthagavikalpakaṃ pratyakṣābham ācāryeṇoktaṃ sataimiram iti ॥

[I,62,i]

atra codyate — ihāvisaṃvādi pravartakaṃ jñānaṃ pramāṇam abhimatam, na hy ābhyām arthaṃ paricchidya pravartamāno 'rthakriyāyāṃ visaṃvādyata ity abhidhānāt । indriyopaghātajasyāpi ca kasyacij jñānasya kvacit samīhite 'visaṃvādanaṃ pravartakatvaṃ cāsty eva । tato yad etat keśādipratibhāsitaimirādijñānaṃ yasya samīhite keśādivastuni saṃvādo nāsti, tasya mā bhūt prāmāṇyam । yat punar etat kāmalopaplutalocanasya śukre śaṅkhādau pītaśaṅkhādinirbhāsam, yac ca cirakālatimi<I,63>rāvṛtanayanatvād viprakṛṣṭatvād vā spaṣṭeṣu nīlādiṣv aspaṣṭanīlādyākāram, yad api naiyānasaṅkṣobhāhitavibhramaṃ sthireṣv api vṛkṣādiṣu gamikriyāviṣṭapādapādipratibhāsi, tasyaivam prakārasyāny asyāpi cātasmiṃs tadgrahād bhrāntasyāpi vastuni pratibandhādīpsitārthāvisaṃvādinaḥ kvacit prāmāṇyam eva nyāyyam । tathā hi tataḥ pravartamāno 'sati pratibandhe niyamena śaṅkhādivastumātrāyātārthakriyāsamartham artham abhisamīhitam āsādayati । atha saṃvādinām apy eṣāṃ vitathapratibhāsitvāt prāmāṇyaṃ neṣyate, anumānasyāpi tarhi neṣṭavyamata eva । na ca neṣyate । tasmāt teṣām api samīhitārthakriyāsamarthe śaṅkhādivastumātre yatra saṃvādas tatrāviruddhaṃ prāmāṇyaṃ paśyāmaḥ । śakyate ca vaktum — yato jñānāt pravṛttaḥ puruṣo 'sati pratibandhe niyamenābhīṣṭam artham āsādayati, tat tatra tasya pramāṇam । tad yathābhimataṃ pratyakṣam anumānaṃ ca । yathoktāc ca jñānāt pravṛttaḥ puruṣo 'sati pratibandhe niyamenābhīṣṭaṃ śaṅkhādivastumātram āsādayatīti svabhāvaḥ । na cedam anumānam, aliṅgajatvān nirvikalpatvāc ca । na ca tṛtīyaṃ pramāṇam iṣṭam, itaḥ pratyakṣam evety abhyupeyam । yat kalpanāpoḍhaṃ samīhitārthāvisaṃvādi, tat pratyakṣam । tad yathābhimataṃ pratyakṣam । tathā ca prakṛtaṃ jñānam । svabhāvaḥ ॥

<I,64>

[I,64,i]

syād etat — śaṅkhādimātre vastuni samīhite saṃvādādiṣṭam eva tasya pratyakṣatvam, viśiṣṭe tu pītādyākāravati visaṃvādān neṣyata iti । na tarhi sataimiram ity anenāpavādapadena bāhyābhyantaropaghātapratyayopahatendriyajñānaṃ kalpanāpoḍhatve 'pi pratyakṣābhamuktam । kevalaṃ tatra sataimiravacane timiraṃ sarvendriyopaghātapratyayopalakṣaṇamātram ity evaṃ vyākhyeyam, upahatendriyajñānasyāpi kasyacit pratyakṣatvāt । nāpy abhrāntam iti viśeṣaṇaṃ kartavyam, bhrāntasyāpi kasyacit kvacit pratyakṣatveneṣṭatvāt ॥

[I,64,ii]

tasmāt sataimiram ity etad apavādapadam anyathā vyākhyāyate । timiraśabdo 'yam ihājñānavacano yathā nimiraghnaṃ ca mandānām ityādau vākye । timire bhavas taimiraḥ । vyavacchedaphalatvāc ca vākyasya sarvavākyaṃ sāvadhāraṇam iti timira eva bhava iti sāvadhāraṇe vākyārthe tad dhito bhavati । kaḥ punar asau । visaṃvādaḥ । sa hi yadi bhavaty ajñāna eva bhavati, na jñāne, tasyaikāntena saṃvāditvāt । prasiddhataraṃ caital loke saha tena taimireṇa vartata iti sataimiram, visaṃvādīti yāvat । savikalpasya ca visaṃvādino bhrāntyādiśabdenopādānād idaṃ nirvikalpam avasīyate । smārtābhilāṣikaṃ ceti cāyaṃ vaśabdaḥ samuccayārtho <I,65> bhinnakramaś ca sataimiraṃ cety evaṃ draṣṭavyaḥ । tenāyam artho bhavati — visaṃvādi ca jñānaṃ pratyakṣābhāsam iti । evaṃ bhrāntasyāpi nirvikalpasya yata saṃvādas tatra pratyakṣatvam । yatra tu visaṃvādas tatra tadābhāsatvam ity etat siddhaṃ bhavati । na caivaṃ sati kaścid virodhaḥ, kalpanājñānavat । yathā hi kalpanājñānasya svādhigamāpekṣayā pratyakṣatvaṃ bāhyaviṣayāpekṣayā tad ābhāsatvaṃ na viruddhyate, tathā yathoktasyāpi jñānasya viṣayabhedāpekṣayā tad ubhayam iti ॥

{1.8cd}

[I,65,i]

atra cety asmanmate । savyāpārapratītatvād iti saha vyāpāreṇa pratītyatvād ity arthaḥ । etat pramāṇatvopacāranibandhanam । pramāṇaṃ phalam eva sad iti । pramāṇasyādhigamaḥ phalam । tac ca svayam eva tadātmakam iti tato na vyatiriktam ॥

[I,65,ii]

na hy atra bāhyakānām iva pramāṇād arthāntaraṃ phalam iti mā bhūd ihāpi tadvad eva doṣaḥ । tasyaiva tv ityādināyam arthaḥ sūcitaḥ — naiva vyavasthirasvabhāvaṃ kiñcid asti sādhyaṃ sādhanaṃ vā, pratītirūpānupātitvāt sarvatra sādhyasādhanavyavahārasya । ihāpi cāsti । jñānasyādhigamarūpatvāt sādhyatvapratītir iti phalatvam upacaryate । tasyaiva ca viṣayākāraparigrahāt savyāpārapratītir iti <I,66> pramāṇatvam upacaryate, vyavahriyata ity arthaḥ । tathā hi tajjñānaṃ viṣayākāratāṃ dadhānaṃ nirvyāpāram api satsvaviṣaye 'dhigamātmanā vyāpāreṇa khyāti nānyathā । tasmāt saiva tasyātmabhūtā viṣayākāratā pramāṇam iti ॥

[I,66,i]

yuktaṃ caitat । tathā hi na kriyāsādhanam ity eva sarvasyāḥ kriyāyāḥ sarvaṃ sādhanaṃ sarvā vā kriyā sarvasya sādhyā, anavasthāprasaṅgāt, kiṃ tarhi tasyāḥ kriyāyās tatsādhanam, yā yataḥ sādhanād avyavadhānena prasiddhim upayāti । saiva ca tasya kriyā sādhyā । tatra rūpādau karmaṇy anubhavātmanā sādṛśyātmano jñānasya tena svabhāvena karaṇabhūtena bhāvyam, yenedaṃ nīlasya jñānam, idaṃ pītasyeti vibhāgena vyavasthā kriyate । anyathā sarvaṃ jñānaṃ sarvasyārthasya syāt, na vā kasyacit kiñcit, aviśeṣāt ॥

[I,66,ii]

indriyāder āvilatādibhedo niyāmaka iti cet, na, tasyājñānasvabhāvatvā<I,67>t sarvajñānahetutvāc ca । nāpi san nikarṣaḥ, ata eva । nāpy arthālocanam, asati viṣayasārūpye 'rthālocanasyaivāsiddheḥ । viśeṣaṇajñānam api, ata eva ॥

[I,67,i]

tasmād yo 'yaṃ niyamo nīlasyaiveyam adhigatiḥ pītasyaiva cetyādikaḥ, so 'rthasārūpyād anyato na sidhyati । tatas tad eva sādhanam arthādhigateḥ, sarvakārakopayoge 'py asyārthasyeyam adhigatir iti sambandhasya tata evāvyavadhānena siddheḥ । tac ca tasya sādhanatvaṃ vyavasthāsamāśrayatvena, na tu nirvartakatvena, abhedāt ॥

[I,67,ii]

syād etat — vastuno 'bhedāj jñānāṃśayor aikye yaiva kriyā tad eva kārakam । ato hatam etad iti । tad asat, yato vastuno 'bhede 'pi yo 'yaṃ dharmabhedaḥ prameyarūpatārthādhigatiś ceti, so 'bhyupagamyata eva vyāvṛttibhedopakalpitaḥ, abhinne 'pi vastuni vijñānapratibhāsabhedena sādhyasādhanavyavasthādarśanāc ca । <I,68> yathā nipīyamānaṃ madhum adayati, ātmanātmānaṃ dhārayati, buddhyā gṛhṇātīti nāyaṃ vastusan niveśī sādhyasādhanavyavahāra ity acodyam etat ॥

[I,68,i]

kathaṃ yathāvyāpāram antareṇāpi tadvat tayā pratibhāsata ity āha — tad yathetyādi । iha nīlādyākāra eka evānubhūyate । sa vijñānasyātmabhūto 'vaśyam abhyupeyaḥ । anyathā tasyārthena sambandho na syāt । na ca tasmāt tadākāram atad ākāraṃ vā bahir vyatiriktaṃ vastūpalabhyate । na cālambanaṃ gaṭate । kathaṃ ca na ghaṭate । yathā ca na ghaṭate, tathā vādavidhiparīkṣāyāṃ vakṣyati ॥

{1.9}

[I,68,ii]

yad apīdaṃ kalpyate — satsv apy anyeṣu hetuṣu jñānakāryāniṣpattiḥ kāraṇāntaraṃ sūcayati । sa bāhyo 'rthaḥ syāt । tasmād vyatirekato bāhyārthasidhir iti, tad apy ayuktam, yato vijñānakāryāniṣpattir vijñānavāsanāparipākavaikalyād api sambhavati । tasmān na vijñānavyatiriktasya kasyacit saṃvittiḥ sambhavati । vijñānam eva tu svasaṃvid itam utpadyata iti svasaṃvittir eva phalam । bhavatu nāma bāhyārthaḥ, tathāpi yathāsaṃvedanam eva viṣayo niścīyata iti tad eva phalaṃ yuktam । na hi yathāsvabhāvam anubhavo 'rthasya, yato yathāsau vyavasthitasvarūpas tathā śakyeta niścetum, sarvajñānānām ekākāratvaprasaṅgāt । anekākārās tu <I,69> vijñaptayaḥ । tathā hy ekasminn eva vastuni pratipattṛbhedena paṭum andatādibhir ākārair anugatāni vijñānāny upalabhyante । na caikaṃ vastvanekākāram, anekatvaprasaṅgāt ॥

[I,69,i]

ato nārthasya yathāsvabhāvaṃ niścayaḥ śakyate kartum iti sandhāno bāhyetar apakṣayor ekenaiva sūtreṇa phalaviśeṣavyavasthāṃ cikīrṣur āha — svasaṃvittiḥ phalaṃ vātreti । pūrvaṃ viṣayasaṃvittiḥ phalam uktā । ato vikalpārtho vāśabdaḥ । atreti pūrvokte pratyakṣe ॥

[I,69,ii]

svābhāsaṃ viṣayābhāsaṃ ceti । svamābhāso 'syeti svābhāsaṃ svarūpābhāsam, grāhakākāram ity arthaḥ । svarūpam evāsya jñānasyābhāsaḥ, yad eva hi jñānasya jñānarūpatvam, tenaiva svena rūpeṇābhāsata iti kṛtvā । viṣayābhāsaṃ ceti । atra yadā bāhyo viṣaya āśrīyate, tadā viṣayasyevābhāso 'syeti vigrahaḥ । yadā tu nāśrīyate, tadā viṣaya ābhāso 'syeti । viṣayaḥ punar atra grāhyāṃśaḥ, tatra viṣayavyavahārāt । tasyetyādi । satyasati vā bāhye 'rtha ubhayābhāsaṃ jñānaṃ saṃvedyate । tasya yat svasaṃvedanaṃ svānubhavaḥ, tatphalaṃ bhaviṣyati ॥

[I,69,iii]

kiṃ kāraṇam iti kayā yuktyā । na hi svasaṃvittiḥ sambhavatīty eva phalatvena kalpayituṃ yujyate । bāhyārthapakṣe tv asambhāvanīyam evaitat । viṣayasya hy adhigamāya cakṣurādayo vyāpāryante, na tu vijñānasya । na ca vijñānopalabdhir eva viṣa<I,70>yopalabdhiḥ, vijñānād viṣayabhedāt । ataḥ svasaṃvitteḥ phalatvam anupapannam iti manyamānasya praśnaḥ ॥

[I,70,i]

tadrūpo hy arthaniścaya iti kāraṇam । yadā hītyādyasyaiva vivaraṇam । hiśabdo yasmādarthe । yasmād yadā saviṣayaṃ jñānam arthaḥ, tadā svasaṃvedanānurūpam arthaṃ pratipadyate pratipatteṣṭam aniṣṭaṃ vā । tasmāt svasaṃvittiḥ phalaṃ yujyate । saviṣayam iti । saha viṣayeṇa saviṣayam । tatrāntarjñeyapakṣe grāhyāṃś alakṣaṇena viṣayeṇa saviṣayam, tatraiva viṣayavyavasthānāt । bāhyārthapakṣe tu bāhyena । tatra vijñaptimātratāyāṃ vijñānavyatiriktasya vastuno 'bhāvād buddhir eva yad eṣṭaṃ svamākāram anubhavati, tad eṣṭam arthaṃ niścinoti, viparyayād viparītam ॥

[I,70,ii]

kathaṃ punar ātmanaivātmānam anubhavati jñānam । na hi tasyaiva karmakartṛkaraṇabhāvo yujyata iti cet, evam etat । naiva tasya paramārthataḥ karmādibhāvaḥ । tathāpi tādātmyāt prakāśavat tatra tathāvyavahāro na virudhyate । prakāśo hy ātmaprakāśanaṃ bhavati, na pradīpāntaram apekṣate । nāpy ātmānaṃ bhāvataḥ prakāśayati । kevalaṃ prakāśātmatayotpadyamāna ātmanaḥ prakāśaka ity ucyate । tadvad anubhavāt manopajāyamānā buddhir ātmanaḥ prakāśiketi vyavahriyate । bāhyapakṣe 'pi yathāsaṃvedanam evārtho 'vasīyate । na hi yathārtham anubbhava iti prāg evoktam ॥

<I,71>

[I,71,i]
