atha saṃvedanānurūpam arthaṃ pratipadyata iṣṭam aniṣṭaṃ vety etāvad eva kiṃ noktam । kiṃ yadā hi saviṣayaṃ jñānam arthaḥ, tadetyanena । asti prayojanam, yasmāt prāk svasaṃvedanaṃ pramāṇam uktam, tena ca jñānasvarūpam eva saṃvedyata iti svasaṃvedanaṃ tasyaiva phalam iti sphuṭam avasīyate । tataś ca svasaṃvedanānurūpaṃ hy arthaṃ pratipadyata iṣṭam aniṣṭaṃ vetīyaty ucyamāne svasaṃvedanam eva pratyakṣam adhikṛtyedaṃ phalavyavasthānam iti kasyacid āśaṅkā syāt । sarvasya ca pramāṇasyedaṃ phalam iti । ata āśaṅkānivāraṇārtham — yadā hi saviṣayam jñānārtha ity uktam । arthaśabdaś cāyaṃ prameyavacanaḥ । saviṣayam iti ca sākalye 'vyayībhāvaḥ । ata etad uktaṃ bhavati — na kevalaṃ yadā jñānaṃ pramāṇasya prameyam apekṣate, tadā svasaṃvedanānurūpam arthaṃ pratipadyata iti svasaṃvittiḥ phalam, api tu yadāpi viṣayam, tadāpīti ॥

[I,71,ii]

ihāsati bāhye 'rthe svasaṃvedanaphalavyavasthāyāṃ grāhakākārasya prāmāṇyaṃ vakṣyati । tataś cāsati bāhye 'rthe prameye yathā svasaṃvedanaphalavyavasthāne grāhakākāraḥ pramāṇam iṣṭam, tathā sati bāhye 'rthe prameye grāhakākāra eva pramāṇam ity āśaṅkā syāt । atas tan nirāsāyāha — yadā tv ityādi । bāhye prameye <I,72> svasaṃvedanaphalavyavasthāyām api viṣayābhāsataiva jñānasya pramāṇam iṣyate, na tu vijñaptimātratāvad grāhakākāraḥ ॥

[I,72,i]

nanu yadāpi bāhyo 'rthaḥ prameya iti pakṣaḥ, tadāpi grāhakākāro 'bhimata eva, tasya svasaṃvedyatvāt । tat kim iti tadā pramāṇatvena na vyavasthāpyata ity āha — tadā hi jñānasvasaṃvedyam apītyādi । jñānasya svasaṃvedyam iti vigrahaḥ । yady api sarvakālaṃ svasaṃvedyam asti svarūpam, tathāpi tad anapekṣya jñānasya bāhye prameye viṣayābhāsataiva pramāṇam, na svābhāsatā, bāhye 'rthe tasyāḥ sādhanatvāyogāt । ayogas tv aparārthatvāt । grāhakākāro hy ātmaviṣayaḥ kathaṃ bāhye 'rthe pramāṇaṃ syāt । na hy anyaviṣayasyānyatra prāmāṇyaṃ yuktam ॥

[I,72,ii]

yasmād ityādinā tasya prāmāṇye kāraṇam āha । mīyata iti niścīyate । yathā yathetyādi । jñānasya jeyākāravaśena bāhyo 'rtho niścīyata ity arthaḥ । atra ca yathā dhūmenāgnir anumīyata ity ucyate, na cāsau sākṣāt tenānumīyate, kiṃ tarhi taddhetukena dhūmajñānena, tathā yad api — so 'rthas tena mīyata ity ucyate, tathāpi tatsādhanayā svasaṃvideti veditavyam । tathā hi yathā yathārthākāro jñāne san niviśate śubhāśubhādirūpeṇa, tathā tathā svasaṃvittiḥ prathate । yathā yathā ca sā khyāti, tathā tathārtho niścīyate śubhāśubhādirūpādiḥ । yadi hi <I,73> tadākāram utpannaṃ syāt, tadā tādṛśasyātmahaḥ saṃvittiḥ syāt । tataś ca tadvaśādiviṣayaniścayo bhavet, nānyathā । tasmād viṣayābāsatā pramāṇam ॥

[I,73,i]

nanu ceha viṣayasārūpyasya saṃvidaṃ prati sādhanatvaṃ pratipādayitum iṣṭam । ato yasmāt sā khyāti tadvaśād iti vaktavye kim artham — yasmāt so 'rthas tena mīyata ity uktam । asti prayojanam । sā hi svasaṃvit, arthasaṃvido yat kāryam arthaniścayaḥ, tat karoti । ata upacāreṇārthasaṃvid eva kāryato draṣṭavyety amum arthaṃ sūcayitum evam uktam । evaṃ hi pramāṇaphalayor viṣayabhedo na bhavati, yatraiva sādhanaṃ bāhye, tatraiva saṃvid iti kṛtvā ॥

[I,73,ii]

kathaṃ tarhi svasaṃvittiḥ phalam uktam । paramārthatas tādātmyāt svasaṃvittiḥ phalam uktam । upacāreṇa tu kāryato 'rthasaṃvittir eva sā dṛṣṭavyety aviruddham । iha vijñaptimātratāyāṃ grāhakākāraḥ pramāṇam, grāhyākāraḥ prameyam iti vakṣyati । atas tatra codyamāśaṅkate ॥

[I,73,iii]

tatredaṃ codyam — kathaṃ punar abhinnātmano jñānasya grāhakākārādivibhāgaḥ, yenāsaty api bāhye 'rthe pramāṇādi syād iti । atas tat parihārāyāha — evam ityādi । asyāyāṃ samudāyārthaḥ । naiva tattvatas tasya vibhāgo 'sti, kevalam avidyopaplutais tadgrāhakākārādivibhāgavad iva lakṣyate । ato yathādarśanam iyaṃ <I,74> pramāṇaprameyavyavasthā kriyate, na yathātvam iti । kathaṃ punar avibhaktaṃ sat tathā pratibhāsate । yathā mantrādyupaplutākṣāṇāṃ mṛcchakalādayo hastyādirūparahitā api hastyādirūpāḥ pratibhāsante, yathā ca dūre maruṣu mahānalpo 'py ābhāti, tathedam apy avidyān dhānāṃ jñānam atathābhūtam api tathābhāti । na ca śakyate kalpayitum — mantrādisāmarthyāt te tathaivotpannā iti, yato 'nupaplutadarśanais taddeśasan nihitais tathā na dṛśyante ॥

[I,74,i]

evam iti yathoktaṃ dvyābhāsaṃ jñānam iti । jñānasaṃvedanam iti jñānasya karmaṇaḥ saṃvedanaṃ darśanam । kimbhūtam । anekākāram । anekā ākārā yasya, tat tathoktam । te punar ākārāḥ, ya anena bhrāntena nirīkṣyante, grāhakapratibhāsādayas te vivakṣitāḥ । upādāyeti tatpramāṇanibandhanaṃ gṛhītvā । tathā tathetyādi । nirvikalpe tāvad grāhakākāraḥ kalpanāpoḍhaṃ pratyakṣaṃ pramāṇam, spaṣṭapratibhāso grāhyākāraḥ svalakṣaṇaṃ prameyam । liṅgaje 'pi grāhakākāro 'numānaṃ pramāṇam, vyaktibhedānuyāyīvāspaṣṭapratibhāso grāhyākāraḥ sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ prameyam iti । upacaryata iti vyavahniyate । etenaitat sūcayati — <I,75> vyāvahārikasya pramāṇasya prameṇasya cedaṃ svarūpam uktam atrāpi vipratipannānāṃ sammmonirāsāya । lokottaram eva tu vibhramavivekanirmalam anapāyi pāramārthikaṃ pramāṇaṃ tasyaiva ca gocaro bhūtaṃ prameyam iti ॥

[I,75,i]

nirvyāpārās tu sarvadharmā iti । etena tasya jñānasaṃvedanasya bhrāntatvam udbhāvitam । na hi tattvataḥ kasyacid dharmasyānekākāradarśanātmako vyavahāraḥ sambhavati, ākārāṇām apariniṣpannatvāt । bhrāntir eva tu sā, yad avidyān dhāstadavedyavedakākāram api jñānam tathā paśyanti । yadi tarhy atattvavidāṃ sarvam eva jñānam upaplutam, kathaṃ pramāṇetaravyavasthā । upaplavavāsanāviśeṣasadbhāvāt । yato jalādipratibhāsino jñānāt sparśanāhlād atṛptyādipratyayānāṃ sambhavaḥ, tadvyavahārāvisaṃvādāpekṣayā pramāṇam, itarat tathāvidhavāsanāvirahād apramāṇam ity adoṣaḥ ॥

[I,75,ii]

atha yad idaṃ kāryāt kāraṇānumānam, tat katham । kathaṃ ca na syāt । yato dhūmapratibhāsi jñānaṃ pūrvam evāvirbhavati, paścād analapratibhāsi । na hi tatprāgdhūmapratibhāsino jñānāt saṃvedyate । tato 'nagnijanya eva dhūmaḥ syād iti kathaṃ <I,76> tenāgner anumānam । naiṣa doṣaḥ । dahanākārajñānajananavāsanāviśeṣānugata eva hi cittasantāno dhūmābhāsāṃ dhiyam utpādayati, na tu yaḥ kaścit । atas taṃ gamayad dhūmatur jñānaṃ prabodhapaṭuvāsanāṃ dahanākārāṃ buddhiṃ bhaviṣyantīṃ pratipattur gamayati । atra hi hetudharmānumānena rasāde rūpādivad anumānaṃ bhavatīty acodyam ॥

{1.10}

[I,76,i]

āha cetyādinā tāṃ prameyādivyavasthāṃ darśayati । ya ābhāso 'syeti vigrahaḥ । svāṃśasya ca mānatvena vidhānād iha viṣayābhāso gṛhyate । prameyaṃ tad iti sa viṣayābhāsaḥ prameyam । pramāṇaphalate punargrāhakākārasaṃvittyor iti grāhakākārasya pramāṇatā, saṃvitteḥ phalatā । atra ca yady api saṃvittiśruter aplāctaratvam, tathāpi grāhakākārasya pramāṇatvāt tasya ca vyutpādyatvenādhikṛtatvād abhyarhitatvam । ato grāhakākāraśabdasyaiva pūrvanipātaḥ । trayaṃ nātaḥ pṛthakkṛtam iti । trayasyāpi tattvato 'pariniṣpannatvāt, na jñānāt pṛthak karaṇam ॥

<I,77>

{1.11}

[I,77,i]

iha dvirūpatām aṅgīkṛtya svasaṃvitteḥ phalatvam uktam । na ca tad dvairūpyaṃ jñānasyopapadyate, tadanupapattyabhāvād iti matvā pṛcchati — atha dvirūpam ityādi । kasmāt punas trairūpye praṣṭavye dvirūpatāpraśnaḥ । dvairūpye siddhe svasaṃvittir api sidhyatīty abhiprāyāt । dvairūpye hi siddhe viṣayasārūpyam ātmabhūtaṃ jñānasya saṃvedyata ity arthād ātmasaṃvedanaṃ sidhyati ॥

[I,77,ii]

viṣayajñānaviśeṣāt tv ityādi । viṣayajñānaṃ rūpādigrāhi cakurādivijñānam । viṣayajñānaṃ viṣayajñānatajñānam । atra yadi tacchabdena viṣayajñānaṃ sambadhyeta, tasyopādānam anarthakaṃ syāt, vināpi tena viṣayajñānālambanasya jñānasya pratīteḥ । tasmāt tacchandopādānasāmarthyād guṇabhūto 'pi viṣayaḥ sambadhyate, anyasyehāprakṛtatvāt । tad etad uktaṃ bhavati — viṣayajñāne viṣayākāraṃ jñānam iti । tad eva viśeṣaḥ । tathā hi tadviṣayajñānād adhikena viṣayākāreṇa viśiṣyate । parābhiprāyeṇaivam uktam । paro hi viṣayajñānasyānubhavākāraṃ kevalam icchati । tajjñānasya tv anubhavākāro 'py asti । atra ca buddher anubhavākārasya siddhatvāt sa sādhyate । na hi kaścid vādī, yo <I,78> jñānasya jñānarūpaṃ necchati । viṣayākārās tu na siddhiḥ parasyeti । tena dvairūpyaṃ sādhyate ॥

[I,78,i]

viṣaye hīti । hiśabdo 'vadhāraṇe bhinnakramaś ca । tadarthasvābhāsam evety etat pramāṇaphalam । tatrārthābhāsaṃ viṣayākāratvāt, svābhāsam anubhavākāratvāt । viṣayānurūpajñānābhāsam iti rūpāder viṣayasyānurūpaṃ jñānaṃ viṣayākāraṃ viṣayajñānaṃ svajñānenālambyata ity eṣa hetur uktaḥ । yatra hi jñāne yad vastu yenākāreṇa pratibhāsate, tattadākāram eva tenālambyata ity etad uktam । tathā hi sāsnādyākāreṇa gauḥ svajñāne pratibhāsamānas tadākāra eva tenālambyate । viṣayajñānajñāne ca viṣayākārānuraktaviṣayajñānākāra eva upalabhyate, na tu tadvyatirekeṇa kiñcid ākārāntaram । na cāpratibhāsamānas tasya viṣayo yujyate, atiprasaṅgāt । tasmād viṣayākāraṃ viṣayajñānaṃ svajñānenālambyata ity eṣa hetvartho labhyate । svābhāsaṃ ceti viṣayākāraviṣayajñānābhāsaṃ satsvarūpeṇāpi pratibhāsata ity arthaḥ ॥

[I,78,ii]

anyatheti dvirūpatābhāve । yadi viṣayānurūpam eva viṣayajñānaṃ syād iti nānubhavarūpam api । nanu ca naiva kaścid viṣayaikarūpaṃ jñānam icchati, tat kim artham idam uktam । viṣayākāre jñāne sādhyamāne kvacid iyam āśaṅkā syāt — <I,79> viṣayākāraṃ cej jñānaṃ pratipadyate, svarūpaparityāgenaiva pratipadyata iti । atas tāṃ nirākartuṃ svarūpam ajahad eva tadviṣayākāram anukarotīti darśanārtham etad uktam । svarūpaṃ veti anubhavākāram eva vā, na viṣayākāram api । jñānajñānam api viṣayajñānenāviśiṣṭaṃ syād iti ।  jñānajñānaṃ viṣayajñānālambanajñānam, tadviṣayajñānenāviśiṣṭam aviśeṣitaṃ bhavet । viṣayānukārānuraktaviṣayajñānākāratvena viśeṣeṇa viśiṣṭaṃ notpāditaṃ syād ity arthaḥ । yadi hy ālambanenātmīyākārānugataṃ svajñānam utpādyata ity etad asti, tadā viṣayajñānād utpadyamānaṃ jñānaṃ yathoktākāraviśiṣṭaṃ syāt । asati tv asmin yathā viṣayaḥ svajñānaṃ na viśeṣayati, svasārūpyeṇa viśeṣeṇa viśiṣṭaṃ notpādayati, tathā viṣayajñānam api svajñānaṃ na viśeṣayeta । viśeṣayati ca । tasmād viṣayajñānasyāpy asti viṣayākāraḥ । yad yad ākāraṃ svajñānenālambyate, tadākāraṃ tad bhavati । tad yathā sāstrādim adākāraḥ svajñānenālambyamāno gauḥ sāstrādim adākāraḥ । viṣayākāraṃ ca viṣayajñānaṃ svajñānenālambyate, tadākāro 'yam ālambyata ity asyā vyavasthāyās tadākāranibandhanatvāt । tasyāṃ sādhyāyam idaṃ kāryam । tadākāratve tu svabhāvaḥ । viṣayānubhavajñānaṃ cātropalakṣaṇamātram । cintājñānam api yathācintitārthākāraṃ jñānākāraṃ ca svajñānenopalabhyate । tathā hi <I,80> yathā viṣayajñānajñānaṃ viṣayānubhavajñānasya ne kevalām artharūpatāṃ vā pratyeti, api tv īdṛgarthaṃ tajjñānam āsīd ity ubhayākāraṃ gṛhṇāti, tathedṛgarthākārā cintāsīd iti svajñānena gṛhyate ॥

[I,80,i]

syād etat — nirākāram eva viṣayajñānam utpadyate । tasmiṃś tv arthakāryatayārthakāryam etaj jñānam ity eṣā smṛtibhir bhavati । tasyāṃ satyām anubhavajñānahetur apy arthaḥ smaryate । tataḥ paścād bhrāntyānubhavajñānam arthena saṃyojyārthākāratayādhyavasyati । na ca yāvatā bhrāntena pratipattrā tat tathāvasīyate, tāvatā tadākāram eva tad bhavatīti yuktam ity āha — na cottarottarāṇītyādi । cakāro 'vadhāraṇe । uttarottarāṇi viṣayajñānajñānādīni tāni pūrvasyānubhavajñānasya yo viṣaya uttarottarajñānāpekṣayā jñānāntaritatvād viprakṛṣṭas tadābhāsāni naiva bhavanti, naiva prāpnuvantīty arthaḥ । kutaḥ । tasyāviṣayatvāt । tasya yathoktasyārthasyottarottarajñānānām aviṣayatvāt । yadi sa teṣām api viṣayaḥ syāt, tadā tadutpanneṣu teṣv arthakāryatayārthakāryāṇy etāni jñānānīty eṣā smṛtiḥ syāt । tatas teṣām api hetuḥ so 'rthaḥ smaryeta । tataś ca tenārthena saṅkalayya tatpratibhāsitvena <I,81> bhrāntena pratipattrā gṛhyeran । na cāsau teṣāṃ viṣayaḥ, kiṃ tarhy ādyasyaiva jñānasya । tatas tad evārthasāmarthyabhāvi saṃyojyārthena tadākāratayā gṛhyeta, nottarottarāṇi, teṣāṃ tadaviṣayatvāt । gṛhyante ca tāny apy arthākārānukāritayā । tathā hy uttarottarasya jñāsyaikaika ākāro 'dhika upalabhyate । ghaṭajñānajñānena hi ghaṭākāraṃ jñānam ālambamānaḥ saha ghaṭākāreṇa ghaṭākāraṃ jñānam āsīd iti pratyeti । tajjñānena tu ghaṭajñānajñānam ālambamāno ghaṭajñānajñānam āsīd iti saha ghaṭajñānākāreṇa ghaṭajñānajñānam । evam uttareṣv api veditavyam । tad evam uttarottarajñānāni pūrvaviprakṛṣṭārthākārāṇi gṛhyante । na ca teṣāṃ svaviṣayaḥ, yatas tv aduktayā nītyā tathā gṛhyeran । tasmāt tāni svabhāvata eva tadākārāṇi bhavantīty abhyupeyam । na cādyasya jñānasya viṣayākāraśūnyatve pūrvaviprakṛṣṭārthābhāsāni bhavanti yathoktaṃ prāk । tasmāt tad apy arthābhāsam eṣṭavyam । ataś ca siddhaṃ dvairūpyam ॥

[I,81,i]

viṣayajñāne tu yaj jñānam, tadviṣayānurūpajñānābhāsaṃ svābhāsaṃ cety etad eva kutaḥ, yatas tadveśena viṣayajñānasya viṣayasārūpyaṃ syād iti cet, yatas tad eva kutaḥ, yatas tadvaśena viṣayajñānasambandhinau taddvārāyātau viṣayākārānubhavākārau tṛtīyaś ca <I,82> svābhāsalakṣaṇa ākāra ity ete traya ākārāḥ svajñānenālambyante । etac ca — uttarottarasya jñānasyaikaika ākāro 'dhika upalabhyata ity anena sampraty evākhyātam । tat kim iti vismaryate । tasmāt tatrāpi viṣayānurūpajñānākāratayā sādhye yad yad ākāraṃ svajñānenālambyata ityādi sādhanaṃ vijñeyam । nanv evaṃ tajjñānādiṣv api sādhanaṃ vācyam ity anavasthā syāt । naitad asti । yasya hi jñānasya san nikṛṣṭo viṣayaḥ, tatra sandeho jāyate — kim ayaṃ nīlākāro viṣayasya, jñānaṃ tu nirākāram, uta jñānasyeti । yasya tu jñānasya viprakṛṣṭo viṣayas tadānīm nāstīti niścitaḥ, tasya viṣayākāratāṃ prati saṃśayo na bhavaty eveti nānavasthā ॥

[I,82,i]

smṛter uttarakālaṃ cetyādi । pūrvam ekasya viṣayasārūpyeṇa viśeṣeṇa dvairūpyaṃ sādhitam । idānīṃ jñānānāṃ parasparavivekena smṛteḥ sādhyate । yathā hi parasparavilakṣaṇeṣu rūpādiṣv anubhūteṣv anyonyavivekena smṛtir bhavati, tathā jñāneṣv api । tasmād asti dvirūpatā jñānasya । anya<I,83>thānubhavamātreṇa pratyartham aviśiṣṭeṣu sarvajñāneṣu bhedenān anubhūteṣu rūpajñānam āsīn mama, na śabdajñānam iti śabdajñānaṃ vā na rūpajñānam iti yeyaṃ vivekena smṛtiḥ, sā na syāt ॥

[I,83,i]

syād etat — yathānubhavātmatve tulye sāmagrībhedāt subhādibhedo bhavati, tathā prativiṣayam aparāparasāmagrīkṛto bhedaḥ sūkṣmo 'sti । ato vivekena smṛtir bhaviṣyatīti । asad etat । spaṣṭo hi bhedaḥ smṛtinibandhanam । tathā hi kasmiṃścid upekṣāsthānīye viṣaye yaj jñānaṃ dhārāvāhi, tasyāpy aparāparendriyādisāmagrī । tathāpi na bhedena smaraṇaṃ yatheyanto buddhikṣaṇā vyatītā iti । yathā ca yamalakayor ākārasāmye 'py asti bhāvato bhedaḥ, tathāpy aspaṣṭatvāt tasya na bhedena pratyabhijñānaṃ bhavati, kiṃ tarhi tayoḥ parasparaṃ samāropaḥ । tasmād aspaṣṭabhede 'rthe na vivekinī smṛtir bhavati । ato 'rthakṛtaḥ kaścid anubhavavasyāsti viśeṣaḥ, yato vivekena smṛtir bhavatītīcchatārthasārūpyam eṣṭavyam । tataś ca siddhaṃ dvirūpaṃ jñānam iti ॥

[I,83,ii]

svasaṃvedyatā cety anenān antaroktāyā evopapatteḥ sādhyāntaram āha । na kevalaṃ smṛter uttarakālaṃ dvairūpyaṃ siddhaṃ jñānasya, api tu svasaṃvedanam api, yat pramāṇaphalatveneṣṭam । asti tāvaj jñānasya kṛtaścid anubhavaḥ । ataḥ smṛtir api <I,84> syāt । tāvatā tu kutaḥ svasaṃvedyateti matvā pṛcchati — kiṃ kāraṇam iti । ātmanaiva jñānasyānubhavo yuktaḥ, nānyeneti niścityāha — na hy asāv ityādi । asyāyam arthaḥ — yatra smṛtiḥ, tatrānubhavaḥ, rūpādivat । asti ca smṛtir iti kāryam ॥

{1.12}

[I,84,i]

syād etad ityādinā jñānāntareṇānubhavo 'bhīṣṭa eva । ataḥ siddhasādhyateti parābhiprāyam āviṣkaroti । jñānāntareṇetyādinā siddhasādhyatāṃ pariharati । yena hi jñānena jñānam anubhūyate, tatrāpy uttarakālaṃ smṛtir dṛṣṭā । na cānubhūte smṛtir yuktā । tato 'nyena tadālambanena jñānena bhāvyam । tatrāpi ca smṛtiḥ । tatas tatrāpy anyeneti । ato jñānāntareṇānubhave 'navasthā jñānānām । ekajñānābhinirhṛtāyām eva jñānaparamparāyām uttarottarāṇi jñānāni pūrvapūrvajñānālambanāny anantāni prasajyanta ity arthaḥ । tathā sati ko doṣa ity āha — viṣayāntarasañcāra ityādi । viṣayāntare jñānasya pravṛttir na syāt । iṣyate ca । tatra yato jñānāt sañcāraḥ, tasya svasaṃvedanaṃ syāt ॥

<I,85>

[I,85,i]

syād etat — mā bhūd antyasya jñānasya jñānasya jñānāntarasaṃvedyatvaṃ smṛtiś ca । tad ekam ananubhūtam asmṛtam eva cāstām । ato viṣayāntarasañcāraḥ syād iti । ayuktam etat । tathā hi yad antyaṃ jñānaṃ nānubhūyeta, tataḥ sarvāṇi pūrvakālabhāvīni jñānāny ananubhūtāni syuḥ, tadupalambhasya parokṣatvāt । yasya yad upalambhaḥ parokṣaḥ, na tat tenānubhūtam । tad yathā devadattasya jñānaṃ devadattānubhūtaṃ yajñadattena । parokṣaś cātmasambandhipūrvakālabhāvijñānopalambhaḥ prāṇinaḥ । viruddhavyāptaḥ । atha vā yad apratyakṣopalambham, na tat pratyakṣam, parokṣavat । tathā cānanubhūtopalambhaṃ jñānam । viruddhavyāptaḥ ॥

[I,85,ii]

syād etat — yad ātmanānubhūtaṃ jñānam, tad eva pratyakṣaṃ bhavati । tena parair yad anubhūtam, na tat pratyakṣam iti । sa tarhy ātmānubhavaḥ kutaḥ siddhaḥ । yadi hy anubhavaḥ sidhyet, tadātmani paratra veti syād vibhāgaḥ । sa eva tv asiddhaḥ । tasyāsiddhāv ubhayatrāpi parokṣatvenāviśeṣād ātmany ayam anubhavo nānyatrety etat parokṣopalambhena durjñānam । tat kuta ātmānubhavaḥ । yadi hi grāhyopalambhāsi<I,86>ddhāv api vastu pratyakṣam iṣyate, sarvam idaṃ jagat pratyakṣaṃ syāt, apratyakṣopalambhatvenāviśeṣāt । na ca bhavati । tasmāt svasaṃvedyātā jñānasyābhupeyeti ॥

{1.13}

[I,86,i]

ihācāryavasubandhor vādavidhir iti loke pravādaḥ । ayaṃ tu sāstrakṛt tat kṛtānāṃ śāstrāntarāṇāṃ nirdoṣatāṃ dṛṣṭvā sadoṣasya vādavidhes tat praṇītatām asambhāvayann āha — na vādavidhir ācāryasyeti ॥

[I,86,ii]

nanu cādṛṣṭakartṛkāṇāṃ śāstrāṇāṃ kartā pravādād evāvasīyate । sa cehāpy astīti kathaṃ na vādavidhir ācāryasyety āha — asāro veti niścaya iti । prakṛtatvād ācāryasya tatreti gamyate । anenaitam arthaṃ sūcayati — na tāvat prasiddhimātreṇārthaniścayo bhavati, artham antareṇāpi tasya sambhavāt । yady api ca tena sa viracitaḥ, tathāpi prathamam anupajātaprajñātiśayena satā । paścād vyavadāt abuddher asya tatrāsāraniścayo jāta iti ॥

[I,86,iii]

kathaṃ punar etad avagamyate yathā tasya tatrāsāraniścaya ity āha — anyathāvayavaprokter iti । nirdoṣāvayavābhidhānād ity arthaḥ । yad doṣadarśanāc cācāryeṇa vādavidhāv asāraniścayād vādavidhāne 'nyathāvayavāḥ proktāḥ, ta evāsmābhir doṣāḥ prakāśyanta iti darśayann āha — tenetyādi । teneti doṣavattvena ॥

<I,87>

{1.14}

[I,87,i]

tathā hy anyathāvayavaprokter ity anena doṣavattvaṃ vādavidheḥ sūcitam । pramāṇādiṣv iti pramāṇāvayavatadābhāsajātitaduttareṣu ॥

[I,87,ii]

tato 'rthād vijñānaṃ pratyakṣam iti । yasya viṣayasya vijñānaṃ vyapadiśyate, yadi tata eva tad utpadyate, nānyataḥ, nāpi tato 'nyataś ca, tajjñānaṃ pratyakṣam । tad yathā rūpādijñānaṃ sukhādijñānam iti । etena bhrāntijñānaṃ nirastam, yathā śuktikāyāṃ rajatajñānam । tad dhi rajatena vyapadiśyate rajatajñānam iti । na ca tadrajatād utpadyate, śuktikayaiva tu tad upajanyate । saṃvṛtijñānam apy anenāpāstam । tathā hi taddhaṭādibhir vyapadiśyate, ghaṭajñānaṃ ghaṭajñānam ity evam । na tu tat tebhyo bhavati, teṣāṃ saṃvṛtisattvenākāraṇatvāt । rūpādibhya eva hi tathāsan niveṣṭebhyas tad bhavati । anumānajñānam apy anenaiva nirastam । dhūmajñānasambandhasmṛtibhyām api hi tad bhavati, nāgnita eva ॥

[I,87,iii]

tato bhavaty eva, na tu na bhavatīty ayam apy atrārtho 'bhimataḥ ॥

[I,87,iv]

tad evaṃ vyavasthita idaṃ paryanuyujyate — kim ayaṃ pratyayāpekṣo niyama āhos vidālambanāpekṣa iti । kiṃ cātaḥ । ubhayathāpi doṣaḥ । pūrvaṃ niyamaṃ tāvad adhikṛty āha — tato 'rthād iti sarvaś ced iti । yadi tata ity ādyasyaiva vivaraṇam । <I,88> nanu vijñānavyapadeśahetor viṣayasya prakṛtatvāt tata ity anena prakṛtapratyavam arśinā sa eva pratyavamṛśyata ity asaṃśayam etat । tat kuta iyam āśaṅkā । yadi tata ity anena sarvaś caturvidho 'pi pratyaya ucyata iti nāyamātrārthaḥ, yas tvayā parikalpitaḥ, yasmād iha sarvadharmātmakatvād ālambanapratyaya eva sarvaśabdenoktaḥ ॥

[I,88,i]

kathaṃ punas tasya sarvadharmātmakatvam । ālambanaṃ sarvadharmā iti lakṣaṇāt । na cānyaḥ sarvadharmasvabhāvo vijñānasya pratyayo vyapadeśahetur asti, yas tata ity anenocyate । tasmād ālambanapratyaya eva sarvaśabdenokta iti veditavyam । tataś cāyam artho bhavati — yadi sarvadharmasvabhāvaḥ pratyaya ucyate, yady ālambanapratyaya ucyata iti yāvat । tena tad acodyam । yasyālambanapratyayasya sambandhitayā jñānaṃ vyapadiśyate, na tat tat eva bhavati, kiṃ tarhi pratyayāntarād api, caturbhiś cittacaittā hīti vacanāt । tad evaṃ pratyayaniyamapakṣe siddhāntavirodha udbhāvitaḥ ॥

[I,88,ii]

ālambananiyamam adhikṛtyāha — ālambanaṃ ced ityādi । atrātivyāpitā lakṣaṇasyoktā । viṣayamātram ity atra yā tadānīṃ san nihito rūpādivyaktiḥ, vijñānasyālambanatvena sā viṣayaśabdenocyate । mātraśabda ālambanāntaraṃ vyavacchinatti । smārtādijñānam api rūpādibhir vyapadiśyate rūpasmṛtiḥ, <I,89> āmlābhilāṣaḥ, agnyanumānam ity ālambanāntaranirapekṣaṃ ca । tatas tasyāpi pratyakṣatā syāt ॥

[I,89,i]

syād etat — anumeyaviṣayaṃ jñānaṃ nāgnimātrād utpadyate, api tu pakṣadharmatvasambandhajñānād api । tat kuto 'yaṃ prasaṅga ity āha — na hy agnyādijñānam ityādi । yady api tadarthāntarād api jāyate, tathāpi na tadarthāntaraṃ tenālambyate । tataś cālambanāntarānapekṣotpattitvāt kena tasya pratyakṣatvaṃ na syāt ॥

[I,89,ii]

nanu ca yena viṣayeṇa yaj jñānaṃ vyapadiśyate, yadi tat tato bhavati, na tu na bhavatīty eṣo 'py atra niyamo 'bhimataḥ । na ca smṛtyādīni yenālambanena vyapadiśyante tasmād utpadyante, tasyāsattvāt । naitad asti, pāramparyeṇāpi tata utpatter abhimatatvāt । anyathā katham idaṃ yujyate, yad uktaṃ vādavidhau — anumānajñānam apy anenaiva nirastam । dhūmajñānasambandhasmṛtibhyām apiśabdād agnito 'pi tad bhavatīty uktaṃ bhavati । tad etat kathaṃ yujyate, yadi vyapadeśahetoḥ pāramparyeṇāpy atra janakatvam abhimatam । anyathā yadi smṛtyādīnāṃ viṣayasya vyapadeśahetos tadānīm asattvād ajanakatvam, tad idam anumāno 'py ajanakatvaṃ samānam itīdaṃ vacanam ayujyamānaṃ syāt ॥

<I,90>

[I,90,i]

atha smṛtyādīnāṃ kalpitaṃ sāmānyaṃ viṣayo vyapadeśahetuḥ, tac ca saṃvṛtisattvād ajanakam । tato na teṣāṃ pratyakṣateti matam । atrāpy etad evottaram । tathā hy anumānasyāpi saṃvṛtisad evālambanam । tataś ca tad ayuktaṃ syāt, yad uktam — dhūmajñānasambandhasmṛtibhyām api hi tad bhavati, nāgnita eveti । tasmāt sthita evātivyāpitādoṣaḥ ॥

[I,90,ii]

iha dvaye vādino 'ntarjñeyavādino bāhyārthavādinaś ca । tatrāntarjñeyavādinām adṛṣṭatatvāvasthāyāṃ pramāṇaṃ prameyaṃ cāpariniṣpannam eva tattvataḥ । kevalaṃ bhrāntānāṃ yathādarśanam idaṃ mānameyavyavasthitidarśanam । etac ca prāg eva pratipāditam । bāhyārthavādinas tu paramārthata eva bāhyaṃ prameyaṃ tadviṣayaṃ ca pramāṇam icchati । tac ca yathā na yujyate, tathā pratipādayitum idānīm ālambanādhikāreṇa vicāram ārabdhum āha — rūpādiṣu tv ālambanārtho vaktavya iti । avaśyaṃ caitad evaṃ vijñeyam । ye hi manyante — vādavidhidūṣaṇapara evāyam ārabhya iti, teṣāṃ yad uktam — svasaṃvedyaṃ tv anirdeśyaṃ rūpam indriyagocara ity atra <I,91> gocarārtho vaktavyaḥ । kiṃ yadābhāsaṃ tatra jñānam utpadyate tathā tadgocara ityādi tulyaḥ paryanuyoga iti pratividheyam । tasmāt sāmānyenaiva bāhyārthāśrayiṇī pramāṇād vyavasthā na ghaṭata iti pratipādanaparo 'yam ārabhya iti veditavyam । tatrāpi bāhyārthavādiṣu balinaḥ svayūthyāḥ । teṣu nihateṣv atare nihatā eva bhavanti, jyeṣṭhamalla iva hinate tadanye mallā iti tair eva saha vicāraṃ karoti ॥

[I,91,i]

ālambanārtha ity ālambanaśabdasyārthaḥ । kiṃ yadābhāsam ity anena pratyekaṃ rūpādiparamāṇūnāṃ svarūpeṇāpratibhāsanāt samūhākāreṇa ca teṣu vijñānasya pratibhāsanād ābhāsārtham ālambanārthaṃ darśayati । atha yathetyādinā kāraṇārtham । yathā vidyamānā iti nīlādisvalakṣaṇena । anyābhāsasyāpīti samūhābhāsasyāpi । yady api svābhāsaṃ vijñānaṃ na janayati, tathāpīty apiśabdasyārthaḥ ॥

[I,91,ii]

sañcitālambanatvād iti samūhālambanatvāt sañcitaṃ sañcaya iti kṛtvā । sañcayaś ca samūhaḥ । sañcitālambanatvaṃ tu teṣāṃ samūhapratibhāsatvāt । atha vā sañcitatvālambanatvād iti । samūhābhāsatvād ity arthaḥ । ālambyate 'neneti karaṇaṃ kārakaṃ kṛtvābhāsa ālambanaśabdenoktaḥ । saṃvṛtisad evālambanam ity apratyakṣateti śeṣaḥ । saṃvṛtisadālambanatvaṃ tu samūhasyādravyasattvāt । anena yat saṃvṛti<I,92>sad ālambanam, na tat pratyakṣam, smṛtyādivat । tathā cendriyajñānam iti vyāpakaviruddhaṃ prasaṅgam āha ॥

[I,92,i]

nanu dravyasatām eva sa paramāṇūnām ākāraḥ । ta eva hi parasparānugṛhītās tathā pratibhāsanta ity anekākārārthavādinaḥ kadācid asiddhatām udbhāvayeyur ity āśāṅkyāha — kāmam ityādi । kāmam ity abhyupagame । nīlādyābhāseṣu vijñāneṣu tato 'rthād ity ato lakṣaṇāt pratyakṣatā syāt tvanmatena । kuta ity āha — tathā hītyādi । teṣv iti nīlādyābhāseṣu vijñāneṣu । tatsamudāye prajñaptisatyāpīti nīlādiparamāṇusamudāye । sa hi yady api prajñaptisan, tathāpi nīlapītādijñāneṣu dravyasadākāro labhyate tvad abhimatayā yuktyā । atha vā teṣv iti nīlādiparamāṇuṣu dravyasadākāro labhyate ॥

[I,92,ii]

dravyasaṅkhyādyākāreṣv api tu prāpnotīti । yadi paramāṇvākāratvāt samūhākārasya paramārthasattvam, dravyasaṅkhyādīnām api paramāṇvākāratvāt paramārthasattvaṃ syāt । tataś ca tadākāravijñānaṃ pratyakṣaṃ syāt । tatrāpi śakyata iyaṃ yuktir vaktum, yadāha — ta eva hītyādi ॥

[I,92,iii]

atha yathetyādi pakṣāntaropanyāsaḥ । evaṃ satītyādi । dravyādiṣu yaj jñānam, tasya pratyakṣatāyā aprasaṅga ity arthaḥ । kuta ity āha — tathā teṣām i<I,93>tyādi । tatheti ghaṭādirūpeṇa । teṣām iti dravyādīnām । na hi nīlādiparamāṇuvat tattvataḥ santi । taiś ca jñānaṃ vyapadiśyate ghaṭajñānaṃ dvitvajñānam iti । na ca tatas tad utpadyate, teṣāṃ tattvato 'sattvāt । ato na taj jñānasya pratyakṣatāprasaṅgaḥ । saṃvṛtisadālambanatvam apy asiddham । na hi svarūpeṇa paramāṇūnāmālambanatva indriyajñānasya saṃvṛtisad ālambanaṃ bhavati ॥

[I,93,i]

kas tarhi doṣa ity āha — evaṃ tv ityādi । na hītyādinātraivopapattim āha । yadi pratyekaṃ paramāṇuṣu jñānaṃ syāt, evaṃ saty ekaikena paramāṇunā tad vyapadiśyeta । tataś ca pratyekaṃ ca te jñānasya kāraṇam, pratyekaṃ ca tais tad vyapadiśyata iti tadālambanasya jñānasya pratyakṣatvaṃ labhyeta । na caivam । tasmād yasya tad vyapadiśyata ity etan na prāpnoti ॥

[I,93,ii]

atha matam — samudāyābhāsatvāt tasya vyapadiśyate । paramāṇavaś ca samudāyāvasthā eva parasparānugṛhītā hetavo jñānasya । tato yasya tad vyapadiśyate, tata evotpadyate iti siddhā pratyakṣatā nīlādijñānānām ity āha — pratyekaṃ cetyādi । samudāyāvasthāyām apy ekaikasyaiva kāraṇabhāvaḥ, na samudāyasyety arthaḥ । tataḥ sa eva prasaṅgo yasya tad vyapadiśyata ity etan na prāpnotīti ॥

<I,94>

{1.15}

[I,94,i]

yadābhāsaṃ na tat tasmād iti । samūhābhāsaṃ kasmān na syād ity āha — citālaṃbanaṃ hi pañcakam iti samūhābhāsam ity arthaḥ । karaṇaṃ kārakaṃ kṛtvābhāsa ālambaśabdenoktaḥ । yatas tat paramārtheneti paramāṇoḥ, na tasya vyapadiśyata iti, atad ābhāsatvena tasyānavadhāritvāt ॥

{1.16}

[I,94,ii]

artharūpaviviktam ityādi । sarvasya hi jñānasya viṣayeṇavyapadeśo dṛśyate rūpajñānaṃ śabdajñānam iti । viṣayarūpavyatirekeṇa tv aśakyaṃ tad vyapadeṣṭum ॥

[I,94,iii]

nanu ca jñānaṃ buddhir iti vināpi viṣayeṇa vyapadeśo dṛśyate । na, abhiprāyāparijñānāt । kaḥ punar atrābhiprāyaḥ । viṣayasya sambandhitayārtharūpaviviktaṃ na śakyam ākhyātum ity ayam abhiprāyaḥ । tathā hi yasyārthasya yaj jñānaṃ vyapadiśyate, yadi tata eva tad bhavatīty etad viṣayacintāprakṛtam eva । anyathā jñānam iti vyapadiśann eva katham evaṃ brūyāt । evaṃ tarhi viṣayarūpeṇavyapadeśo 'sya bhaviṣyaty āha — viṣayo 'sya ceti । sāmānyarūpeṇa rūpatvādinā vyapadiśyeta । sāmānyaṃ ca kalpitaṃ buddhyārūḍham eva nendriyaviṣayābhimate 'sti । tat kathaṃ tatra vyapadiṣṭe tad vyapadiṣṭaṃ bhavati । ato yena vyapadiśyata ity etan na sambhavatīti darśayan nāha — tasmān na vyapadiśyata iti ॥

<I,95>

[I,95,i]

nanu cāvyapadeśyam api vastu dṛśyavikalpyāv arthāv ekīkṛtyādhyavasitatad bhāvatayā vyavahartṛbhir vyapadiśyate । tvayāpy avaśyam etad abhyupeyam, anyathā vyavahārāyogāt । syād etad evam, yadi bāhyaṃ kiñcid dṛśyaṃ syāt । tac ca nāsti, ālambanalakṣaṇayogād ity aparihāra evāyam । nanu cāyam ukta evārthaḥ । tat kim arthaṃ punar ucyate । asti prayojanam । pūrvaṃ hi paramāṇūnāṃ paramāṇurūpam eva sarvasūkṣmam adhikṛtyocyate । prākteṣām eva dravyasatāṃ tadrūpam ity anekākārārthavādino matam āśaṅkya tasya dṛśyatām abhidheyatāṃ cābhyupetya doṣāntarābhidhitsayā pratyakṣatānujñātā । samprati saty api tasmiṃs tasyāpy adṛśyatvenānabhidheyatvāt kutaḥ pratyakṣateti pratipādanāyedam ucyate । kathaṃ punas tasyāpy adṛśyatvam । evaṃ manyate — sarvathā vā svākāravijñānajanakatvaṃ grāhyatvaṃ syāt kenacid vākāreṇa । yadi prathamavikalpaḥ, jñānasya sarvathārthasvabhāvatāpatter ajñānatvaprasaṅgaḥ । atha dvitīyaḥ, samanantarātītaṃ jñānamanyaviṣayasyāpi jñānasya grāhyaṃ syāt, yatas tasyāpi jñānatvādinā kenacid ākāreṇa svābhāsajñānajananam asty eveti । tasmād ayuktaṃ <I,96> grāhyalakṣaṇam । ataś ca sthitam etat — na bāhyārthāśrayā pramāṇādivyavasthā yujyata iti ॥

{1.17}

[I,96,i]

naiyāyikānāṃ tv iti । rūḍher anantaraṃ ca tanmatasyopakṣepād ākṣapādānām iti gamyate । indriyārthasan nikarṣotpannam ityādi ॥

[I,96,ii]

indriyāṇi ghrāṇarasanacakṣustvakśrotrāṇi । arthāḥ pañca gandhādayas tadāśrayāḥ karma sattādāyaś ca । teṣāṃ sannikarṣaḥ sanmandhaḥ ॥

[I,96,iii]

sa tu pañcavidhiḥ saṃyogaḥ saṃyuktasamavāyaḥ saṃyuktasamavetasamavāyaḥ samavāyaḥ samavetasamavāyāś ca । tatrendriyasya dravyeṇa saṃyogalakṣaṇaḥ sanbandhaḥ, na rūpādibhiḥ । anyathobhayāśrayatvāt saṃyogasya te 'pi guṇavantaḥ syuḥ । nirguṇaś ca guṇāḥ । tasmād indriyasaṃyogād dravye jñānam utpadyate, yadātmā manasā saṃyujyate, mana indriyeṇa, indriyam arthena । dravyamātrārhe 'bhipretaḥ । dravyasamaveteṣu tu rūpādiṣu guṇeṣu tathā dravyatvādiṣu sāmānyaviśeṣeṣu karmaṇi ca <I,97> saṃyuktasamavāyāt । rūpatvādiṣu saṃyuktasamavetasamavāyāt । tathā guṇatvakarmatvayoḥ । śabde tu samavāyāt । sa hi śravaṇaśaṣkulīparicchinadharmābhisaṃskṛtākāśadeśalakṣaṇe śretrendriye samaveto gṛhyate । yas tu śrotrādivicchinn deśa utpadyate, sa tatrāsamavetatvān na gṛhyanta eva । tena tu śabdāntarāṇi sarvadikkāny ārabhyante, tair apy anyāni । evaṃ śabdāntarārabdhaśabdaparamparayā śrotrendriye yaḥ samavaiti śabdaḥ, tasyendriyasamavāyād grahaṇaṃ bhavati, yadātmā manasā saṃyujyate, mano 'pi śrotreṇa । śabdajātau tu samavetasamavāyāt । sattāyāṃ tu dravyasamavetāyāṃ saṃyuktasamavāyāt, guṇakarmasamavetāyāṃ saṃyuktasamavetasamavāyāt, śabdasamavetāyāṃ tu samavetasamavāyād iti । tad evaṃ pañcaprakāraḥ sambandho jñānahetuḥ ॥

[I,97,i]

tasmād utpannaṃ nābhivyaktaṃ jñānaṃ pratyakṣam । jñānagrahaṇaṃ sukhādivyavacchedārtham ॥

[I,97,ii]

vyapadiśyate jñāpyate saṃyogyādinā liṅgeneti vyapadeśyo viṣayaḥ । nāsya vyapadeśyo viṣayo 'stīty avyapadeśyam । atha vā tad eva jñānaṃ svarūpeṇa na vyapadiśyate na nirdiśyata ity avyapadeśyam ॥

<I,98>

[I,98,i]

mṛgatṛṣṇādir viṣayo vyabhicārī, yathā jalādirūpatvena gṛhyate, tathāsattvāt । nāsya vyabhicāryastīty avyabhicāri । atha vā tad eva jñānamat asmiṃs tadgrahād vyabhicāri ॥

[I,98,ii]

vyavasāya ātmāsyeti vyavasāyātmakam । ātmaśabdaḥ svabhāvavacanaḥ kāryavacano vā ॥

[I,98,iii]

indriyārthodbhava iti । udbhavaty asmād ity udbhavaḥ । indriyārthāv udbhavo 'syeti vigrahaḥ । indriyārthagrahaṇaṃ tat sannikarṣopalakṣanārtham । nāsti vyapadeśyādisambhava iti । ādigrahaṇād vyabhicāritvasya vyavasāyātmakatvasya ca ॥

[I,98,iv]

yadi nāsti, kim iti viśeṣaṇam ayuktam ity āha — viśeṣaṇārtham । nāsti vyapadeśyādisambhava iti । ādigrahaṇād vyabhicāritvasya vyavasāyātmakatvasya ca ॥

[I,98,v]

yadi nāsti, kim iti viśeṣaṇam ayuktam ity āha — viśeṣaṇaṃ hītyādi । yady avyapadeśyādisvabhāvam itarasvabhāvaṃ cendriyasannikarṣajaṃ jñānaṃ syāt, tata idaṃ viśeṣaṇatrayaṃ yujyate । iha cāvyapadeśyam avyabhicārīti ca viśeṣaṇadvayaṃ sambhavaty eva, na vyabhiccarati । vyavasāyātmakatvaṃ tu na sambhavaty eva । tad eva ca viśeṣaṇaṃ bhavati, yat tasminn āśraye bhavati taṃ ca vyabhicarati, tatrāsattvāt, yathā nīlatvam itpalasya ॥

[I,98,vi]

na cāstīndriyabudddher iti । yadā bahuvrīhipakṣaḥ, tadevam uktam । anena vyapadeśyatvasyāsambhavenāvyapadeśyatvasyāvyabhicāraṃ darśayati । kasmān nāstīty āha — <I,99> anumānaviṣayatvād ityādi । vyapadeśyaṃ hi sāmānyam, na svalakṣaṇam, tasya pūrvam adṛṣṭatvāt । tac ca sāmānyam anumānasyaiva viṣayaḥ, dhūmādibhiḥ pūrvadṛṣṭasāmānyenāgnyādi anumānāt, na pratyakṣasya, tasyāsādhāraṇaviṣayatvāt ॥

[I,99,i]

athāpi syāt — yadi viṣayo na vyapadiśyate, na nāma । jñānaṃ tu vyapadiśyate । tad asti vyapadeśyam । tataś ca vyabhicārād yuktam avyapadeśyatvaṃ viśeṣaṇam । iha ca tad eva jñānam, svarūpeṇa yan na nirdiśyate । tad avyapadeśyam uktam ity āha — anirdeśyatve cāvyabhicāra iti । kasmād ity āha — na hīndriyabuddhir ityādi । anirdeśyasvarūpam eva hi sarvaṃ jñānam । naivānirdeśyatve vyabhicāro 'sti । atha sāmānyarūpeṇāpi yan na nirdiśyate, tad avyapadeśyam । evam apy asambhavaḥ syāt । sarvam eva hi jñānaṃ, sāmānyarūpeṇa vyapadiśyate । tad anena tat puruṣapakṣe 'pi doṣa uktaḥ ॥

[I,99,ii]

pakṣilas tv āha — jñānasya samākhyāśabdo nāsti, yena pratīyamānaṃ vyavahārāya kalpate, anyatretikaraṇayuktād viṣayasaṃśabdanād rūpam iti jñānam, rasa iti jñānam iti । tadā ca vyapadiśyamānaṃ śābdaṃ bhavati । tato vyavacchedārtham avyapadeśyam ity āha । arthagrahaṇakāle tu samākhyāśabdo na vyāpriyate, tadā tasyāvyapadeśyatvam iti । tasyāpy etad evottaram — anirdeśyatve cāvyabhicāra iti, vyavahārakāle 'pi jñānasvarūpasya vyapadeṣṭum aśakyatvāt । so 'pi <I,100> hi tāvad viṣayaḥ svarūpeṇa vyapadeṣṭum aśakyaḥ । kutaḥ punas tenānyo vyapadekṣyate । na ca vyapadeśācchābdatvaṃ prasajyate, kiṃ tarhi vācyatvam ity asamīkṣitābhidhānam etat ॥

[I,100,i]

na ca vyabhicāriviṣayatve, sambhavo 'stīty anuvartate, manobhrāntiviṣayatvād ityādi । vyabhicāro 'tathābhāvaḥ । yathāsāv upalabhyate, tathā tasyāsattvam, yathā marīcikāder viṣayasya । sa ca yatra jñāne svarūpeṇa pratibhāsate, tad apekṣayā vyabhicāritvam । bhrānte ca manovijñāne sa tathā pratibhāsate । tathā hy anudakādisvabhāvam api bhūtasaṅghātam udakādirūpeṇādhyavasyanty upajāyate manobhrāntiḥ । tatas tat kalpitatvāt tasyā eva sa viṣayaḥ, nendriyajñānasya । tato na tadvyavacchedārtham avyabhicārigrahaṇaṃ kartavyam ॥

[I,100,ii]

nanv asati tasminn akṣopaghātajaṃ yad vyabhicāriviṣayaṃ dvicandrādijñānam, tasyāpi pratyakṣatā syāt । tatas tan nirāsāya tad avaśyaṃ kartavyam । naitad asti, arthasannikarṣagrahaṇenaiva tasya pratipakṣepāt । anyathendriyajam ity evaṃ vācyaṃ syāt, na tv indriyārthasannikarṣotpannam iti, tasya vyavacchedyābhāvāt । idaṃ bahuvrīhim ahikṛtyoktam ॥

<I,101>

[I,101,i]

yadā tu tad eva jñānaṃ svayam avyabhicārīti tat puruṣaḥ parair ākṣīyate, tadaivaṃ vaktavyam — avyabhicāritvāt । dvicandrādijñānaṃ tu sannikarṣodiṅmātradarśanenaiva pūrvānusāreṇa gamyata iti kṛtvā ॥

[I,101,ii]

vyavasāyo 'pi hītyādinā viśeṣaṇasyāsambhavam āha । no vikalpyeti । niścayo hy evaṃrūpaḥ — gaurevāyam, nāśva iti । sa ca yāvad gotvādisāmānyaṃ na vikalpayati tena ca tadvantaṃ na yojayati, tāvan nopajāyata eva । na ca ghrāṇādijñānavad ity asambhavo viśeṣaṇasya । nirvikalpayann api cakṣuṣā rūpam īkṣate । na ca vikalpadvayaṃ yugapad abhyupeyate saṃvedyate veti kuto 'siddhiḥ ॥

[I,101,iii]

athetyādi । ayathārthaṃ jñānaṃ mithyājñānam । ādiśabdena saṃśayajñānaṃ gṛhyate । tasyāyathārthādijñānasya nivṛttasya — vyavasāyātmakam ity ucyate । etad darśayati । nātra vyavasāyaśabdo niścayaparyāyaḥ, kiṃ tarhi bhūtārthagrahaṇaparyāyaḥ । vyavasāyātmakam iti bhūtārthagrahaṇasvabhāvam ity arthaḥ । kasmād ayuktaṃ viśeṣaṇam ity āha — avyabhicārāc ceti । caśabdād asambhavāc cendriyabuddhāv aya<I,102>thārthatvasya । kutaḥ punar asambhava ity āha — sarvā hītyādi । mātraśabdo 'yathārthagrahaṇanirāsārthaḥ । svārthagrahaṇamātreṇāsambhavaṃ darśayati । ayathārthatvaṃ hi yan nivartayitum iṣyate, tad indriyajñāne na sambhavaty eva । indriyabuddhir iti ca yady api sāmānyaśabdaḥ, tathāpi prakaraṇād indriyārthasannikarṣotpannāyām eva vartate ॥

[I,102,i]

avyabhicārād ity anenaitad darśayati — yady api mūḍhaḥ sambhavaḥ manyate, tathāpi tat pūrvam  eva nirākṛtam avyabhicārīty anena viśeṣaṇena । tat kim etena vyavasāyātmakavacaneneti । atha vā na kevalam asambhavān na yuktam, kiṃ tv avyabhicārāc ca । tam avyabhicāraṃ darśayati sarvā hītyādinā । kvacic caśabdo na paṭhyate । tatrārthaḥ — kathaṃ tathāpy ayuktaṃ viśeṣaṇam ity āha — avyabhicārād iti । indriyabuddher yathārthatvasyāvyabhicārād ity arthaḥ । katham avyabhicāra ity āha — sarvā hīyādi ॥

[I,102,ii]

nanu ca vyavasāyātmakam ity atra kāryaparyāya ātmaśabdaḥ । tataś ca yathoktadoṣābhāva ity āha — etenetyādi । prayuktaḥ pratikṣiptaḥ । vyavasāyakāryam iti । vyavasāyaḥ kāryam asyeti vigrahaḥ । kathaṃ prayuktam ity āha — na hy astītyādi । indriyabuddhyantaraṃ hi sāmānyākāreṇārtho buddhau sanniviśate । <I,103> tathā tatrāsanniviṣṭasya nāmajātyādiyojanā na sambhavati । tad antaraṃ kim etad ity abhyūhavikalpaḥ । tataḥ pūrvānubhūtānusāreṇānusmaraṇavikalpaḥ । tadanantaraṃ nirūpaṇavikalpo niścayātmako bhavati । tad yadi vyavasāyaḥ kāryaṃ yasya tajjñānam indriyārthasannikarṣotpannam iṣyate, evaṃ sati pūrvānubhūtasmaraṇāntaraṃ niścayajñānaṃ bhavatīty anusmaraṇajñānam indriyārthasannikarṣajaṃ prāpnoti । sākṣād grahaṇaṃ viprakṛṣṭāyathārthajñānakāryasya vyavacchedyatve pratyakṣābhāvaprasaṅgāt ॥

[I,103,i]

tad anena prapañcana yasya yatra vyabhicāraḥ sambhavaś ca nāsti, na tat tasya viśeṣaṇam । tad yathā balākāyāḥ śuklatvaṃ kṛṣṇatvaṃ ca । nāsti cāvyapadeśyatvāder indriyajñāne yathāyogyaṃ vyabhicāraḥ sambhavaś ceti vyāpakābhāvaṃ darśayati । kaḥ punar ayaṃ vyabhicāro nāma । yadi tato 'nyatrabhāvaḥ, evaṃ sati nīlatvaṃ bhramarasya niśeṣaṃ syād avyapadeśyatvaṃ ca jñānasya, dāhaduḥkhādāv api bhāvāt । atha tatrābhāvaḥ, evam api prayatnānantarīyake tan nāsti, yato vyabhicāraḥ sādhyasya syāt । prayatnānantarīyakatvam eva tu kvacid anitye nāstīti tasyaiva syād vyabhicāraḥ । naiṣa doṣaḥ । anekadhā hi vyabhicāraśabdasyārthaḥ । kvacid anyathā bhāvo vyabhicārī viṣaya iti, kvacid anyatrabhāvo vyabhicārī hetur iti, kvacit tatrābhāvo vyabhicāri viśeṣaṇam ityādikaḥ । iha tu tatrābhāvo 'bhimataḥ ॥

<I,104>

[I,104,i]

athāpītyādi । anenaitad darśayati — nāniṣṭanivṛttaye 'vyapadeśyādigrahaṇam, kiṃ tu pramāṇādīnāṃ svabhāvaparijñānān niḥśreyasaprāptiḥ, atas tat svabhāvapradarśanāya । tasmāt siddhasādhanam iti । tan netyādinaitad āha — pratyakṣalakṣaṇe vivakṣite ko 'vasaro jñānasvabhāvapradarśanasyeti । tatraitat syāt — tad eva pratyakṣalakṣaṇaṃ na śakyate vaktuṃ vinā tatsvabhāvapradarśanenety āha - tasya cetyādi । lakṣaṇaṃ hi nāma yad arthāntaravyāvṛttena rūpeṇa lakṣyaṃ gamayati । tac ca lakṣyam indriyārthasannikarṣotpannam ity anenaiva siddham iti vṛkṣā svabhāvakathanam । anena hetur āviṣkṛtaḥ । atha niṣprayojanasyāpi nirdeśaḥ kriyate, evaṃ saty atiprasaṅga iti darśayann āha — jñānasvabhāvanirdeśyatve cetyādi । anena dṛṣṭāntaḥ । yasya pratyakṣalakṣaṇaṃ pratyupayogo nāsti, na tat tad adhikāre nirdeśyam, guṇatvādivat । nāsti ca pratyakṣalakṣaṇaṃ pratyupayogo 'vyapadeśyatvādeḥ । vyāpakābhāvaḥ ॥

[I,104,ii]

yas tu manyate — naivendriyārthasannikarṣajasya pratyakṣasyāvyapadeśyatvādiviśeṣaṇam, kiṃ tarhi pratyakṣadvayam evaitat parasparāsaṅkīrṇarūpam ekena sūtreṇa lakṣyate । avyapadeśyam avyabhicāri vyavasāyātmakam ity anena hi sūtraikadeśena <I,105> mānasaṃ lakṣyate । indriyārthasannikarṣotpannam ity anena tv indriyārthasannikarṣajam । tataś cendriyārthodbhave nāstītyādi yad uktam, tat sūtrārthāparijñānavijṛmbhitam ॥

[I,105,i]

ata eva so 'py adoṣo na sukhādi prameyaṃ veti, ya ukto 'nantaro 'pi hetur asiddha iti, tena manasa indriyatvaṃ vaktavyaṃ pratyakṣavyapadeśaprasiddhyartham । kiṃ cāvyapadeśyam avyabhicāri vyavasāyātmakam ity etāval lakṣaṇam astu । anenaiva pūrvasyāpi pratyakṣaṇavaiyarthyaprasaṅgaḥ ॥

[I,105,ii]

sarvatra cetyādinā lakṣaṇasyāvyāpitām āha, yataś cakṣuḥ śrotravijñānayor api pratyakṣateṣṭā tayoś ca sannikarṣotpattyyasambhavaḥ । tam asambhavaṃ darśayann āha — sāntaragrahaṇam ityādi । sāntaragrahaṇaṃ vicchinna iti grahaṇam । adhikagrahaṇam indriyātiriktagrahaṇam । tan na syāt । kuta ity āha — na hītyādi । etena yad indriyeṇa nirantaram, na tad indriyāt sāntaram iti gṛhyate, nāpy adhikam iti, gandhādivat । tathā ca rūpaśadāv iti viruddhavyāptaṃ prasaṅgam āha । asti ca tat tathāvidhaṃ grahaṇam । tathā hīndriyaparimāṇātiriktasvarūpā vicchinnā iti <I,106> ca śailādayaḥ śabdāś ca gṛhyanta iti prasiddham etat । prāptigrahaṇe tu sati yāvatā bhāgena prāptiḥ, tāvateva grahaṇaṃ syāt । avicchinnā iti gṛhyeran । rūpagrahaṇaṃ cātra cakṣurviṣayopalakṣaṇārtham । yo yataḥ sāntara iti gṛhyate, na tasya tena saha nairantaryam । tad yathā pārasyāpareṇa । svagrāhakād indriyāt sāntarāv iti ca gṛhyete rūpaśabdāv iti prasaṅgaviparyayeṇa vyāpakaviruddhadvayam etat । itiśabdopānānam asiddhatāparihārāya ॥

[I,106,i]

nanu cendriyam atīndriyam । tat kathaṃ tad apekṣayā kiñcit sāntaram iti gṛhyetādhikam iti vā । na ca rūpādīnāṃ parimāṇam asti, nirguṇatvād guṇānām । tat kutas teṣām ādhikyagrahaṇam । na ca paro gandhādibhiḥ sahendriyasya nairantaryam icchati, tais tasya saṃyogābhāvāt । tat katham idaṃ yuktam — na hīndriyanirantare gandhādāv ityādi । yatra dravye gandhādayaḥ samavetāḥ, tad dravyam atrendriyanirantaraṃ jñeyam, tena sahendriyasya saṃyogāt । tad dvāreṇa ca gandhadīnām api <I,107> nairantaryam । asti ca saṃyuktasamavāyalakṣaṇam ity adoṣaḥ ॥

[I,107,i]

yat tūktam — nanu cendriyam atīndriyam ityādi, tatra yadīndriyāpekṣayā na tathā rūpaśabdau gṛhyete, kim apekṣayā tarhi vaktavyam । adhiṣṭhānāpekṣayeti cet, evaṃ tarhi yadi rūpaśabdāv adhiṣṭhānād vicchinnāv ity adhikāv iti ca gṛhyete, tadabahirvartina indriyād api tau tathaiva gṛhyete yo yato vicchinna ity adhika iti ca gṛhyate, sa tadabahirvartino 'pi vastunas tathaiva gṛhyate । tad yathā ghaṭād vicchinna ity adhika iti ca gṛhyamāṇaḥ parvato ghaṭābahirvartino 'py udakādes tathaiva gṛhyate । indriyādhiṣṭhānād vicchinnāv ity adhikāv iti ca gṛhyete vivādāspadībhūtau rūpaśabdau । svabhāvaḥ ॥

[I,107,ii]

yad apy uktam — na ca rūpādīnām ityādi, tatra yadi rūpādīnāṃ parimāṇaṃ nāsti, kathaṃ tarhy alpaṃ rūpaṃ mahadrūpam iti gṛhyate । upacārād iti cet, syād etat — rūpādayo yatra samavetāḥ, taddravyam aṇu mahad vā । taddvāreṇa rūpāder ādhikyādyaupacārikam iti । astu yathā tathā, tena tu bhāktenāpi gandhādivad rūpāder apy adhikam iti grahaṇaṃ na prāpnotīty etāvad ucyate । api ca tulyapratyayaparicchedyatvādaupacārikatvam evāyuktam । yādṛśo hi dravye mahad dravyam alpaṃ veti pratyayaḥ, <I,108> tadaviśiṣṭo rūpādiṣu mahad rūpam alpaṃ veti । na ca mukhyopacaritayos tulyapratyayaparicchedyatvam । na hi yādṛśena pratyayena mukhyo gauḥ paricchidyate, tādṛśenaivopacārito vāhīkaḥ । yadi vāśrayadvāreṇa guṇā guṇavantaḥ pratīyante, sarvaḥ śabdo mahānityeva pratīyate, tadāśrayasya nabhaso mahāparimāṇatvāt । tataś ca hastimaśakādiśabdānāṃ parimāṇabhedapratītir na syāt । tasmāc ca te 'pi guṇavanto 'bhyupeyāḥ, na vā dravyam apīti ॥

{1.18}

[I,108,i]

bahirvṛttitvād ityādinā hetvor asiddham āha । tathā hy adhiṣṭhānābahirvṛttitvam āśritya sāntarādhikagrahaṇayor hetvoḥ siddhir abhisaṃhitā । bahirvṛttitve tu sā nopapadyate । yasmād indriyaṃ bahirnirgatya visargatya visarpadviṣayeṇa saṃyuktaṃ tam adhiṣṭhānād adhikam avabhāsayati pradīpālokavat, tasmād upapadyate tadviṣayasya sāntarādhikagrahaṇam, adhiṣṭhānān nendriyād iti bhāvaḥ ॥

[I,108,ii]

atra codyate — cakṣuṣastaijasatvādraśmayo nirgatyārthaṃ prakāśayantīty abhyupagamād uktaṃ bahirvṛttitvam āśaṅkitum । śrotraṃ tu śravaṇaśaṣkulīparicchinna ākāśapradeśaviśeṣaḥ । tasya naiva paro bahirvṛttitvam icchati । tat kathaṃ tasya tadāśaṅkitam iti । evaṃ manyate — pradeśavat tvam ākāśasya bhāktam । paramārthatas tu <I,109> tan niravayavam eva । yathoktayā nītyā bhāktapakṣe yad abahirvṛttitvaṃ tatra doṣa ukte 'gatyā paramārthapakṣasamāśrayeṇa bahirvṛttitvaṃ kadācit paraḥ kalapayed iti । tasmād yuktam āśaṅkitum । tatra cikitsādiprayogād ity upapattiḥ ॥

[I,109,i]

nanu pādābhyaṅgādir adhiṣṭhānād anyatrāpi cakṣurādeḥ kriyate । tato nāyam ekānto yatra cikitsāprayogaḥ, tatrendriyam iti । naitad asti, tatrāpi dhātrīcikitsādvāreṇa kumārakasyeva cakṣurāder adhiṣṭhānasthasyaiva naḍīsañcāreṇa cikitsāprayogāt । anyathā tatrāsannihitaṃ tena sambandhaman anubhavat kathaṃ cikitsyeta । atha cikitsākāle pādādau sannihitam, evaṃ sati pādāde rūpagrahaṇaprasaṅgaḥ । tasmāt svādhiṣṭhānastham eva yathoktena prakāreṇa cikitsyata ity abhyupeyam । tad etad uktaṃ bhavati । yad indriyaṃ svādhiṣṭhāne cikitsyate, tat tatraiva vartate, ghrāṇādivat । svādhiṣṭhāne ca cikitsyete cakṣuḥśrotre iti svabhāvaḥ ॥

[I,109,ii]

ata indriyād eveti । nipāto bhinnakramaḥ । vicchinnaḥ evety evaṃ drṣṭavyam । kiṃ kāraṇam । yato 'dhiṣṭhānād api vicchinne 'rtha iti gṛhyate, na kevalam indriyāt । adhiṣṭhānadvāreṇaiva hīndriyād arthasya sāntaragrahaṇaṃ pratīyate, yathoktaṃ prāk ॥

<I,110>

[I,110,i]

doṣāntaraṃ vaktukāmo bahirnirgatim abhyupety āha — saty api cetyādi । anyathetyādinā bahirnirgatasya viṣayopalambhāsāmarthye hetum āha । yasyendriyasyādhiṣṭhānapidhāne viṣayagrahaṇaṃ nāsti, tasya bahirnirgatasyāpratibaddhaṃ viṣayagrahaṇasāmarthyaṃ nāsti, tvagādīndriyavat । nāsti ca svādhiṣṭhānapidhāne cakṣuḥśrotrayor viṣayagrahaṇam । kāyābhāvaḥ ॥

[I,110,ii]

nanu cakṣuṣaḥ prabhāvalakṣaṇā vṛttir adhiṣṭhānapidhāne vinaśyati, adhiṣṭhānapidhānakāle tatraivāśu praviśati vā । tato 'yam adoṣaḥ । apihitādhiṣṭhānam eva hi tadviṣayagrahaṇasamartham, nānyatheti । śrotrendriyaṃ prati tāvad ayam asamādhiḥ, tasyādhiṣṭhānapidhāne 'pi bahirvṛttitvān nityatvāc ca । cakṣuḥ prati yadi nāmāyaṃ parihāra iti pratyāśā syāt, sāpi tyajyatām, yataś cakṣuṣa ātmabhūtaḥ prabhāvayavī nirgatya sarvātmanā viṣayeṇa samprayuktatvāt tatraiva sannihito nādhiṣṭhāne, tadavyatiriktatvāc cakṣur api । na hi tasyāvayavāḥ santi, yato bhāgenādhiṣṭhāne 'pi varteta । tataś ca tadānīṃ tadadhiṣṭhānābhimataḥ śarīrāvayavastasyādhiṣṭhānaṃ na bhavaty evāsambandhāt, indriyāntaravad iti prasaṅgo vā । atha sāvayavaḥ prabhāvayavī <I,111> kalpyate, evam api yas tasya pradeśo viṣayeṇa samprayukto jñānopajananahetuḥ, tatra sa eva doṣaḥ । athārthāntaratvaṃ tasya cakṣurindriyādiṣyate, sa eva tarhi cakṣū rūpadarśanasāmarthyāt tallakṣaṇatvāc ca cakṣuṣaḥ । tatrāpi ca sāvayavatvaniravayavatvapakṣayoḥ sa doṣas tadavastha eveti yat kiñcid etat ॥

[I,111,i]

pañcānāṃ cendriyatva iti, ghrāṇarasanacakṣustvakśrotrāṇīndriyāṇīti sūtrāt । na sukhādi prameyaṃ veti lakṣaṇanyūnatām āha, sukhādijñānasya pratyakṣalakṣaṇenāsaṅgrahāt । tataś ca sukhādīnāṃ prameyatvābhyupagamavirodhaḥ । tatraitat syāt — yady api sukhādi pratyakṣaviṣayo na bhavati, tathāpy anumānādiviṣayatvāt prameyaṃ bhaviṣyatīti । ata āha — yad dhītyādi । svagrahaṇaṃ parakīyeṣu mukhaprasādādiliṅgasya sulabhatvāt । sveṣu tu yadā liṅgābhāvān nānumānam, sādṛśyābhāvān nopamānam, upadeśābhāvān nāgamaḥ, indriyārthasannikarṣābhāvān na pratyakṣam, tathā kathaṃ teṣāṃ prameyatā । athāyaṃ neṣyate doṣaḥ, evaṃ tarhi sukhādijñānaṃ pañcamaṃ pramāṇam upasaṅkhyeyam iti darśayann āha — tasya veti । tathāpi pramāṇacatuṣṭvābhyupagamabādhā ॥

<I,112>

[I,112,i]

mano vāstv indriyāntaram iti । yady eṣa doṣo neṣyata ity abhiprāyaḥ । evam api pañcendriyābhyupagamavyāghātaḥ ॥

{1.19}

[I,112,ii]

aniṣedhād ity aneneṣṭam eva śāstre mana indriyatveneti darśayati । asti hy ekeṣām iti sāṅkhyādīnām ॥

[I,112,iii]

anyendriyarutaṃ vṛtheti । ghrāṇādīnām apīndriyatvasya tata eva siddhatvāt tadvacanavaiyarutaṃ syāt । tasmāt punar vacanād avasīyate — anyeṣām indriyatvaṃ nābhimatam iti । kecid āhuḥ — ghrāṇarasanacakṣustvakśrotrāṇīndriyāṇi bhūtebhya iti naivātra ghrāṇādīnām indriyatvaṃ vidhīyate, kiṃ tarhīndriyatvena prasiddhānām eva bhaitikatvam । abhaitikaṃ ca manaḥ । tasmān na nirdiśyata iti । etac ca na । anyendriyasaṅkhyāsvabhāvanirākaraṇād ghrāṇādīti bhūtebhya iti ca bhaitikatvasiddher indriyagrahaṇānarthakyaṃ syāt ॥

[I,112,iv]

jñānasya cetyādi । indriyasannikarṣayoḥ pramāṇatve na syāt phalābhāvaḥ, jñānasya, phalatvāt । jñānād anarthāntaraphalavādinaś ca yathā svamate darśitam iti manyate । niścayātmakaṃ hītyādi । yasyāniścayātamakaṃ pramāṇam iṣṭam, tasya niścayaḥ phalam arthāntaraṃ syāt । na tu vyavāniścayātmakaṃ pramāṇam icchato 'nyat phalaṃ bhavati । nanu ca niścayajñānam anekajñānāntaritād anusmaraṇavikalpād anantaraṃ bhavati, yathoktaṃ prāk । na ca vyavahitasya phalatvaṃ yuktam, anyathātiprasaṅgaḥ <I,113> syāt । tat kutas tasya phalatā । satyam, tathāpi yasyāniścayātmakaṃ pramāṇam iṣṭam, tasya sthūladarśitayā niścayo 'rthāntaraṃ phalaṃ syād iti kalpanāpi tāvat sambhavet । yasya tu vyavasāyātmakam eva pratyakṣam iṣṭam, tasya kalpanāpy eṣā na sambhavatīti darśanārtham evam uktam । tad evam arthāntaraphalābhyupagamavyāghātaḥ ॥

[I,113,i]

viśeṣaṇajñānam ityādinā yady api niścayātmakatvenābhedaḥ, tathāpi viṣayabhedena jñānabhedāt pramāṇāt phalasya bhedaṃ darśayati । bhinnatvān na viśeṣeṇa ityāder ayam arthaḥ — yady ato 'nyaviṣayaṃ karaṇam, na tasya tatra phalaṃ bhavati । tad yathā palāśād anyaviṣayasya cchedanasya palāśe । viśeṣyād anyaviṣayaṃ ca viśeṣaṇajñānaṃ karaṇam iti vyāpakaviruddhaḥ । anyaviṣayasya pramāṇasyeti hetuḥ । pramāṇasyeti caitat karaṇatvopalakṣaṇam । na cānyatra phalaṃ yuktam iti pramāṇaphalam । na hy anyaviṣayasyetyādivyārptiḥ । yathetyādir dṛṣṭāntaḥ ॥

[I,113,ii]

viśeṣyajñāhetutvād ity asiddhatām āha । evaṃ manyate — yathā cchedanaṃ khadirād icchadānimittatvāt khadirādiviṣayam, evaṃ viśeṣaṇajñānaṃ viśeṣyajñānani<I,114>mittatvād viśeṣyaviṣayam iti । viśeṣyajñānanimittatvaṃ tasya, tadabhāve tadabhāvāt । nātiprasaṅgād iti ॥

[I,114,i]

yaś ca pramātā kartā, yac ca gavādi karma pramīyate, yatra ca deśe 'dhikaraṇe, yasmāc cāpāyād apādānāt, yasmai ca dātum, tac ca sampradānam, etad api sarvaṃ viśeṣyajñānahetutvād viśeṣaṇajñānavat karaṇaṃ prasajyata ity arthaḥ । tasmād ityādi । iha dvau tacchabdau । tatra dvitīyasya sambandhī yac chabdo yasyeti ṣaṣṭhyantaḥ śrūyamāṇo 'py anumīyate । yathā gatibuddhipratyavasānārthaśabdakarmākarmakāṇām aṇikartā sa ṇāvit yatra । sa ca karmaṇīty anena sāmānādhikaraṇye vyākhyeyaḥ । tenāyam artho bhavati — yasyaiva jñānasya yatra karmaṇi jñeye vyāpārakhyātiḥ kārakāntarāvyavahitasya vyāpārapratītiḥ, tasyaiva karmaṇo jñeyasya tajjñānaṃ pramāṇam iti । iha ca viśeṣaṇajñānasyaiva vyāpārakhyātiḥ, tadākārotpattyā । anyathā <I,115> viśeṣaṇajñānam eva tan na syāt । tasmāt tasyaiva viśeṣaṇasya tat pramāṇam, na viśeṣyasya, tatra tadvyāpārāprathanāt ॥

[I,115,i]

nanu ca pramāṇaṃ karaṇaṃ kārakam । kriyāyāś ca kārakāṇi bhavanti, na kārakāntarasya । tat kathaṃ tasyaiva karmaṇas tat pramāṇam ity ucyate । naiṣa doṣaḥ । naiveyaṃ sambandhalakṣaṇā ṣaṣṭhī, kiṃ tarhi kṛdyogalakṣaṇā yathā palāśānāṃ śātana iti । ayam arthaḥ — tasyaiva viśeṣaṇasya tat pramāṇam । tad eva tena pramīyate, na viśeṣyam iti । tasmāt siddhaṃ bhinnaviṣayatvam ॥

{1.20}

[I,115,ii]

tatra cetyādi । nanu ca viśeṣaṇe 'dhigantavye viśeṣyajñānasya phalatvam uktam । tat kim ucyate phalābhāva iti । naiṣa doṣaḥ । caśabdo 'vadhāraṇārthaḥ । tatraiva viśeṣaṇa evādhigantavya ity arthaḥ । yadā mandāloke dośe viśeṣaṇam eva kevalaṃ gavādimātraṃ paricchidyate na vyaktiviśeṣaḥ, tatra saṃśayād gavādimātrasya ca sāmānyarūpatvāt tasya ca viśeṣaṇāntarābhāvāt, na sāmānyasya viśeṣaṇaṃ sambhavati, tadā viśeṣaṇajñānasya pramāṇatvaṃ vā syāt phalatvaṃ vā । anyatarābhyupagame 'nyatarasya hānir ity abhyupetabādhā ॥

<I,116>

[I,116,i]

dvayaṃ tac ced iti tat parihāraḥ । atra caikasyobhayarūpavirodhaparihārāya tad yathetyādidṛṣṭāntaḥ । yogināṃ hi yoganiṣpattāv ātmānaṃ paśyatāṃ sa grāhyaś ca bhavati grahītā ca । arthāntaraphalavādin idam aniṣṭam evaṃ sati prasajyata ity āha — yady arthāntare 'pītyādi । svādhigame tu jñānasyetyādyanenaitad darśayati — ātmadṛṣṭāntena nārthāntare prameye viśeṣaṇajñānam ubhayathā sidhyati, dṛṣṭāntadārṛṣṭāntikayor vaiṣamyāt, kiṃ tu svādhigama eva jñāsyobhayabhāvaḥ । svādhigame ca jñānam ubhayathā pramāṇaṃ prameyaṃ ca mayeṣyata eva, tac ca tvayātmanidarśanena samarthitam iti ॥

[I,116,ii]

evaṃ tarhītyādinā yathā pradīpasyāndhakāranivṛttiḥ phalam arthāntaram, evam jñānādinivṛttiḥ phalaṃ bhaviṣyatīti darśayati । viṣayabhedo 'py atra nāstīty upanyāsaḥ । na sarvatreti phalavyavasthānasyāvyāpitvam āha । kuta etat — na sarvatrety āha — kvacid ityādi । ābhogamātreṇa jñānam utpadyate, na tatra tasyājñānam asti । tad yathā kasyacit prājñasya kvacic chilpaviśeṣe । utpadyate ca kvacij jñeye lokasyābhogamātreṇa jñānam । vyāpakaviruddham āha ॥

[I,116,iii]

nivṛttir nāsatī phalam iti । ajñānādyabhāvo hy ajñānādinivṛttiḥ । na cābhāvasya kiñcana kartavyam asti, nirupākhyatvā । akriyamāṇaś ca prasi<I,117>ddhir bhavitum arhati, na pramāṇaphalaṃ bhavitum arhatīty arthaḥ । yad asat, na tat pramāṇaphalam, atyantābhāvavat । asatī ca nivṛttiḥ । viruddhavyāptaḥ । pradīpasyāpi nāndhakāranivṛttimātraṃ phalam, kiṃ tu ghaṭādyavabhāsanam । atas tadavasthaḥ pramāṇaphalabhāvadoṣa iti ॥

{1.21–1.22a}

[I,117,i]

kenacit sambandheneti । vṛttikāramatabhedenānekasambandhāḥ । tatra kvacit sambandhe pratyakṣalakṣaṇam idaṃ sūtraṃ na sambhavatīty ataḥ kenacit sambhandhenety āha ॥

[I,117,ii]

tatra kenacit sambandham āhuḥ — prasiddhiliṅga ātmā । prasiddhir jñānam ity anarthāntaram । tasyāś ca prasiddher guṇatvam anityatvaṃ ca śabdavad draṣṭavyam iti । āha — anityā ced buddhir anityaṃ ca kāraṇavad bhavati, tasmād asyā api kāraṇaṃ vācyamanyatvaṃ ca jñātur anena hetuneti । ucyate — ātmendriyamano 'rthasannikarṣādyanniṣpadyate, tad anyat । yady ato niṣpadyate, tat tato 'nyat । tad yathā turyādibhyaḥ paṭādiḥ । tathā cātmādibhyo jñānaṃ niṣpadyate । tasmāt tad api tebhyo 'nyat । kāraṇam apy anenaiva darśitam ātmādi । asmin sambandhe pratyakṣalakṣaṇam idaṃ sūtraṃ nopapadyate ॥

<I,118>

[I,118,i]

apare sambandham ācakṣate — laiṅgikaṃ pramāṇam uktam । ata āha — kiṃ laiṅgikam evaivaṃ pramāṇam । nety ucyate । ātamendriyamano 'rthasannikarṣādyanniṣpadyate, tad anyat । pratyakṣaṃ pramāṇam iti vākyaśeṣaḥ । atra sambandhe pratyakṣalakṣaṇam idaṃ sūtraṃ vyākhyāyate ॥

[I,118,ii]

asautram api bhāṣyakāroktam astīndriyārthasannikarṣaḥ pratyakṣam ātmanaḥ sannikarṣo veti । ataḥ sautram ity āha । dravyagrahaṇena guṇakarmaṇor api sautraṃ pratyakṣalakṣaṇam aparam astīti darśayati । tat punar guṇakarmasu sannikṛṣṭeṣu jñānaniṣpatter dravyaṃ kāraṇaṃ । kāraṇakāraṇaṃ cety atat । svāśrayeṇānabhivyakteṣu guṇakarmasu jñānaṃ nopajāyate । tasmāt tadāśrayo dravyaṃ guṇakarmāṇy abhivyañjayat tajjñānasya kāraṇaṃ bhavati । guṇakarmajñānasya kāraṇam indriyārthasannikarṣaḥ । tasya kāraṇaṃ dravyaṃ ghaṭādi kāraṇakāraṇam ity ucyate । atra ca prādhānyād ekārthasamavetakāraṇatvāc cātmanaḥ sannikarṣād utpadyate । indriyamano 'rthasannikarṣās tu tasyānugrāhakāḥ ॥

[I,118,iii]

kecit tv iti । jñānasya hi pramāṇatve phalam anyan syāt । tathā hy adhigamaḥ phalam । na ca jñānād adhigamo 'rthāntaram । ataḥ śrāyakādayaḥ sannikarṣam icchati । asādhāraṇakāraṇatvād iti । itare hi sannikarṣāḥ smṛtyādijñānasādhāraṇāḥ । indriyārthasannikarṣas tu pratyakṣasyaiva kāraṇam ॥

<I,119>

[I,119,i]

prādhānyād iti । ātamamanasoḥ prādhānyāt tatsannikarṣasyāpi prādhānyam । ataḥ sārasvatādayaḥ tam icchanti । tatrātmahaḥ prādhānyam, jñānakartṛtvāt talliṅgatvāt phalopabhoktṛtvāc ca । manaso 'pi sarvaviṣayatvāj jñānenaikārthasamavāyāc ca ॥

[I,119,ii]

evaṃ cetyādinā śāstravirodham āha । yathā hy ātmano 'gnyādisamanusmṛtimataḥ pratyakṣaṃ liṅgamālocyāpratyakṣe bhavaty anumānam arthe, tathāsyaiva viśeṣasmṛtimataḥ sāmānyamātrālocanād viśeṣeṣv gṛhyamāṇeṣu saṃśaya iti tulyā laiṅgikena saṃśayasya niṣpattiḥ । yathā ca bhūtārthasambandhavaśenāyam arthasya svabhāva ity utpadyate pratyakṣam, tathā bhūtārthasambandhavaśenāyam eva nānya ity utpadyate nirṇaya iti pratyakṣam, tulyāsya niṣpattir iti yad uktam, tad virudhyate । vicārapūrvakatvān nirṇayasyeti sambandhaḥ । sāmānyapratyakṣiṇaḥ saṃśaye sati vicārayato viśeṣarūpeṇārthāv adhāraṇaṃ yadā, tadā gaur evāyam, na gavaya iti nirṇaya utpadyate । viṣayālocanārthatvād iti viṣayānubhavaprayojanatvād ity arthaḥ । viṣayālocanamātrārthaṃ hīti । mātraśabdo 'dhikavyavacchedārthaḥ । etad uktaṃ bhavati — na viśeṣaṇādhyāropādau vyāpriyata iti । tac ca nirvikalpakatvāt । yasya ca viṣayānubhavamātraṃ prayojanam, tadvicāranirapekṣaṃ pravartate । tad darśayati — tatra kuto vicāra iti । tataś ca vaidharmyān na tena nirṇayasya tulyotpattiḥ, yathānumānena । <I,120> syād etat — vidyamānārthasambandhavaśād utpattimātram atidiśyata iti । tad ayuktam, viśeṣātideśān arthakatvaprasaṅgāt । saṃśayānumānādibhir apy evam utpattis tulyā prāpnoti, teṣām api sāmānyādibhūtārthābhisambandhavaśenotpatteḥ । anatideśa eveti jñānaṃ tasyāpi sādharmyasyābhāvāt ॥

[I,120,i]

sarvathāgrahaṇaprasaṅga iti । sarvair ākārair bāhuleyatvādibhir api grahaṇaṃ syāt । yatrāṃśe śaktiḥ, tasyaiva grahaṇaṃ bhaviṣyatīty āha — sarvātmanetyādi । niravayavattvān nāsty eva so 'ṃśaḥ,  ya indriyeṇa na sannikṛṣeṇa । tataś cārthād vyatiriktatvāt tadviśeṣāṇām arthavat teṣv api grahaṇotpādanaśaktiḥ syāt । nanu ya evāṃśo jighṛkṣitaḥ, sa eva gṛhyata ity āha — kim etad ityādi । yadā parān paśyato dṛṣṭvā pūrvam evārthadarśanāt kim etad ity aviśeṣeṇa jighṛkṣāyāṃ satyāṃ tatra gatvā paśyati, tadāyaṃ doṣa āpadyate । sannikarṣavādinaś cemaṃ doṣam udbhāvayatāyam arthato jñānavādino 'py udbhāvita eva bhavati । tathā hi sannikarṣo 'rthagrahaṇahetur ity eṣa doṣa udbhāvyate । jñānapramāṇavādināpi ca sa eva jñānasya hetur iṣyata iti samāno doṣaḥ । tathā hīmam eva doṣam anumāne 'bhidhāsyati ॥

[I,120,ii]

yadīndriyārthasambandhe sati sarvātmano grahaṇaṃ prasajyate, tadā bhavato 'pi tribhir indriyaiḥ sambandhyamāne viṣaye kim iti na sarvātmanā grahaṇaṇaṃ bhavatīti cet, nāsmābhis tasya sannikarṣo hetur iṣyate, tasyādravyasattvāt । api cāsmākaṃ <I,121> cakṣurādināpi sarvathā gṛhyate 'rtha iti matam । kevalaṃ na bhavatīty avyavahārayogyatvād agṛhītakalpa eva sa ity uktam etat । yadi punaḥ paro 'py evaṃ brūyāt, nārhati sa evaṃ vaktum, yat sākṣād ālocanam arthānāṃ yathā gaur evāyam aśva evāyam iti, tatpratyakṣam iti vacanāt, tathā bhūtārthasambandhavaśenāyam asya svabhāva ity utpadyate pratyakṣam iti vacanāt, tathā yeyam indriyāṇām artheṣu prasiddhiḥ, śabdo 'yaṃ rūpam idaṃ raso 'yaṃ sparśo 'yam iti vacanāt, yato niścayātmakaṃ paraḥ pratyakṣam icchati ॥

[I,121,i]

iyam eva niścayānāṃ svārthapratipattiḥ, yat tan niścayanam । tac ced ākārāntaravad aniścitam, kathaṃ tair gṛhītam । katham idānīm aniścīyamānaṃ pratyakṣeṇa tadāpi gṛhītaṃ nāma । na pratyakṣaṃ kasyacin niścayātmakam । tad yad api gṛhṇāti, tan na niścayena, kiṃ tarhi tatpratibhāsena । tan na niścayāniścayavaśāt pratyakṣasya grahaṇāgrahaṇe । naivaṃ niścayasya । kiñcin niścinvato 'py anyatrāniścayena grahaṇāgrahaṇam । tasmāt tad evāsya grahaṇam, yo niścayaḥ । anyathaikākāre 'pi tan na <I,122> syāt । kiṃ punaḥ sarvāt manā gṛhīte 'pi tathā niścayo na bhavati । sahakārivaikalyāt । anubhavo hi yathāvikalpābhyāsaṃ niścayāñ janayati, yathā rūpadarśanāviśeṣe 'pi kuṇapakāminībhakṣyavikalpān । tatra buddhipāṭavaṃ tadvāsanābhyāsaḥ prakaraṇam ityādayo 'nubhavān niścayotpattihetavaḥ । teṣām eva tu tāratamyādiviśeṣāt paurvāparyam । yathā janakādhyāpakatvāviśeṣe 'pi pitaramāyāntaṃ paśyataḥ pitā me āgacchatīti prāgniścayo bhavati, nopādhyāya iti । so 'pi bhavan niścayo 'sati bhrāntikāraṇe bhavati । tasmān nānubhūta ity eva sarvākāraniścayaḥ ॥

[I,122,i]

yadi tarhi paraḥ savikalpaṃ pratyakṣam icchati, kathaṃ tad uktam — viṣayālocanamātrārthaṃ hi catuṣṭayasannikarṣajam iti । pramāṇasiddham indriyajñāsyāvikalpakatvam iti vastuvaśād ācāryeṇa tad uktam । asmābhis tu parābhyupagamavaśād evam uktam ity avirodhaḥ । yadi parasya niścayātmakaṃ pratyakṣam ity abhyupagamaḥ, kathaṃ pratyakṣeṇa nirṇayasya tulyotpattir ity etad yujyate । na hi tenaiva tasya tulyotpattir iti yuktam abhyupetum । ayam aparas tasya doṣo 'stu, ya evam icchatīty alam iti prasaṅgena ॥

[I,122,ii]

viṣayabhedo 'pīti । pramāṇasyātmamanoviṣayatvāt phalasya cārthaviṣayatvāt । nanu jñānam apy ātmani samavāyāt tadviṣayam eva । naitad asti । jñānasya hi jñeyaṃ <I,123> viṣayatvenābhimatam, na samavāyikāraṇam । anyathā sarvajñānānām ekaṣayatā syāt । ātmamanaḥ sannikarṣas tvanālambanaḥ । tasya samavāyikāraṇāt ko 'nyo viṣayaḥ syād ity anuttaram etat । viṣayabhede ko doṣa ity āha — na hītyādi ॥

[I,123,i]

api cetyādinābhyupetabādhām āha । śāstra uktam — sāmānyaviśeṣāpekṣaṃ dravyaguṇakarmasu pratyakṣam, dravyaguṇakarmāpekṣaṃ ca dravyeṣv iti । atra sāmānyagrahaṇena mahāsāmānyaṃ sattā gṛhyate । viśeṣagrahaṇena dravyatvādīni śeṣāṇi sāmānyāni viśeṣāś cāpekṣyā bhavanti । tatra sāmānyāpekṣaṃ dravye saddravyam iti, viśeṣāpekṣaṃ dravyaṃ pṛthivī ghaṭa ityādi, dravyaguṇakarmāpekṣaṃ daṇḍī śuklo gacchatīti ॥

[I,123,ii]

kuto na yujyata ity āha — yasmād ityādi । svārthamātragrāhikatvād ity etad viṣayālocanārthatvād ity asya vivaraṇam । sandhānaṃ yojanam । tasya svarūpaṃ darśayatīdam asyetyādinā । avaśyam iti । anyathā yo 'pi viśeṣaṇaṃ viśeṣyaṃ ca na gṛhṇāti tayoś ca sandhānaṃ na karoti, so 'pi tathā gṛhṇīyād iti manyate । matublopādabhedopacārād eveti yathāsambhavaṃ draṣṭavyam । tathā hi guṇavacanebhyo matublopaḥ, abhedopacāro 'pi na sarvatra । na hi <I,124> kriyādravyarūpeṇāśrayatītir asti । matubarthas tu yatra gamyate, sa eva matublopena lakṣyate ॥

[I,124,i]

yadīndriyabuddhau tan nopapadyate, kva tarhi tad ity āha — tac cetyādi । prāgviśeṣaṇaṃ viśeṣyaṃ ca gṛhītvā lokavyavasthāṃ cānusmṛtyānusandhānaṃ śakyate kartum, nānyathā । tadā cendriyajñānaṃ ciraniruddham iti smārtenākṛṣya viśeṣaṇaṃ manasaiva yojanaṃ kriyate । atas tatraiva tad upapadyate । anyathā hīti yadi smārtākṛṣṭatvaṃ viśeṣaṇasya neṣyate । tad anena yad viśeṣaṇāpekṣaṃ jñānam, na tat pratyakṣam, mānasam eva vā tat । tad yathā surabhi madhuram iti jñānam । yathoktaprakāraṃ ca gauḥ gacchatīti । vyāpakaviruddham, dvitīyasādhyāpekṣyā tu svabhāvam āha । na cārhatīti । dṛṣṭānte sādhyavaikalpāśaṅkām apakāroti । bhinnendriyagrāhyatvād iti । dṛṣṭānte gandharasayorghrāṇarasanagrāhyatvād dravyasya ca cakṣuḥsparśanagrāhyatvāt । tad etad uktaṃ bhavati — yad bhinnendriyagrāhyaviśeṣaṇaviśeṣyaviṣayaṃ jñānam, na tat pratyakṣam, mānasam eva vā tat । tad yathā rūpam amlam iti jñānam । tathā ca surabhi madhuram ity etaj jñānam iti । pūrvavad dhetubhedo yojyaḥ ॥

[I,124,ii]

idānīṃ dravyam eva na kiñcid asti, rūpādisamudāye tad upacārāt । tat kutas tatra pratyakṣaṃ bhaviṣyatīti dravye vicāramārabhate । yadi cetyādi । asyāyam arthaḥ — <I,125> yad anekendriyagrāhyam, na tad ekam, rūpādivat । tathā ca dravyam iti vyāpakaviruddhaḥ prasaṅgaḥ । anekendriyagrāhyatvaṃ tu dravyasya, darśanaṃ sparśanaṃ ca dravyam ity abhyupagamāt ॥

[I,125,i]

rūpādyabhedo veti । etad darśayati — rūpādiṣv api bhedavyasthāyā anekendriyagrāhyatvaṃ nibandhanam । yadi ca saty api tasmin dravye bhedo neṣyate, rūpādiṣv api sa na syād iti । grahaṇabhedād rūpādīnām anekatvavyavastheti cet, bhavatu, tato 'pi nāsmābhir bhinnendriyagrāhyatvād eva bheda ity avadhāryate । api ca bhinnendriyagrāhyatvena grahaṇabhedo 'py ākṣipta eva । avaśyaṃ hi bhinnendriyagrāhyatve grahaṇabhedena bhāvyam । nanu dravye saty api bhinnendriyagrāhyatve na bhavati grahaṇabhedaḥ । na, tasyaiva dravyasya vicāryamāṇatvād rūpādiṣv api tulyaparyanuyogāc ca ॥

[I,125,ii]

dṛṣṭaṃ cendriyādinā pratyakṣasiddhaṃ dravyasyaikatvaṃ rūpādeś cānekatvam । tat kathaṃ tad anumānenānyathā śakyate kartum iti darśayati । bhāvaguṇatvayor ivety anenāpi bhāvaguṇatvābhyām anekāntam āha । bhāgaguṇatvayor āśrayā rūpādayaḥ sārvendiryāḥ । tatas tayor api sārvendriyatvam । yathoktam — etena guṇatve bhāve ca sārvendriyaṃ jñānaṃ vyākhyātam iti । abhedajñānaṃ punar yad eva mayā dṛṣṭam, tad eva spṛśāmīti । <I,126> nendriyeṇa tad iti parihāraḥ । akṣānekatvavaiyarthyād ity anekendriyakalpanāyā nirnimittatvād ity arthaḥ । ekam indriyam anekam arthaṃ sakalaṃ nālam avagantum itīndriyāntaraṃ parikalpyate । yadi punas tad indriyāntarārthe 'pi pravartate, indriyabahutvakalpanā nirnimittā syāt । etad uktaṃ bhavati — kāryabhedenendriyabhedo 'vasīyate । indriyakāryaṃ ced ekenaiva kriyate, nendriyāntare pramāṇam astīti tan na kalpanīyaṃ syād iti । apārthiketi nirnimittety arthaḥ ॥

{1.22b–1.23a'}

[I,126,i]

athāpi syād iti । evaṃ manyate — anekam indriyam ekakm arthaṃ paricchettuṃ samartham, na punar ekam anekam artham । aneke ca rūpādayaḥ । tato nāstīndriyabahutvakalpanāvaiyartham iti । svārthe bhinne 'pītyādi । yadi hy ekam indriyam indriyāntarārthe 'pi pravarteta, tataḥ sarva eva sa tasya svārthaḥ syāt । svārthe ca bhinne 'pi nīlādivattasya śaktiḥ syād evety aparihāraḥ । saṅkhyādibhedena ceti, saṅkhyāparimāṇāni pṛthaktvaṃ saṃyogavibhāgau paratvāparatve karma ca rūpisamavāyāc cākṣuṣāṇīti siddhāntāt । na tv indriyāntarārtha ity etena yaś cakṣur indriyārthaḥ, na tatra tvag indriyasya sāmarthayam, rūpādivat । tathā ca dravyam iti vyākapaviruddhaṃ prasaṅga sūcayati । indriyāntarārthatvenaivetyādi । rūpasparśator hi sann api bhedo yāvad bhinnenendriyeṇa nāvasīyate, tāvan na śakyate jñātum । yadi punar ekenendriyeṇa grahaṇaṃ syāt, tadā yathā nīlādīnāṃ cakṣur gocaratvenābhedas tathā rūpasparśayor api syāt । tataś ca sparśo 'pi cakṣuṣā gṛhyeta । <I,127> yataś cakṣuṣāgrahaṇam iti । bhedakṛtam indriyāntarāgrahaṇaṃ darśayati । tad etena yatra sparśanendriyasya sāmarthyam, na sa cakṣur indriyārthaḥ, sparśavat । sparśanendriyasya sāmarthyaṃ ca dravya iti vyāpakaviruddhaṃ prasaṅgam āha ॥

[I,127,i]

asyaiva sādhyaviparyaye 'niṣṭaṃ prasaṅgayann āha — tad yadītyādi । yadi punaś cakṣuḥ sparśanagrāhyam api dravyaṃ gṛhṇātītīṣyate, tadendriyāntarārthe 'pi cakṣuṣaḥ svārtha ity abhyanujñātaṃ syāt, dravyavat । tataś ca svārthatvāt tasya sparśarasādibhedena bhinnasyāpi nīlāder iva cakṣuṣā grahaṇam ity ato na bhinnatvam anekendriyagrāhyatve hetuḥ, nānekendriyakalpanāyāṃ hetur ity arthaḥ, yato bhinno 'pi svārtha ekenaivendriyeṇa paricchidyate । tataś ca tadayuktam āpadyate, yad uktam — bhinnatvād anekendriyagrāhyā rūpādaya iti । kiṃ tarhīndriyāntarārtha indriyāntareṇa na śakyate grahītum, evam anekam indriyaṃ śakyate kalpayitum iti darśayati । tad evaṃ sthitam etat — na dravyam anekendriyagrāhyam asti ॥

[I,127,ii]

punar asyaiva spaṣṭīkaraṇāya dravyasyānekendriyābhyupagame 'bhyupetabādhā prāpnotīti darśayann āha — yadi ceyādi । yady abhinnam artham anekam indriyaṃ gṛhṇīyāt, <I,128> tataḥ svaviṣayaniyamo syād indriyāṇām । ataś ca rūpādīnāṃ sārvendriyatvaṃ pratyekaṃ syāt, dravyavat । sārvendriyagrahaṇaṃ cātraikendriyagrāhyatāniyamanirāsaparam, yad āha — evaṃ hi rūpādayo 'nekendriyagrāhyāḥ prāpnuvantīti । na niyamenaikendriyagrāhyāḥ syur ity arthaḥ ॥

[I,128,i]

svaviśeṣaniyāmākā iti svaviśeṣe niyāmakāḥ । indriyabuddhīnām iti sanmbandhīyam । na hi dravyasaṅkhyādikarmasv iti । ādigrahaṇād bhāvaguṇatvapṛthaktvādayo gṛhyate । na syād ityādi । dravyasya sparśanena cakṣuṣā ca grahaṇaṃ na syāt । śeṣāṇāṃ cakṣuṣeti yojanīyam ॥

[I,128,ii]

evaṃ tarhīti । anyathā niyāmakatvam āha । evaṃ ceti । atra pakṣe 'nantarokto doṣo nāvataratīti darśayati । yasya yatra niyamakāraṇaṃ nāsti, na tatra tasya niyamaḥ । tad yathecchamātravṛttīnāṃ kvacid arthe hastādisañjñānām । nāsti ca niyamakāraṇam indriyāṇāṃ dravyādiṣu । kāraṇābhāvaḥ । sūtravirodha iti । abhyupetabādhām āha ॥

<I,129>

{1.23'abcd}

[I,129,i]

yuktyāpītyādi । yo 'bhāvaḥ, nāsau kriyate, khapuṣpavat । abhāvaś cendriyāntareṇāgrahaṇam । vyāpakaviruddhaḥ ॥

[I,129,ii]

anye sūtram anyathā vyācakṣate — tadgrahaṇena svaviśeṣavyatiriktaṃ viśeṣāntaram abhipretam । tadabhāvāt sparśatvādyabhāvād rūpe cakṣurindriyaṃ pravartate । tena ca sparśatvādyabhāvena rūpatvabhāvo lakṣyate । avyabhicāra indriyāntareṇāgrahaṇām iti । tad api yuktyapi cetyādinaiva nirakṛtam । yuktyanuvidhāyitve hi sati tathāvyākhyānaṃ śobheta yuktivirodhe tu kaṣṭakalpanākalpanaiva । api ca svaviśeṣāṇāṃ prakṛtatvāt tacchatrutyā teṣām eva grahaṇaṃ yuktam, na viśeṣāntarāṇām, aprakṛtatvāt । tadabhāvena ca bhāvopādānam ayuktam ity asāram etat ॥

[I,129,iii]

pūrvake tu vyākhyāne nāsty ayaṃ doṣaḥ । yatra hi yasya hetur nāsti, na tat tatra bhavatīti yuktam, yad āha — syāt tv ityādi ॥

[I,129,iv]

yadi tarhi dravyaṃ nāsti, yad aham adrākṣam, tad evās prākṣam ity asyābhedajñānasya ko viṣayaḥ । na cāviṣayam evaitad iti śakyate vaktum, deśādiniyamenotpatter abhimatapratyakṣavad iti matvāha — yat tarhītyādi ॥

[I,129,v]

anyagocaram ityādi । dravyādanya evāsya kalpito viṣaya iti darśayati । bhinnaṃ viṣayam ityādi । rūpaṃ sparśaṃ ca parasparato vyāvṛttaṃ viṣayam upalabdhava<I,130>tas tad utpadyate । tena yady api kalpitaviṣayam, tathāpi sati rūpādyupalambhe tasya bhāvān marīcikādau jalajñānavad eśādiniyamenaiva tad utpadyata iti sūcayati । tatsahacarasamudāyaviṣayam iti । sa cakṣuḥsparśanopalabdho bhinno viṣayaḥ sahacaro 'syeti tadguṇasaṃvijñāno bahuvrīhiḥ । punas tatsahacaraḥ samudāyo viṣayo 'syeti bahuvrīr eva । evaṃ rūpasparśayoḥ sahacaropalakṣaṇatve 'pi sati na gandhādisamudāyamātraviṣayatoktā bhavati । smārtam abhedajñānam iti । yeṣu rūpādiṣv anubhavapuraḥsaro ghaṭa iti saṅketaḥ, tatsamudāye punaruttarakālaṃ rūpaṃ sparśaṃ copalabdhavataḥ smārtaṃ sa evāyaṃ ghaṭa ity abhedajñānam utpadyate ॥

[I,130,i]

yas tv āha — samudāyo 'vastutvān na kenacij jñānenānubhūyate । tat kathaṃ tatra smṛtir iti, tasyedam acodyam । samudāyo hi kalpitaḥ । yaś ca kalpitaḥ padārthaḥ, sa vijñānasya grāhyāṃśatayātmabhūta iti svasaṃvittyaivānubhūyate । anyathā kathaṃ saiveyaṃ mahatī prāsādamāleti smaraṇaṃ syāt । kuta etat — samudāyaviṣayaṃ tat, na punar vastusaddhaṭādidravyaviṣayam ity āha — rūpādyagrahe tadbuddhabhāvād iti । yo yad agrahe saty upalabdhilakṣaṇaprāpto nopalabhyate, na sa tato vyatirikto 'sti । tad yathā kāṣṭhādibhyaḥ ṣaṇṇagarī prāsādamālā vā । rūpādyagrahe <I,131> nopalabhyate copalabdhilakṣaṇaprāptaṃ ghaṭādidravyam iti svabhāvānupalabdhim āha । yatrālokāgrahaḥ, tatra rūpaṃ dṛśyam eva na bhavati । vināpi cālokena kaiścit prāṇibhis tasya grahaṇāt, na tenānekāntaḥ ॥

[I,131,i]

tathā viśeṣyān ityādi । bhāvaguṇatvābhyāṃ yaḥ prāg anekānta uktaḥ, tatparihārāyopanyāsaḥ । viśeṣyā rūpādayaḥ । tān bhinnān sadguṇa iti cānena viśeṣaṇenāsambaddhān eva prāg upalabdhavataḥ । tato 'rthāntaravyavacchedaviṣayam asadguṇavyāvṛttilakṣaṇam, yat sāmānyaṃ tad viṣayam iti yāvat । abhedena sarvatreti । tad dhi mānasaṃ sāmānyākārānuraktaṃ jñānaṃ santam api teṣāṃ bhedam antardhāpya svākāraṃ cābhinnam eṣu pratyasyaikatvam ivāpādayat tān abhedena sarveṣu teṣūpajāyate, naikatraiva । na bhāvaguṇatvayoḥ pratyakṣam iti । ato nānekānta ity abhiprāyaḥ । tasyānupalakṣaṇād iti । bhinnapadārthaviṣayaṃ prāg anubhavajñānam । tatas tat pūrvakaṃ mānasaṃ sāmānyajñānam ity asya bhedasyānupalakṣaṇāt ॥

[I,131,ii]

tulyagocarateṣṭā ced ity anaikāntikatvasamarthanāyopanyāsaḥ । tulyagocaratve hetum āha — tadagre tadbuddhabhāvād iti । nāgṛhītaviśeṣaṇā viśeṣye buddhiḥ pravartata ity arthaḥ । tataś ca rūpādīnāṃ viśeṣyāṇāṃ sārvendriyatvāt tadviśeṣaṇayor api <I,132> bhāvaguṇatvayoḥ sārvendriyatvaṃ sidhyati । ye hi viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhūtāḥ, te tulyendriyaviṣayāḥ । tad yathā daṇḍaṇḍinaḥ । tathā ca sattvatadvanto guṇatvatadvantaś ca । svabhāvapratirūpakaḥ ॥

[I,132,i]

aniṣṭam anuṣajyata iti । prasaṅgavyājenānaikāntikatvam āha । dravyavantītyādi । dravyam eṣām āśrayo 'stīti dravyavanti । atra dravyavān guṇo viśeṣyaḥ, dravyaṃ viśeṣaṇam । tataś ca yathā guṇaḥ pāñcendriyaḥ, tathā dravyam api syāt । tathaikadravyatvād ityādi । dravyaṃ hy adravyam anekadravyaṃ ceṣyate, na tv ekadravyaṃ dravyam । tatrādravyaṃ dravyam, yasya dravyāntaram āśrayo nāsti, yathā paramāṇv ākāśādikam । anekadravyaṃ tu dravyam, yasyānekaṃ dravyam āśrayaḥ, yathā ghaṭaḥ । sa hy anekatra samavetaḥ । atrāpy ekaṃ dravyaṃ bhāvasya sārvendriyasya viśeṣaṇam iti dravyam api sārvendriyaṃ syāt । na ceṣyate । tasmād anekāntaḥ ॥

[I,132,ii]

dravyavṛtter ityādi । dravyavṛttir yo bhāvaḥ, tasyaikaṃ dravyaṃ viśeṣaṇam । na cāsau sārvendriyaḥ, kiṃ tarhi guṇavṛttiḥ । tato 'yam aprasaṅgaḥ । kuta etat abhinno <I,133> bhāvo dravyādibhāve na pratiṣidhyate, na punar bhinna ity āha — tathā hy uktam ityādi । bhāvasya dravyasvabhāvapratiṣedhe kṛte guṇas tarhi syāt karma cety āśaṅkāpanodāyedam uktam — guṇakarmasu ca bhāvān na karma na guṇa iti । ataḥ prakṛtasyaiva bhāvasya dharmaś caśabdena smuccīyate । anyathā samuccayāya cakāro na yujyate । dravyavṛtteś ca guṇakarmasvavṛtter guṇakarmasvabhāvanirāso na syāt । yadi cetyādi । yady ayaṃ viruddhadharmādhyāsa iṣyate, tato bhinnaḥ syāt । tataś cāyam anantarokto doṣaḥ syāt, etac ca sūtraṃ virudhyate — salliṅgāviśeṣādviśeṣaliṅgābhāvāc caiko bhāva iti bhāvaḥ ॥

[I,133,i]

yadā cetyādi । yadāyaṃ cakṣuṣā dṛṣṭāgniṣṇo 'yam iti gṛhṇati, tadā sparśo 'py agniviśeṣaṇatvac cākṣuṣaḥ syāt । na caivam iti ॥

{1.24}

[I,133,ii]

ato py anekāntaḥ । dṛṣṭaḥ hīty anenārthāpattisamāṃ jātim upanyasyati । anantareṇāpi cetyādinā bhinneṣv api nīlādiṣv indriyabhedābhāvaṃ darśayantaru<I,134>caitanye svāpavad dvitīyām upalabdhisamām । grahaṇabhedād iti ca hetvantaropadarśanāt prathamām ॥

[I,134,i]

anyathoktam ityādinārthāpattisamāṃ nirasyati । syād etat — anekānta ity anena na hetor vyabhicāra uktaḥ, kiṃ tarhi pratijñādoṣaḥ, yatas tvayā bhinnendriyagrāhyatvād evety avadhārayatā hetvantaraṃ nāstīti pratijñātaṃ bhavati । tac cāyuktam, hetvantarasyāpi sadbhāvād ity ata āha — na cetyādi । na cātrānekānta iti nāyaṃ niyamo vyabhicārīty arthaḥ ॥

[I,134,ii]

na sarvaṃ sādhyam ityādinā dvitīyām upalabdhisamām apākaroti । na buddhibhedo 'py anyatva ityādinā hetvantare 'pi sādhyasya vṛttiṃ darśayan sādhyavyabhicārapradarśanāt prathamām ॥

[I,134,iii]

bhede 'bhedaḥ kuto 'nyatheti । grahaṇabhedāt kevalād anyathā, indriyabhede grahaṇabhede ca saty abhedo naiveti yāvat । yatra cetyādinā yadi kevalād grahaṇabhedān nīlādiṣu bhedaḥ, evaṃ sati yatrendriyabhedo grahaṇabhedaś cāsti, tatra sutarāṃ bhedaḥ sidhyati, indriyābhedakṛtāyā abhedāśaṅkāyā abhāvād iti darśayati ॥

<I,135>

[I,135,i]

eteneti dravye pratyakṣanirākaraṇanyāyena । guṇādiṣv iti । ādiśabdena karmasu । apeditaṃ pratyākhyātam । katham ity āha — tad api hītyādi । svādhāraṃ guṇakarmaṇoḥ svasāmānyaṃ guṇatvaṃ karmatvaṃ ca । sva ādhāro yasya, tat svādhāram । tatsambandhadvāreṇa । utpadyata ity anena saha sambandhaḥ, viśeṣaṇasambandhadvāreṇotpadyata iti yāvat । tataś ca yad viśeṣaṇāpekṣam, na tat pratyakṣam ityādi pūrvavat sādhanaṃ vācyam । kiṃ ca tad api catuṣṭayādisannikarṣād evotpadyata itīdaṃ darśanam । ādiśabdena trayasannikarṣād dvayasannikarṣāc ca yathāsambhavam । tataḥ ko doṣa ity āha — yathā ca na sarvatretyādi । tatra catuṣṭayasannikarṣādātmamanaindriyadravyasannikarṣād rūpādiṣu karmasu ca । trayasannikarṣāc chabde । tatra dravyeṇa sahendriyasya sambandho nāsti, vyomnaḥ śrotratvāt tatraiva ca samvāyāc chabdasya dvayasannikarṣād ātmamanaḥsannikarṣāt sukhādiṣu । tad evaṃ guṇakarmasvasannikṛṣṭeṣu jñānaniṣpatter dravyaṃ kāraṇakāraṇaṃ ceti yad uktam, tad api dūṣitam iti ॥

<I,136>

{1.25}

[I,136,i]

kāpilānām ityādi । tatroktam — kim anumānam  evaikaṃ pramāṇam । nety ucyate । śrotrādivṛttiś ca pratyakṣam । pramāṇam iti śeṣa । śrotratvakcakṣur jihvāghrāṇānāṃ manasādhiṣṭhitā vṛttiḥ śabdasparśarūparasagandheṣu yathākramaṃ grahaṇe vartamānā pratyakṣaṃ pramāṇam ॥

[I,136,ii]

manaseti manovṛttyā । prakṛtivikārayor abhedopacārād evam uktam । adhiṣṭhānārthaḥ । tad yathā rājapuruṣeṇādhiṣṭhiḥ pravṛttas tena saheti gamyate ॥

[I,136,iii]

anye tvāhuḥ — manasādhiṣṭhiteti manasā saṃviditā, yathoktam — bāhyeṣv artheṣv indriyaṃ vyavasāyaṃ kurute । tasmiṃs tv indriyavyavasāye mano 'nuvyavasāyaṃ kuruta iti । anena hi grantenendriyavṛttir eva bāhyaviṣayākārā manovṛttyā saṃvedyate, na tv indriyavṛttisahitayā bāhyo 'rtha iti pratipāditam । tasmād yā śrotrādivṛttir manovṛttyā gṛhyate, sā tayādhiṣṭhitety uktā ॥

[I,136,iv]

vṛttir indriyāṇāṃ svaviṣayasānnidhye tadākāreṇa pariṇāmo jñeyaḥ । sā punar dviprakārā sapratyayā cāpratyayā ca । pratyayaḥ pauruṣeyo bodha ucyate caitanyarūpo viṣayānubhavasvabhāvaḥ । etac cātmanaḥ svarūpaṃ nānyasya kasyacit, <I,137> acetanatvāt । tena pauruṣeyeṇa pratyayena saha yā sampṛktā tadekarūpatām ivāpannā, sā sapratyayā । yathā taptāvasthāyām ayogolakas tejaḥsamparkād atat svabhāvo 'pi tejaḥsvabhāvatām ivāpadyate, tathā vṛttir ananubhavarūpāpi caitanyasaṃsargāc caitanyarūpatām ivāpadyate । yā punar vṛttiḥ pradīpaprabheda kevalaṃ viṣayapralāśikā, na tu caitanyasamparkād āsāditatadrūpeva, sāpratyayety ucyate । tatrāpratyayavṛttinivṛttye grahaṇe vartamānety āha । śabdasparśarūparasagandhānāṃ yathākramam ity anena svaviṣayaviniveśavacanān niyataviṣayatvam ॥

[I,137,i]

nanu śrotrādivṛttter eva śabdādīnāṃ grahaṇam । tatra kānyā vṛttir yā grahaṇe vartate । kecid āhuḥ — indriyaviṣayāntarālavartinī kaśābhighātavadūrdhvākṣiptajalavad vā viṣaye svasminn apratiṣṭhitā vṛttir ucyate । pratiṣṭhitā tu viṣayākāreṇa partiṇāmena pariniṣpannā grahaṇam iti । yatrāpi cāntarālaṃ nāsti ghnāṇādau tatrāpīndriyasya viṣayasaṃyogānantaraṃ vikriyopajāyamānā viṣayākāratvenāpariniṣpannā vṛttir jñeyā । tathā pariniṣpannāntargaṇam iti ॥

<I,138>

[I,138,i]

anye tv āhuḥ — vṛttīnāṃ nirvikalpatvopadarśanārtham etad bhedenoktaṃ śabdādīnāṃ grahaṇe vartamāneti । etad uktaṃ bhavati — svarūpagrahaṇamātre vartamānā pratyakṣaṃ pramāṇaṃ nānyatheti । yady api vikalpane 'syāḥ sambhavo nāsti, tathāpi jaiminīyādibhir vikalpakaṃ pratyakṣaṃ kalpitam । tadapekṣayaitad viśeṣaṇam । sarvaiva tu vṛttir grahaṇamātre vartate, na vikalpana iti । grahaṇe vartamāneti tatsvabhāvety arthaḥ ॥

[I,138,ii]

anye tv apratyayām eva vṛttiṃ pramāṇam icchanti, sapratyayāṃ tu phalam । grahaṇe vartamāneti caivaṃ varṇayanti । grahaṇe phale kartavye grahaṇanimittaṃ pravṛttety arthaḥ ॥

[I,138,iii]

indriyānavastheti । ānantyam indriyāṇāṃ prasajyata ity arthaḥ । katham ity āha — tair hītyādi । yathoktam — badhiraḥ satsv indriyeṣu navasu śabdaṃ na śṛṇoti । tasmāc chrotram eva śabdaviṣayam । anena tv agādīnāṃ svaviṣayaviniveśo boddhavya iti ॥

[I,138,iv]

trayo guṇās traiguṇyaṃ trailokyavat । utkarṣa ādhikyam, apakarṣo nyūnatā । mātraśabdaḥ svabhāvabhedavyavacchedāya । na hi śabdādīnāṃ sattvādiguṇasvabhāvānāṃ svarūpabhedo 'sti । tataś ca śāntaghoramūḍhaṣaḍjādibhedenānantyādanantam indriyaṃ syāt । yathā hi śabdādijātibhedo guṇotkarṣād bhavati, tathā <I,139> ṣaḍjādibhedo 'pi । ata etad uktaṃ bhavati — ye guṇotkarṣabhedabhinnāḥ, te bhinnendriyagrāhyajātisamanvitāḥ, śabdasparśādivat । tathā ca dhaivatādayaḥ śabdaviśeṣā iti svabhāvaḥ prasaṅgaḥ । tataś cābhyupetabādhaḥ ॥

[I,139,i]

athetyādi । yady utkarṣāpakarṣabhedeṣv api ṣaḍjādiṣu śrotrendriyagrāhyaikatraiguṇyajāti mat tvam iṣyate, prāptam ekam evendriyam, sarvatra traiguṇyasyābhedāt । ye 'bhinnatraiguṇyajāty avitāḥ, te śrotrendriyagrāhyāḥ, ṣaḍjādivat । tathā ca śabdasparśādayaḥ । sa eva prasaṅgaḥ ॥

[I,139,ii]

nanu karmavaśād indriyābhinirvṛttiḥ, na grāhyavaśāt । tatra katham idaṃ codyate — anantam ekaṃ vendriyaṃ prāpnotīti । asmākaṃ karmavaśādācintyaś ca karmaṇo vipāka iti manam । paras tu puruṣautsukkyanivṛttaye pradhānasya pravṛttir iti manyate । tatra yady ekenaivendriyeṇa puruṣārthaḥ sampadyeta, ekendriyātmanaiva prakṛter yuktaḥ pariṇāmaḥ, anyathānyatheti yuktaṃ codyam । syād etat — na brūmastraiguṇyam eva śrotrendriyagrāhyam, api tu tasyaiva pariṇāmo buddhyanugamanimittaṃ sādṛśyaṃ nāma jātiḥ । sā ca sarvaśabdabhedeṣv anuvartamānā vyāvartate sparśādibhyaḥ । saiva śrotrendriyeṇa gṛhyate । tena na kaścid doṣa ity āha — na hi traiguṇyavyatirekeṇetyādi ॥

<I,140>

[I,140,i]

kathaṃ nāstīy āha । asty eva saṃsthānākmikā jātiḥ । traiguṇyābhede 'pi hi traiguṇyasaṃsthānāmātrabhedāc chabdādijātayo bhidyante । tathā hy uktam — śabdasparśarūrasagandhāḥ pañca trayāṇāṃ sukhaduḥkhamohānāṃ sanniveśaviśeṣā iti । tasmāc chabdākārapariṇatāḥ sukhādayo yena samavasthitāḥ saṃsthānabhedena, tataḥ saṃsthānāntareṇa samavasthatāḥ sparśādaya iti vyapadiśyante । tato niyatendriyagrāhyatā na cendriyānantyam, pañcatvāt saṃsthānānām ॥

[I,140,ii]

saṃsthānaṃ dvigrāhyam iti । nanu saṃthānam adravyasat । tat kutas tasya dvigrāhyatā । naiṣa doṣaḥ । parābhiprāyeṇaivam uktam । paro hi rūpīndriyavijñānānvayena manovijñānena saṃsthānam upalabhya tayor vijñānayoḥ sūkṣmatarakālabhedasya duravadhāratvāṭ, tadevedaṃ cakṣuḥsparśanavijñānaṃ dīrghādisaṃsthānagrāhīti yathā manyate tathedam uktam । etad darśayati । bhavatu nāma saṃsthānaṃ vastutas taddvigrāhyaṃ dṛṣṭam iti svaviṣayaviniveśavyāghāta iti ॥

[I,140,iii]

śabdādayaś cety abhyupeyabādhām āha, atha vā prasaṅgaviparyayeṇa । yo yad dharmo na bhavati, nāsau tadātmakaḥ । tad yathā caitanyam apradhānadharmakaṃ na tadātmakam । na bhavanti ca śabdādayaḥ saṃsthānadharmāṇa iti vyāpakābhāvam, saṃsthānaṃ na trigocara iti sādhyābhāve hetvabhāvam āha ॥

[I,140,iv]

saṃsthānakṛtaṃ cetyādi । vīṇāpaṇavādiśabdajātīnāṃ hi parasparato bhinnānāṃ śabdajātyanatikrameṇāvasthānāt samānadeśatvaṃ syāt । tac cāyuktam । na hi dīrghahrasvādisaṃsthānam ekadeśaṃ dṛṣṭam iṣṭaṃ cety abhyupetabādhā ॥

<I,141>

[I,141,i]

tulyasaṃsthāneṣu cetyādi । saṃsthānabhedakṛtaṃ jātibhedam icchataḥ suvarṇādimayeṣu dhaṭādiṣu tulyasaṃsthāneṣu saṃsthānasvabhāvatvāj jātibhedānāṃ saṃsthānasya ca teṣu tulyatvād āpannam ekatvaṃ suvarṇādijātīnāṃ tatkāraṇānāṃ ca śabdādīnāṃ tatkāraṇānāṃ ca satvādīnām । nanu mātrādīnām eva tulyasaṃsthānānāṃ yuktam ekatvam, suvarṇādīnāṃ tu katham । tadavyatirekāt te 'pi samasaṃsthānā ity acodyam etat ॥

[I,141,ii]

svaviṣayavṛttyabhāva iti cakṣuṣā ghaṭādigrahaṇe śabdādīnāṃ grahaṇāt । prasaṅgaviparyayeṇa ca — yo yad abhede 'pi bhidyate, nāsau tadātmakaḥ । yathā caitanyābhede 'pi bhidyamāhaḥ sattvādayo na tadātmakāḥ । saṃsthānābhede 'pi ca bhidyante suvarṇādaya iti vyāpakaviruddham āha ॥

[I,141,iii]
