jātimātragrāhikā veti saṃsthānamātragrāhikā । mātraśabdaḥ sukhādigrahaṇavyavacchedārthaḥ । jātiviśiṣṭasukhādigrāhikā veti saṃsthānaviśiṣṭasukhādigrāhikā । arthasvabhāvāgrāhaṇam iti śandādīnāṃ sukhādisvabhāvāgrahaṇam । syād eta — saṃsthānād avyatirekād arthasvabhāvasya tadupalabdhau so 'py upalabdha evety āha — yasmād dṛṣṭetyādi । etena yasya saṃsthānamātropalabdhiḥ, na tasya svabhāva upalabhyate । tad yathā mandaprakāse pradeśe gavāder upalabhyamānasya saṃsthānamātrasya । saṃsthānamātropalabdhiś cendriyavṛttyā śabdādīnām iti viruddhavyāptam āha ॥

<I,142>

{1.26}

[I,142,i]

arthabhedāgraha iti śabdāder arthasya viśeṣopalabdhir na syāt, tatra saṃsthānāntarābhāvād iti । śabādayo hi saṃsthānātmakā jātayaḥ । na ca tatrāparasaṃsthānam asti yena vīṇāśabda iti grahaṇaṃ syād ity abhyupetahānam ॥

[I,142,ii]

atha mā mūdeṣa doṣa iti śabdajāter api saṃsthānāntaraṃ viśeṣaḥ kauśikādir iṣyate । evaṃ tarhy ayaṃ doṣaḥ prasajyata iti darśayann āha — arthe vetyādi । arthaḥ svaviṣayaḥ, tatra vikalpikā syāt । kuta ity āha — svārthaviśiṣṭasyetyādi । śabdajātiviśiṣṭasya tadviśeṣasya kauśikāder grahaṇād ity arthaḥ । niyogataś ca viśeṣaḥ śabdajātiviśiṣṭo grāhyaḥ, anyathā śabdasyāyaṃ viśeṣa iti na gṛhyeta । na ca jātiviśiṣṭatadbhedagrahaṇābhyupagame jātimātragrāhikety api pakṣo hīyate, yato mātraśabdena sukhādi vyavacchidyate, na śabdādijātiviśeṣaḥ । tad etad uktaṃ bhavati — yā viśeṣaṇavyavacchinnārthagrāhiṇī buddhiḥ, sā savikalpikā । tad yathā citragurayam iti buddhiḥ । tathā ca śabdādiviśeṣaviṣayā buddhir iti svabhāvaḥ prasaṅgaḥ ॥

[I,142,iii]

athetyādinā pakṣāntare 'pi tam eva doṣam āha ॥

[I,142,iv]

sukhādīṃś ceti । sukhādaya eva śabdād ātmanā sanniviṣṭā ity ataḥ paśnaḥ । na tāvat pratyekam ityādi । ekaikasya sukhāder grahaṇe hīndriyavṛttīnāṃ svavi<I,143>ṣaya eva niveśo na syāt, sarvatra sukhādīnām aviśeṣāt । sa ceṣyate । tasmān na pratyekaṃ sukhādi grāhyam, kiṃ tarhi śabdādi । ta eva tarhi pratyekaṃ pariṇatāḥ śabdādisvabhāvā bhaviṣyantīty āha — na hītyādi । pañca trayāṇāṃ sanniveśaviśeṣā ity abhyupagamān naitat samasti । tadetad uktaṃ bhavati — yac chabdādisvabhāvaṃ na bhavati, na tac chrotrādivṛttigrāhyam, caitanyavat । na bhavati ca pratyekaṃ sukhādi śabdādisvabhāvam iti vyāpakābhāvaḥ ॥

[I,143,i]

na, ananyatvād ity asiddhim āha । yac chabdādibhyo 'nanyat, tacchrotrādivṛttigrāhyam, śabdādivat । tathā ca sukhādi । svabhāvaḥ ॥

{1.27}

[I,143,ii]

nānyac ced ityādi । yac chabdāder ananyat, na tat tasya kāraṇam, śabdādivat । tathā ca sukhādīti viruddhavyāptam āha । tataś cābhyupetabādhā । yad uktam ityādinā hetutvābhyupagamam āha । sattvaṃ śabdakāryaṃ pratyākhyāya śabdātmanā vyavatiṣṭhamānaṃ rajastamasoḥ śabdabhāvāya vṛttiṃ khyāpayati । rajaḥ śabdakāryaṃ pratyākhyāyetyādi sarvaṃ pūrvavat । ayaṃ tu viśeṣaḥ । rajaḥ sattvatamasoḥ śabdabhāvāya pravṛttiṃ karoti । tamaḥ sattvarajasoḥ śabdabhāvāya pravṛttiṃ vyavasthāpayatīti ॥

<I,144>

[I,144,i]

athānanyatve 'pi kāryakāraṇabhāva iṣyate, evaṃ saty aniṣṭam idam āpadyate iti darśayann āha — sattvādīnāṃ vetyādi । yad ekasmāc chabdād abhinnasvabhāvam, tad abhinnam, śabdasvarūpavat । tathā ca sattvādayaḥ । yad anekasmāt sattvāder abhinnasvabhāvam, tad anekam, sukhādivat । tathā ca śabda iti svabhāvau prasaṅgau । tadviparyayeṇa tu — yad anekam, na tad ekasmāc chabdād abhinnasvabhāvam । yathā bahavaḥ pumāṃsaḥ । tathā ca sattvādi । yad ekam, na tat sattvādibhyo 'bhinnasvabhāvam । yathaikā caitanyavyaktiḥ । tathā ca śabda iti vyāpakaviruddhau । tataś cābhyupetaṃ hīyate । vikalpārtho vāśabda iti kāryakṛnna vety atra yo vāśabdaḥ ॥

[I,144,ii]

ananyatve 'pi na grāhyam ity anekāntam āha । tatparamāṇur iti śabdaparamāṇuḥ । tanmātrādi veti śabdatamnātrādi, ādiśabdenāhaṅkāro mahān pradhānaṃ ca gṛhyate । na cetyādināpy anekāntam āha । yataḥ kāryatvakāraṇādayo nendriyaviṣayād bhidyante, na cendriyadhiyāvasīyante ॥

[I,144,iii]

sarvā syāc citrākāreti । yāpy acitrākāreṣyate sāpi, citratvāt sattvādisamudāyasya । na bhinna ityādinā sādhyābhāve hetor abhāvam āha । tadvaśenetyādi । yadākāraṃ viṣaye jñānam utpadyate, tadākāraḥ sa viṣayaḥ pratīyate । dṛṣṭaṃ cetyādinā hetum āha । yad abhinnākāraṃ grahaṇam, na taccitraviṣayam, caitanyagrahaṇam । vyāpakaviruddhaḥ ॥

<I,145>

[I,145,i]

viṣayāntara itīndriyāntaraviṣayatvenābhimate ॥

[I,145,ii]

nanu cetyādi । sarvatrābhede 'pi sukhādijāter naikendriyatvaprasaṅgaḥ, yataḥ saṃsthānaviśiṣṭān sukhādīn gṛhṇāti । tac ca saṃsthānaṃ viṣayāntare nāsti ॥

[I,145,iii]

anekasaṃsthānabhedeneti nīlapītādisaṃsthānabhedena । naikasaṃsthānānuvṛttir dṛṣṭety anenānuvṛttim adekasaṃsthānābhāvavyavahārāya svabhāvānupalambham āha । sa evetyādi । yataḥ saṃsthānabhedād bhinnendriyagrāhyatvaṃ śabdasparśādijātīnām iṣṭam ekasyām eva ca rūpajātāv anekaṃ saṃsthānam iṣṭam, atas tad evendriyān antyaṃ prasajyate ॥

[I,145,iv]

naiva hi śabdalakṣaṇebhya iti । pūrveṣāṃ kāpilānām ekarūpā eva sarvatra sukhādayaḥ, mādhavas tu sarvatra teṣāṃ bhedam icchati । ye sukhādayaḥ śabdātmanā riṇamanti na sparśādyātmanā, te śabdalakṣaṇaṃ trikam ity ucyante । evaṃ ye sparśātmanaiva pariṇamanti nārthāntarātmanā, te sparśalakṣaṇaṃ trikam iti । evam anyatrāpi jñeyam । nanu trayāṇāṃ saṅghas trikam । tatraikavacanena bhāvyam । tat kathaṃ trikebhya iti । naiṣa doṣaḥ । pratiśabdam anyadanyatrikam । ato <I,146> bahutvātrikāṇāṃ bahuvacanam । anye tv anyathā trikāṇi vyācakṣate । śabdaparamāṇur evaikas trikas tridravyātmakaḥ, sukhādīnām ekatvena piṇḍībhūtatvāt । īdṛśāḥ sarve śabdaparamāṇavaḥ । tathā sparśādiparamāṇava indriyaparamāṇavaś ca veditavyāḥ । ta evāsañcitāḥ prāksṛṣṭeḥ pradhānam ity ucyante । yadā tu sṛṣṭikāle saṃhanyante, tadā vikāravyapadeśaṃ bhajante । ete ca śabdādilakṣaṇāstrikāḥ śrotrādilakṣaṇāś ca parasparato bhinnajātīyā eveti mādhavasya matam ॥

{1.28}

[I,146,i]

anye 'pi ca tasya prakriyābhedo yathoktam — rūpādimat pradhānaṃ sāvayavaṃ karmapūrvikā sṛṣṭiḥ saṃsāraś cānādir vyākhyābhedaḥ svayūthyair mata iti । pūrveṣāṃ kapilaśiṣyāṇāṃ pradhānaṃ na rūpādimat । śakyātmanā tatra rūpādayo vyavasthitā, na vyaktyātmanā । niravayavaṃ ca । na ca karmapūrvikā sṛṣṭiḥ, <I,147> api tu pradhānapūrvikā । saṃsāraś ca śakyātmanā prāksṛṣṭeḥ । na te vyaktyātmanā । mādhavena tu sarvam anyathābhyupagatam । ata evāsau sāṅkhyanāśakaḥ । naiva hītyādinaikendriyaprasaṅgaṃ pariharati, ye sattvādayaḥ śabde hebhyo 'nya eva rūpādyātmanā pariṇamantīti kṛtvā ॥

[I,147,i]

sa cābhinna ityādinānantyaprasaṅgam ॥

[I,147,ii]

spaṣṭatareṇeti । svārtha eva tarappratyayo 'lpāc taram iti yathā । kuta etat । mādhavoktakramasya dūṣyatvenāspaṣṭatvāt, tulyajātīye ca pratiyogini prakarṣapratyayavidhānāt । atha vā paraparikalpitaspaṣṭatvāpekṣayā prakarṣapratyayaḥ ॥

[I,147,iii]

ekaikarūpā iti । kecit sukhasvabhāvā eva, kecic chabdarūpā eva । evaṃ kriyādiparamāṇavo veditavyāḥ । te ca sarvatra deśe kāle ca । etena pradhānadharmakatvam āha । pṛthag ity asaṃhatāḥ samānajātīyair asambaddhā viprakīrṇā ity arthaḥ । ta evaṃvidhāḥ paramāṇavaḥ pradhānam ity ucyante । jātitaḥ sarvagatānām iti । naikam eva paramāṇudravyaṃ sarvagatam asti, kiṃ tu ta eva paramāṇavo 'parisaṅkhyātāḥ sarvatra santi । ekajātīyās teṣāṃ pradhānam ity ākhyātāḥ kariṣyanta iti darśayati ॥

{1.29}

[I,147,iv]

yady evaṃ te paramāṇavo 'tīndriyā, na ca tair vyatiriktaṃ kāryam ārabhyate, tat kathaṃ kāryarūpā lakṣyanta ity āha — kāryarūpās tv ityādi । yathā paraspareṇā<I,148>sambaddhās tuṣāraleśā viyataḥ patanto nopalakṣyante, parasparasaṃyuktās tu haritapatrādau patitāḥ pratyakṣībhavanti, tathā paramaṇavaḥ । samprayogaviśeṣād iti viśeṣagrahaṇaṃ dviparamāṇvādikasya samprayogasya vyavacchedārtham । svajāty anatikrameṇeti śabdādijātyanatikrameṇeti । śabdaparamāṇava eva hi saṃhatāḥ śrotrendriyagrāhyaḥ śando bhavati । tathā sukhaparamāṇava eva sampiṇḍitāḥ svasaṃvedyaṃ sukhaṃ bhavati । na tu saṃhatā vijātīyakāryarūpatāṃ pratipadyante ॥

[I,148,i]

syād etat — trirūpatve 'pi paramāṇūnām ekākārā buddhiḥ pariṇāmaviśeṣād bhaviṣyatīty āha — aṇūnāṃ tv ityādi ॥

[I,148,ii]

sukhādivyatirekeṇeti sukhādyākāram antareṇety arthaḥ । yābhin nety ekarūpā । kuto na yujyata ity āha — anekasvābhāvya iti । atha vā bhinnam anekaṃ svābhāvyam asyeti bahuvrīhiḥ । svabhāva eva svābhāvyam, vartamānasāmīpyavaj jñānākāravaśena hi viṣayasvabhāvo 'vadhāryate । yadi punar anyathāsthite 'pi viṣaye tadupagrāhi jñānam anyākāram iṣyate, na tadvaśena viṣayāvadhāraṇaṃ syāt । tac ceṣṭam tad etena yad ekākāraṃ jñānaṃ na tadbhinnānekasvabhāvaviṣayam, caitanyajñānavat, tathā ca śabdajñānam iti vyāpakaviruddham āha ॥

<I,149>

{1.30}

[I,149,i]

kiṃ kāraṇam iti । trayaḥ saṃyuktā ekasvābhāvyena pariṇaṃsyanti । ataḥ siddhasādhanam ity abhiprāyaḥ । vijātipariṇāmo vilakṣaṇānekasvabhāvānām abhinnaikasvabhāvāpattiḥ । jātibhedād iti kāryakāraṇajātibhedaprasaṅgād ity arthaḥ । tataścāsatkāryavādaḥ syād ity abhyupetahāniḥ । atha vā jātibhedāt sukhādīnām । na hi te bhinnāḥ samprayoge 'py ekasvabhāvatayā pariṇantum arhanti, svajātyanatikrameṇa kāryārambhāt । nanu ca bhinnā api guḍodakādayaḥ pānakādyekasvabhāvatāṃ pratipadyanta ity āha — ekaśabdavācyāstv ityādi । pānakādayo 'pi naiva paramārthataḥ santi, kevalaṃ vyavahāralāghavārthaṃ ta eva guḍādaya ekena śandena vyapariśyante ॥

[I,149,ii]

yad utkaṭam iti yathā svalpasaktuḥ pracuralavaṇasaṃsarge lavaṇarasa eva gṛhyate । jighṛkṣitaṃ veti yathā śvabhiḥ pramamātanau bhakṣyasvabhāvatvam evopalabhyate । tathā śabdādāv api veditavyam ॥

[I,149,iii]

śabdagrahaṇanirapekṣeti । śabdo hi naikaguṇātmakaḥ, kiṃ tarhi triguṇātmakaḥ । tathā ca na gṛhṇātīti tan nirapekṣā ॥

<I,150>

{1.31}

[I,150,i]

sa eva nātmaiko 'syeti śabdasyaikadeśena viṣayatve 'nekātmakatvanivṛttim asambhāvayan pṛcchati — kiṃ kāraṇam iti indriyārthe viśiṣṭo hīti kāraṇam āha । anekarūpe hīti śabdatvaguṇatvasattvādirūpabhedena । sa caika eveti
sukhādīnām anyatamaḥ । tad etena yac chrotreṇa na gṛhyate, na sa tasyārthaḥ, caitanyavat sāmānyadharmajñeyatvādivac ca । tathā ca rūpadvayam iti vyāpakābhāvam āha । evam indriyāntare 'pi vācyam । saktulavaṇasaṃsarge tu gṛhyata eva sakturasaḥ । tathā hy anyādṛśaḥ kevalasya lavaṇasya rasa upalabhyate, anyādṛśaḥ saktusaṃsarge । samānaś ca sparśādiṣv iti tulyaḥ । etena tam evaikendriyaprasaṅgam āha ॥

[I,150,ii]

kathaṃ punar asminn api pakṣe doṣaḥ, yāvatā śabdādiṣu guṇānāṃ bhedo 'bhyupetaḥ । satyam, abhyupagataḥ । sa tu vyaktibhedo na svabhāvabhedaḥ, sarvatra sukhādīnāṃ prakāśakatvādirūpasyāviśiṣṭatvāt । na ca vyaktibhedamātreṇendriyāntaragrāhyatvaṃ yuktam, mā bhūc chabdādīnāṃ vyaktibhedenānantyādanantam indriyam iti । nanu śabdādibhāvenāpi bhedaḥ । naitad asti । trikāṇāṃ hi śabdādibhāvena bhedaḥ, na tu sukhādīnāṃ trirūpatvābhyupagamād ity āha — ayukta ityādi ॥

<I,151>

[I,151,i]

tasmād varam ityādi । nanu siddhāntavyāpādād ayam api duṣṭa eva pakṣaḥ, mādhavapakṣād alpadoṣatvād asyety abhiprāyeṇaivam uktam ity doṣaḥ ॥

{1.32}

[I,151,ii]

vṛttipramāṇasyāvidhānata iti । bāhyeṣv artheṣv indriyaṃ vyavasāyaṃ kurute । tasmiṃs tv indriyavyavasāye mano 'nuvyavasāyaṃ kurute । yathā cendriyavyavasāye mano 'nuvyavasāyaṃ kurute, evaṃ mānasaṃ vyavasāyam indriyaṃ saṃvedayata ity anena granthena parasparasaṃvedanaṃ vṛttidvayasyoktam । tasya pratyakṣatvenāvidhānato na sarvaprameyaviṣayaṃ pramāṇam uktam ity avyāpitā lakṣaṇasya ॥

[I,151,iii]

syād etat — āgamānumānabhyāṃ tadubhayasaṃvedanam । ato 'yam adoṣa ity āha — antareṇetyādi । yadā svasantatipatitāṃ vṛttiṃ saṃvedayate, tadā liṅgābhān nānumānam upadeśābhāvān nāgamaḥ । tasmāt pratyakṣam evedaṃ yuktam ity abhiprāyaḥ ॥

<I,152>

[I,152,i]

nanu śrotrādivṛttiś cety atra caśabdo manovṛttisaṅgrahārtha iti । ato manovṛttes tāvat pratyakṣe 'ntarbhāvaḥ । indriyavṛttayas tu naiva manovṛttisaṃvedikāḥ śāstreṇoktāḥ । tathā hi yathā cendriyavyavasāye mano 'nuvyavasāyaṃ kurute, evaṃ mānasaṃ vyavasāyam indriyaṃ saṃvedayata iti vedayatirayaṃ lābhārthaś curādau paṭhyate । yathā cendriyavyavasāyaṃ manovyavasāyo jānāti, evaṃ mānasaṃ vyavasāyam indriyavṛttiḥ prāpnotīty arthaḥ । naitad asti । caśabdas tāvad iha pramāṇāntarasamuccayārthe 'numānaṃ pramāṇaṃ śrotrādivṛttiś ceti । manovṛttisamuccayārthe tu caśabde 'viśeṣeṇa sarvasyā manovṛtteḥ pratyakṣatvaprasaṅgo viśeṣānupādānāt ॥

[I,152,ii]

yo 'py āha — manasādhiṣṭhiteti manasā saha śrotrādivṛttiḥ pratyakṣam ity artha iti, tasyāpy eṣa eva prasaṅgaḥ ॥

[I,152,iii]

prāptyarthe 'py anyaḥ saṃvedanād ayuktaḥ । prāptir hy abhinnakālayer eva bhavati, na bhinnakālayoḥ । tatra yadi prāptiprasiddhyartham indriyavyavasāyena manovyavasāyasya yaugapadyam iṣyate, tasya viṣayo bāhyārthaḥ syād indriyavyavasāyo vā । yadi pūrvaḥ, dvāradvāribhāvo na syāt, sahotpannasyopakāritvāyogād anupakāriṇaś ca dvārabhāvānupapatteḥ । anyathā manovyavasāyo 'pīndriyavyavasāyasya dvāraṃ syāt । <I,153> yadi ca manaso bāhye 'rthe sākṣād vṛttiḥ, evaṃ satītareṣām indriyāṇāṃ tatra vṛttir apārthikā prāpnoti, manasaiva puruṣārthasya sampāditatvāt । arthendriyavyavasāyas tasya viṣayaḥ, evam apy aviṣayanimitto viṣayī syāt । tac cāyuktam । na nimittasya viṣayatvam upapadyate । anyathā manovyavasāyo 'pīndriyavyavasāyasya viṣayaḥ syāt ॥

[I,153,i]

yas tu manovṛttyāpīndriyavṛtteḥ saṃvedanam icchann āha — naivedaṃ parasparasaṃvedanam anubhavātmakam uktam, kiṃ tarhi prāptisvabhāvam । yathendriyavyavasāyo manovyavasāyena saṃvedyate prāpyate, evaṃ mānasaṃ vyavasāyam indriyaṃ saṃvedayate prāpnoti, tena saha saṅgacchata ity artha iti, so 'py anenaiva nirākṛtaḥ ॥

[I,153,ii]

kiṃ ca tasyāpratyakṣopalambhasyārthadṛṣṭir api na prasidhyati yathoktaṃ prāk । tasmād ayuktā prāptyarthakalpanā ॥

[I,153,iii]

yo 'py āha — śrotrādivṛttir bāhye 'rthe pratyakṣaṃ pramāṇam । tasmiṃs tv indriyavyavasite 'rthe manaḥ paścād vyavasāyaṃ kuruta ity arthaḥ । anyathā yadīndriyavṛttāv eva mānaso vyavasāyaḥ syāt, anuśabdaprayogo 'narthakaḥ syāt, insriyavṛtteḥ kenacit prāg ananubhūtatvāt । atideśo 'py upakāramātrātideśād upapadyate । etad uktaṃ <I,154> bhavati — yathendriyopakārāpekṣaṃ bāhye 'rthe manaḥ pravartate, evaṃ manaupakārāpekṣam indriyam apīti, tasyāpy etad apratyakṣopalambhasya nārthadṛṣṭiḥ prasidhyatīty anenaivāpāstam । tasmāt parasparasaṃvedanam evātrārthāt ॥

[I,154,i]

naiṣa doṣa iti । naivedaṃ vṛttisaṃvedanaṃ pramāṇam iṣyate । smārtaṃ hi tat । yathā kāmakrodhadveṣabhayādayaḥ smaryante, tathendriyavṛttayo manovṛttiś ca manasā । granthaś caivaṃ nīyate — bāhyeṣv indriyaṃ vyavasāyaṃ kurute pratyakṣalakṣaṇam, tasmiṃs tv indriyavyavasāye mano 'nuvyavasāyaṃ kuruta ity anantaraṃ smārtam । yathā cendriyavyavasāye mano 'nuvyavasāyaṃ kurute 'nantaroktam, evaṃ mānasaṃ vyavasāyam indriyaṃ saṃvedayate smārayatīty arthaḥ, anekārthatvād dhātūnām । dvitīyaś ca hetumaṇṇij iha veditavyaḥ । indriyaṃ hi smaraṇānukūlaṃ manasa upakāraṃ kurvat tatprayuṅkta iveti । smaraṇenaiva ca vṛttiviṣayīkaraṇe 'rthadṛṣṭiḥ prasidhyatīti manyate । tad evaṃ vṛttigrahaṇasyāpramāṇatvān na tasyāsaṅgrahān nyūnatvam ॥

<I,155>

[I,155,i]

yathoktam iti । vṛttisaṃvedanasya smārtatvajñāpakam āha — smṛtipratyakṣavyavasāyaviśeṣa iti । viśeṣaśabdaḥ pratyekam abhisambadhyate ॥

[I,155,ii]

nanu cānyārtha evāyaṃ granthaḥ śāstra upanyastaḥ । tat katham anena smārtatvaṃ jñāpyate । tathā hi kim indriyamanobhyāṃ sahaiva bāhyeṣv artheṣu vyavasāyāḥ kriyanta āhosvit saha naiva kriyanta iti saṃśaya idam uktam — bāhyeṣv artheṣv indriyaṃ vyavasāyaṃ kurute । tasmiṃs tv indriyavyavasāye mano 'nuvyavasāyaṃ kurute । kasmāt । asti hy ayaṃ smṛtipratyakṣavyavasāyaviśeṣa iti । etad uktaṃ bhavati — smṛtipratyakṣavyavasāyaviśeṣo 'sti । nāyaṃ prasiddhataro 'pahnotuṃ śakyate । na cobhayor bāhyārthapravṛttāv ayam upapadyate । yadi hi bāhye 'rthe manaḥ pravartate nendriyavṛttiṣu, tadā tā manovṛttibhir anadhiṣṭhitāḥ pauruṣeyeṇa caitanyenāsampṛktā apratyayāḥ syuḥ । tataś ca kathaṃ pratyakṣaṃ pramāṇam ucyeran । na hy apratyayā vṛttayaḥ pratyakṣaṃ pramāṇaṃ bhavanti । pratyakṣābhāvāc ca smṛtir api tatpūrvikā na syāt । yadā tv indriyavyavasāye mano 'nuvyavasāyaṃ kurute, tadā smṛtipratyakṣavyavasāyaviśeṣa upapadyate । tathā hi sāmprate kāle bāhyeṣv artheṣv indriyavyavasāyaṃ pravṛttam anvadhyavasyati । manasīndriyavyavasāyaḥ svaviṣayābhāso <I,156> manovyavasāyena sampṛktaḥ pauruṣeṇa pratyayena sapratyayo bhavati । evaṃ pratyakṣavyavasāyas tasyendriyasya bhavati । pratyakṣatvaṃ tasyendriyavyavasāyasya bhavatīty arthaḥ । kevalasya tu pratyakṣavyavasāyāt paścāt smṛtivyavasāyo manaso bhavatīti । tathā coktam — kevalaṃ tv atītānāgatayoḥ kālayoḥ pravartata iti ॥

[I,156,i]

nanu cendriyavyavasāyasahitasya bāhye 'py arthe pravṛttasya sāmprate kāle manasaḥ pratyakṣavyavasāyo bhaviṣyati, kevalasya tu paścāt smṛtivyavasāyaḥ । naitad asti । evaṃ bāhyārthagrahaṇe sati dvayor apy ekārthakāritvādānarthakyam indriyāṇāṃ syāt । tathā hy uktam — naikārthakāriṇor indriyayoḥ kalpane sāmarthyam iti । yata evaṃ smṛtipratyakṣavyavasāyaviśeṣo bāhyārthe pravṛttau manaso nopapadyate, tasmāt — tasmiṃs tv indriyavyavasāye mano 'nuvyavasāyaṃ kurute, na bāhyeṣv artheṣv iti । tad evam — nendriyamanobhyāṃ saha bāhyeṣv artheṣu vyavasāyāḥ kriyanta ity asyārthasya pratipādānāya — asti hy ayam ityādir grantha upanyastaḥ, na tu vṛttisaṃvedanasya smārtatvapratipādānāya । tat katham — tat smārtatvajñāpakatvenokta iti । na cedaṃ vṛttisaṃvedanaṃ sāṅkhyasya smārtaṃ jñānam abhīṣṭam । anubhūtapūrvaṃ <I,157> hi smaryate । vṛttisaṃvedanaṃ cedam aprūva cedam apūrva evānubhavaḥ । tat katham idaṃ parābhiprāyeṇoktam — smārtaṃ hi tadvṛttisaṃvedanam iti । parasya gatyantarābhāvāt । tathā hi vṛttyupalabhyas tāvan niyatam abhyupeyaḥ, anyathā tadanupalambhe 'rthopalambho 'pi na syād ity andhamūkaṃ jagat syāt । na ca vṛttisaṃvedanaṃ pratyakṣādiṣv antarbhavati । ato gatyantarābhāvād idam apy asaduttaraṃ brūyād ity āśaṅkyaivam uktam ॥

[I,157,i]

indriyavṛttau tv anataram iti । indriyavṛttigrahaṇena manovṛttir api gṛhyate ॥

[I,157,ii]

smārto nānanubhūtatvād ityādinā — yad ananubhūtam, na tatra smārtaḥ pratyayo bhavati । tad yathā santānāntarīyeṣv ananubhūteṣu । ananubhūtāś cendriyavṛttaya iti kāraṇaviruddham āha ॥

[I,157,iii]

yugapaddve ityādi । yadi smārtatvaprasiddhaye hetor asiddhatvam iṣyate । evaṃ hi sahabhūbhyām indriyamanovyavasāyābhyāṃ parasparaṃ saṃvedane tāsu smārtaḥ pratyayaḥ sambhavaty anantaram ॥

<I,158>

[I,158,i]

evaṃ ceti । viṣaya indriyavyavasāyo grāhyo viṣayiṇo grāhakasya manovyavasāyasya । manovyavasāyo 'pi viṣayo grāhyo viṣayiṇo grāhakasyendriyavyavasāyasya । parasparasaṃvedane hi tayor apekṣayā viṣayatvaṃ ca bhavati viṣayatvaṃ ca । tayor nimittanimittibhāva iṣyate parasparam । na hy anyathā viṣayaviṣayitvaṃ sambhavati । na ca yugapadutpannayor nimittanimittatvam upapadyate ॥

{1.33}

[I,158,ii]

sa ceti । abhyupety doṣāntaram āha । yo 'sāv indiryavṛttyanubhavo yat pūrvakaḥ smārtaḥ pratyayaḥ, sa pramāṇaṃ nokta iti saiva nyūnatā । kāmādiṣu tarhi kathaṃ smārta ity āha — svasaṃvedyatvād ityādi । etenaitat sūcayati — kāmādyupanyāsaḥ svabādhāya kṛtyotthāpanam । tathā hy asmākaṃ svasaṃvedyatvena kāmādīnām abhyupagamāt, tatra smārtaḥ sambhavati । bhavatas tu tathā teṣām anabhyupagamāt, tadasambhava eva । atha svasaṃvittir abhyupeyate, sāpi tarhi lakṣaṇenāsaṅgṛhīteti saiva nyūnatā । nanu ca śāstreṇa smārtatvaṃ pratipāditam ity āha — andhapadam evaitad iti । yathāndhapadasyādarśanapūrvo vinyāsaḥ, tathāsyāpi, pramāṇenāparicchidyābhidhānāt । atha vān dhāni padāny anunmīlitārthāni <I,159> yatra vākye, tat tathoktam । tathā hītyādināndhapadhapadatvaṃ darśayati । indriyārthe 'pi smārto na sambhavati yo 'nubhūtaḥ, kiṃ punarvṛttiṣv ananubhūtāsv ity apiśabdasyārthaḥ ॥ syād etat — tasmiṃs tv indriyavyavasāye sati bāhya evārthe mano 'nuvyavasāyaṃ kuruta iti śāstrārthaḥ । tato 'nanubhūtatvam asiddham ity āha — hānir vetyādi । hāniḥ śāstrasyānyadarśane smaraṇam, indriyavṛttyānubhūtatvān manasā ca smaryamāṇatvāt । tac cāyuktam । na hi devadattānubhūtaṃ yajñadattaḥ smarati । svamate tarhi katham indriyajñānānubhūtaṃ manasā smaryata iti cet, parasyaivāyaṃ doṣaḥ, yasyedaṃ matam — nānyenānubhūtam anyaḥ smaratīti । asmākaṃ tu — ekasantatau jñānāntarānubhūtam api smaryata iti samaya ity adoṣaḥ ॥

[I,159,i]

ananubhūte vā smārta iti । atha manasaivānubhūtasya smaraṇam iṣyate, evaṃ saty ananubhūte 'rthe smaraṇaṃ syāt, tasya mansā pūrvam ananubhūtatvāt — dvitīye kṣaṇe mānasa iṣyata iti । ata indriyavṛttisahaja ity āha ॥

<I,160>

[I,160,i]

yad uktam ityādi । śātra uktam । kiṃ bāhyeṣv artheṣv indriyamanobhyāṃ sahavyavasāyāḥ । nety ucyate । kasmāt । naikārthakāriṇor indriyayoḥ kalpane sāmarthyam iti । etad uktaṃ bhavati — yadīndriyamanobhyāṃ dvābhyām api bāhyasyārthasya grahaṇalakṣaṇaṃ kāryam ekārthakāritvam iṣyate, evaṃ sati sāmarthyam indriyāṇāṃ na syāt, arthavattā na syād ity arthaḥ । tayor api bāhyārthagrahaṇam atraikārthakāritvam । bāhyārthagrahaṇāc ca dvābhyām apīndriyāṇām arthavattā na syāt । katham । yadi tāvad viṣaye pravartamānaṃ mana indriyavṛttikṛtam anugrahaṃ nāpekṣate, evaṃ satīndriyāṇāṃ sarvathaivānarthakyaṃ syāt, manasaiva bāhyārthopasaṃhārāt puruṣasyopabhogasiddheḥ । indriyavṛttayaś ca bāhyārthābhāsā mānasair avyavasāyair anadhyavasitās tair asampṛktā apratyayāḥ syuḥ ॥

[I,160,ii]

yac cedaṃ dvāradvārivicāre paṭhyate — manasyekībhūtān indritavyavasāyān puruṣaś cetayate, na tv indriyavyavasāyair manovyavasāyān iti । tasmān mana eva dvāri dvārāṇīndriyāṇīti, tad api vyāhanyate, yugapad ekārthakāritve dvayor api dvāradvāritvaprasaṅgāt । andhādīnām api ca rūpādiviṣayaṃ pratyakṣaṃ syāt ॥

[I,160,iii]

athāpi — indriyakṛtam anugraham apekṣya bāhye 'rthe manaḥ pravartate na kevalam asāmarthyād ity ucyate, evam api naivendriyāṇāṃ sāmarthyaṃ syāt, yasmād evam iṣyamāṇe sapratyayāyā vṛtter asambhavaḥ syāt । indriyavṛttau pradīpaprabhāyām iva hi <I,161> sahakāritvenāvasthatāyāṃ mana eva bāhye 'rthe grahaṇāya pravartate । tatra — yathā pradīpaprabhāyāṃ satyāṃ cakṣuṣo vṛttiḥ, pradīpaprabhā tu sahakāriṇy eva kevalam, tathendriyavṛttau manaso bāhye 'rthe grahaṇāya vṛttiḥ, indriyavṛttis tu sahakāriṇy eva । sā ca manovṛttyāgṛhyamāṇāsampṛktā tayāpratyayaiva sarvadā syāt । indriyavyavasāyānāṃ ca manasyekībhāvād arthavattvam uktam, nānyathā । tena te yadi manovyavasāyair anuvyavasīyante, evaṃ manasyekībhavantaḥ pauruṣeṇa saṃvedyante । tataś ca tena sampṛktās tadrūpatām ivāpannāḥ prāmāṇyaṃ pratipadyante । anyathā teṣāṃ prāmāṇyam eva na syāt ॥

[I,161,i]

yeṣām apy apratyayā vṛttiḥ prāmāṇyenābhimatā, sapratyayā tu phalam, teṣām api yathoktena prakāreṇa sapratyayāyā vṛtter asambhavāt phalābhāvaḥ । tadabhāvāc ca pramāṇasyāpy abhāvaḥ । na hi niṣphalaṃ pramāṇaṃ yuktam ity eke ॥

[I,161,ii]

cakṣur manasor dvāradvāribhāvān naite ekārthakāriṇī kalpayitum asmākaṃ sāmarthyam asti, yugapad ekārthakāritve dvayor api dvāradvāritvaprasaṅgād ity anye ॥

[I,161,iii]

naiṣa doṣa ityādinaitat pratipādayati । neti yo 'yaṃ pratiṣedhaḥ, tena na sahavyavasāyakriyāmātraṃ pratiṣidhyate, kiṃ tu niyamavatī yā sahavyavasāyakriyā, <I,162> sā pratiṣidhyate manasaḥ smārtādhikavyavasāyapradarśanārtham । na sahaiva, api tu paścād api smārto vyavasāyo 'dhiko manasā kriyata iti ॥

[I,162,i]

saha tu siddha evetyādinaitad āha । niyamarahitāṃ sahavyavasāyakriyāṃ prati praśna eva nopapadyate, tasyāḥ prāg eva jñātatvāt । tasmād gamyate — kiṃ sahaiva kriyante, pṛthakkriyanta evety evam ayaṃ praśnaḥ pravṛttaḥ, na tu kiṃ saha kriyante, āhosvinna saha kriyanta iti । kuta etat — saha tu siddha eva vyavasāye paśna ity āha — sāmprate kāla ityādi । śāstre śnotrādīnāṃ svaviṣayaviniveśaṃ sāmpratakālavṛttitvaṃ ca pratipādyaivam uktam । tathā — manaḥ sarvārtheṣu traikālyaṃ pravartate । bāhyeṣv artheṣu sāmprate kāle kenacid indriyeṇa yuktaṃ yadā mano bhavati, tadā pratyayavatī vṛttir indriyasya bhavati । kevalaṃ tv atītānāgatayor ityādi prāg uktam, paścād ayaṃ paśnaḥ kṛtaḥ । atra kenacid indriyeṇa yuktaṃ yadeti vacanāt siddhaḥ pūrvam eva sahavyavasāyaḥ । tato — niyamavatīṃ sahavyavasāyakriyām ārabhya paśnaḥ । pratyuttaram api ca — naikārthakāriṇor indriyayoḥ kalpane sāmarthyam astīti tatpratiṣedham eva pratīti gamyate । tato na śāstrahāniḥ ॥

<I,163>

[I,163,i]

tasya vyāghāta iti kathaṃ kṛtvā । yato yathā cendriyavyavasāya ityādinā parasparavṛttisaṃvedanaṃ pratipāditam । avaśyaṃ caitad evaṃ vijñeyam । arthāntarakalpane hi yathoktadoṣaprasaṅgaḥ syāt । tataś ca na kalpayitavyam — indriyapravṛttisahajo bāhye 'rthe manaso 'nubhavaḥ paścāt smārta iti ॥

[I,163,ii]

apārthikā prāpnotīti doṣāntaram āha । manasetyādinātraiva hetum । trikālaviṣayaṃ sarvārthaṃ ca mana ity uktam । tac ced abāhyārthe sākṣāt pravartate, tenaiva puṃso 'rthaḥ kṛta iti śrotrādīnāṃ vaiyarthyaṃ syāt । tataś ca naiva tadātmanā prakṛteḥ pariṇatiḥ syāt । pauruṣautsukyanivṛttaye hi tasyāḥ pariṇāma iṣyate । anyathā prāptakaivalye 'pi puṃsi syād iti ॥

{1.34}

[I,163,iii]

satsamprayoga ityādi । asya sambandhaḥ — athāto dharmajijñāseti prastuty āha — tasya nimittaparīṣṭiḥ । tasya dharmasyopalabdhinimittāni pramāṇāni parīkṣyante । tatra pratyakṣeṇa tāvad dharmo nopalabhyata iti darśayann āha — satsamprayoga ityādi ॥

<I,164>

[I,164,i]

sataḥ satā vā samprayoga iti vigrahaḥ । sampragrahaṇaṃ sampratyutkarṣeṇa ca yo yogas tasya jñāpanārtham । evaṃ cātmādibhir api yo yogaḥ sasaṃskāra upagṛhīto bhavati । anyathā sadyoga ity etāvad eva brūyāt । samprayoga indriyāṇām arthena sambandhaḥ sannikarṣo vyāpārātiśayo vā, yatrotpanne buddhir utpadyate । satsamprayoga ity asyendriyāṇām ity anena sambandhaḥ । puruṣasyety asyāpi buddhijanmety anena । indriyaśabdena mano 'pi gṛhyate । tenātmamanaḥsamprayogādyadātmaviṣayaṃ buddhijanma, tasyāpi pratyakṣatvaṃ vihitaṃ bhavati । buddhijanmeti ca karmadhārayaḥ ṣaṣṭhītatpuruṣo vā । yadā karmadhārayaḥ, tadā janmaviśiṣṭā buddhiḥ pratyakṣam । buddhir hi janmanaiva viṣayaṃ prakāśayati । na tu janmavyatirekeṇa vyāpārāntaraṃ tasyāḥ samasti, kṣaṇikatvād iti jñāpanārthaṃ janmagrahaṇam । yadā tu ṣaṣṭhīsamāsaḥ, tadā buddhiviśiṣṭaṃ janma pratyakṣam ॥

[I,164,ii]

tatra sad ity asadvyudāsāyetyādinā yat samprayogād gamyate, na tasya pratyāyanāya sacchabda upādeyaḥ । samprayogavat । tathā cādadvyudāsa iti vyāpakaviruddham āha । sata eveti । dviṣaṭhatvāt tasyānyatarābhāve 'sambhavāt ।

<I,165>

[I,165,i]

nanu sata evety evakārād eva niyamasya gatatvān niyamād iti na vācyam । athaitad ucyate, evaśrutir apārthikā syāt । naiṣa doṣaḥ । niyamasyaiva hi svarūpam evaśabdena dyotyate । vākyabhedaṃ ca kṛthaivaṃ vyākhyeyam — sata eveti yo 'yaṃ niyamaḥ, asmān niyamāt sata eva samprayogo bhavatīti । atha ca niyamān na satprayogo yukta iti sambandhaḥ kartavyaḥ, naiva satprayogo yukta ity evaṃ vā ॥

{1.35}

[I,165,ii]

pratiyogyathetyādi । anyathārthatvād sacchabdasya siddhasādhanam āha । kim arthaṃ punaḥ prāk sata eveti bruvatā ṣaṣṭhīsamāso darśitaḥ, idānīṃ tu kena samprayoga iti tṛtīyāsamāsaḥ । samāsāntare 'py eṣa doṣa iti sūcanārtham । tathā hi śabareṇa sati samprayoge, nāsatīti bruvatā karmadhārayo 'yam iti vyākhyātam । tatrāpi cāyam anivāryo doṣaḥ, yat saptam yeṣā nimittārthā syāt, yasya ca bhāvena bhāvalakṣaṇam ity anena vā । na cāsato nimittatvaṃ lakṣaṇatvaṃ ca sambhavati । tataś ca yadi samprayogena samittena buddhijanma bhavati, tadbhāvena vā tādbhāvo lakṣyate, evaṃ sati samprayogaḥ sann ity etad gamyata eva ॥

[I,165,iii]

syād etat — satyam, gamyate, tathāpi yeṣāṃ pareṣām asatkalpanātītānāgataviṣayaṃ yogijñānam asaty api samprayoge bhavatīti, tan nirākaraṇārthaṃ sadgraha<I,166>ṇam iti । ayuktam etat, saptam yan tenaiva samprayogaśabdena sadarthāvyabhicāriṇāsyāḥ kalpanāyā nivāritatvāt । api cāsmākaṃ yogijñāṃ sadviṣayam eva prāg evākhyātam ॥

[I,166,i]

yad apy atītānāgataviṣayaṃ yogināṃ jñānam ucyate, tasyāpy upacārād atītānāgataviṣayatvam abhyupeyate । paramārthatas tu tad api vartamānaviṣayam eva । kathaṃ kṛtvā । pratyutpanno hi bhāvo 'tītānāṃ hetupratyayānāṃ sākṣāt pāramparyeṇa vopakāryaḥ । yad anantaraṃ yasyotpādaḥ, tasya sākṣāt, yebhyas tu vyavadhānena, teṣāṃ pāramparyeṇa । anāgatānāṃ cāsau bhāvānām upakārakaḥ । ye 'nantaraṃ tato bhavanti bhāvāḥ, teṣāṃ sākṣāt । tad uttarakālabhāvināṃ tu pāramparyeṇa । yac cāsyātītopakāryatvam anāhatopakāritvaṃ ca vyavahitam itarac ca, so 'sya svabhāvaḥ । taṃ ca pratyutpannaṃ bhāvaṃ bhāvanāprakarṣaparyantajena jñānena yoginaḥ paricchindantaḥ <I,167> sarvātmanaiva paricchin danti, tasya niravayavatvāt । evaṃ paricchinne tasmin samādhivyutthitānāṃ yogināṃ ye tasya bhāvasyopakārakā upakāryāś cārthā atītānāgatāḥ, tat pratyavamarśīni jñānāny avisaṃvādīni bhāvanāmayajñānaviśeṣabalād upajāyante, yair atītānāgatapadārthavyavasthā kriyate । tad evam atītānāgarārthaviṣayaṃ pratyavamarśajñānaṃ yogijñānasya kāryam iti kāraṇe kāryopacārāt tad apy atītānāgataviṣayam ity ucyate । bhavatu nāma tan nirviṣayam eva, paramārthato 'tītānāgatayor asattvāt, tathāpi tasya sphuṭātītānāgatārthapratibhāsasyāvikalpatvād avisaṃvāditvāc ca pratyakṣatvam aviruddham eva । yathā hi bhavadbhiś codanājanitāyā buddher anāgatadharmaviṣayāyā rūpāgrahe 'py avisaṃvādāt prāmāṇyam iṣyate, tathāsmābhir api yathoktāt kāraṇāt tasya pratyakṣatvam । sphuṭātītādyarthapratibhāsitvaṃ punas tasya nirvikalpatvam avisaṃvāditvaṃ ca yogabalāt, karmadevatādyadhiṣṭhānabalāt satyasvapnadarśanavat । tato niṣprayojanaṃ sad ity etad akāryam eva ॥

<I,168>

[I,168,i]

nanu ca naivedaṃ pratyakṣalakṣaṇam, kiṃ tu dharmaḥ kaiścid yogijñānapratyakṣādilakṣaṇa uktaḥ । tat pratiṣedhārtham idam uktam । codanālakṣaṇo 'rtho dharmaḥ, na pratyakṣalakṣaṇaḥ । kutaḥ । yasmāt tad īdṛśaṃ pratyakṣam, bhaviṣyaṃś ca dharmo na jñānakāle 'sti, tato 'nimittam atīndriyasyārthasyāvabodhane, vidyamānopalambhanatvāt tasya । tat pūrvakatvāc cānumānādy api dharmasyānimittaṃ bhavati । tasmāc codanālakṣaṇa evārtho dharma ity etad atra pradhānaṃ vidheyam । na tu pratyakṣalakṣaṇapradhānam idaṃ pratyakṣasūtram । pratyakṣasya siddhatvād anuvādamātram evedaṃ kriyata iti । tad ayuktam, asiddhatvāt pramāṇānām । etac ca prāg eva pratipāditam । api ca yadi siddhatvāt pratyakṣasya nānena lakṣaṇaṃ vidhīyate, kiṃ tadīty etāvad eva <I,169> dharmasyānimittatvam, evaṃ sati pratyakṣam animittam, vidyamānopalambhanatvād ity etāvad eva vaktavyam । syād etat — svarūpanirdeśe saty evaṃlakṣaṇaṃ pratyakṣam iti svarūpavijñānāt tasyānimittatvaṃ sidhyati, nānyatheti । yadi svarūpanirdeśam antareṇa tasya svarūpaṃ na jñāyate, na tarhi tat siddham । tataś ca tasya lakṣaṇavidher evāśrita iti na dūṣaṇān mucyase ॥

[I,169,i]

viśiṣṭo 'kṣasya kathyatām iti । indriyasya hi viśiṣṭa eva viṣayaḥ pratiyogī, yathā cakṣuṣo rūpam ity evamādi । ata evaṃ vaktuṃ yuktam — rūpādisamprayoga iti ॥

[I,169,ii]

athāpi syād iti । ātmendriyamano 'rthasannikarṣāj jñānam utpadyate । sa ca rūpādiśabdair na śakyate vaktum । atas tat pratītaye sadgrahaṇam iti । indriyāṇām iti tu vacanam upalakṣaṇārtham, kākebhyo dadhi rakṣyatam iti yatheti manyate ॥

<I,170>

[I,170,i]

sanmātram ityādinā pūrvakam eva sādhanaṃ sūcayati ॥

[I,170,ii]

syād etat — asati tasyāvṛttir ity asad etat । tathā hy asatām api mṛgatṛṣṇādīnāṃ samprayogo dṛṣṭaḥ । tataś cāsiddho hetur ity āha — ye 'pi hītyādi । pratyakṣābhāsaviṣayatvāt pratyakṣābhāsāḥ । ata evāsantaḥ । tato na taiḥ saha kasyacit samprayogaḥ । tataś ca na tan niṣedhāya sadgrahaṇaṃ yuktam iti ॥

[I,170,iii]

syād etat — asati sadgrahaṇe dvicandrādijñānasyāpi bhrāntasya pratyakṣatā syāt । atas tan nivṛttaye sadgrahaṇam iti । naitad asti, tasya samprayogagrahaṇenaiva nivartatvād ity uktam etat । yadi tarhi tair na samprayogaḥ, kathaṃ jalādipratibhāsaṃ vijñānam ity āha — deśaviśeṣe tv ityādi । marujāṅgalādau deśaviśeṣe । tatrāpi na sarvadā, kiṃ tarhi yadā sūryaraśmibhiḥ santāpitā bhavanti, tadā kāraṇaṃ bhavanti, nānyadā yad āha — sūryopatāpād iti । avyapadeśyā iti svalakṣaṇasyāvyapadeśyatvāt । krameṇeti । prāg indriyajñānam । tataḥ sādṛśyāvasayī manovikalpaḥ । tato jalādisadṛśavastusmaraṇam । tadantaraṃ tad evedam iti bhrāntaṃ manovijñānaṃ sāmānyālambi bhavati । <I,171> vināpi tadartheneti jalādinā kalpitena, samanantarapratyayaviśeṣavaśenaivotpatteḥ ॥

{1.36}

[I,171,i]

athetyādinā viśiṣṭa eva vyutpattisamāśrayeṇa kathita iti darśayati । yo vā yasyeti praśaṃsāyām api sacchabdo vartat, satpuruṣa iti yathā ॥

[I,171,ii]

tat sīdaty anyad apy atreti । yathā hy asty arthaḥ sacchabda indriyārthavyabhicārān nālam indriyārthapratyāyanāya tathā sadanārtho 'pi । tathā hīnndriyāntarārthā api rajaḥprabhṛtaya indriye sīdanti । prabhṛtiśabdena karṇād imālādayo gṛhyante । añjanādīnām api copakāritvāt praśastatā vidyate । atas tat samprayoge 'pi pratyakṣatā syāt ॥

[I,171,iii]

nanu yo yasminn indriye sīdati, anyatrāvṛtter iti vacanāt tasyaivendriyasya viṣayabhāvopagamanalakṣaṇaṃ sadnam atra vivakṣitam । praśaṃsārtho 'py atra yogyatvenoktaḥ । yogyatvaṃ cehendriyasya viṣayabhāvopagamanasāmarthyam eva vaktum iṣṭam । na caivam prakāraṃ sadanādi rajaḥprabhṛtīnām asti । tat kuto 'yaṃ prasaṅgaḥ ।

<I,172>

[I,172,i]

uktam atra — asty artha iva sacchabdaḥ sadanādyartho 'pi nālaṃ viśeṣapratipādanāyeti । yadi caivam prakāram iha sadanādyābhipretam. tataḥ samprayogaśandena nārthaḥ, sati yad abuddhijanma tat pratyakṣam ity etāvataiva samprayogasyāpi labdhatvāt । na hi tena vinaivaṃvidhaṃ sadanādi tvam atyā sambhavati । tasmāt saṃśleṣaḥ sadanam upakāritvaṃ ca praśastatvam eṣṭavyam । tataś ca rajaḥprabhṛtiṣu prasaṅgaḥ ॥

[I,172,ii]

kiṃ punar atrāniṣṭam । yadi hi rajaḥprabhṛtibhiś cakṣurādīndriyasamprayogād rajaḥprabhṛtiviṣayā buddhir nopajāyate, naivāyaṃ doṣaḥ, buddhijanma pratyakṣam iti vacanāt । yac ca tat samprayogād vijñānaṃ jāyate tadviṣayam, tad iṣyata eva pratyakṣam । naiṣa doṣaḥ । na hy atra rajaḥprabhṛtibhiḥ samprayogāt tadviṣayendriyajñānasyotpannasya pratyakṣatā prasajyate, kiṃ tarhi pratyakṣajñānasyotpattiḥ । etad uktaṃ bhavati — yadi ya indriye sīdati tasya vā praśastaḥ, sa indriyārthaḥ, rajaḥprabhṛtayo 'py evaṃvidhāḥ । tat tat samprayoge 'pi pratyakṣaṃ jñānam utpadyeteti ॥

{1.37–1.38b}

[I,172,iii]

naivaṃ bhaviṣyatītyādinā sacchabda indriyārtha eva rūḍhaḥ, tad vyutpattau viśiṣṭasyaivārthasambandhinaḥ sadanāder āśrayaṇāt । yathā gośabdo gojātāv evānanya<I,173>sādhāraṇaṃ gamanam āśritya vyutpādita iti darśayati । viṣama upanyāsa iti dṛṣṭāntadārṣṭāntikayor vaiṣamyāt । rūḍhibalena hi viśeṣam āśritya vyutpattiḥ kriyate । na ca sacchrutir indriyārthe rūḍhety asad etat ॥

[I,173,i]

tan nairantaryasya bādhakam iti । samprayogo nairantaryam । yadi hītyādinā sarvārthasamprayogaśruter artham āha । nanu ca samprayogaśrutyā vyāpāraviśeṣaḥ pratyāyyate, tat kuto 'yaṃ doṣaḥ । kaḥ punar indriyasya vyāpāraḥ । yadi grahaṇam, cakṣurvijñānam antareṇāpi cakṣurvijñānasya sadbhāvāt । atha prakāśanam, cakṣuṣa eva taijasatvenābhimatatvāt tasyaiva prakāśanaṃ syāt, na śeṣāṇām । śrotrasya vākāśasvabhāvasya niṣkriyatvāt kuto vyāpāraḥ । samprayogagrahaṇaṃ ca vyartham । avaśyaṃ hi buddhijanmani karaṇānāṃ vyāpāreṇa bhāvyam । na ca loke samprayogaśrutir vyāpārārthā pratītā । prasiddhārthagrahaṇaṃ ca sūtre 'bhyupetam । tenāyaṃ pakṣo 'tyantam ayukta iti sannikarṣapakṣa evāśrayaṇīyaḥ । tataś ca yathoktam aniṣṭaṃ prasajyata iti ॥

<I,174>

{1.38c–1.39a'}

[I,174,i]

vṛttikāro buddhijanmeti sopaskāraṃ vākyaṃ vyācaṣṭa ity ata idam āha — buddhikāraṇasāmagrīm ityādi । seti guṇabhūtāpi buddhiḥ parāmṛṣyate, na tu sāmagrī, tadvyatiriktasya strīliṅgasyopanyāsād vṛttau ca tathāvivaraṇāt । saṃskāro dharmādharmau, ātmaguṇo vā jñānajo jñānahetuḥ, saṃskāraviśeṣeṇa jñānaviśeṣotpādāt । anyad ityādinā yad asat, na tat pratyakṣam, khapuṣpavat । tathā ca sāmagrīvyatirikto hetur iti vyāpakābhāvam āha ॥

{1.39b–1.40b}

[I,174,ii]

buddhijanmeti kiṃ punar ity anenāpi yad anarthakam, na tat kartavyam, tadanyānarthakavat । tathā ca buddhijanmagrahaṇam iti vyāpakaviruddham ॥

[I,174,iii]

syād etat — asati tasminn abuddhijanmahetor api samprayogasya pratyakṣatā syāt । ataḥ samprayogaviśeṣaṇārthaṃ tat kartavyam iti । asad etat । na hi sannikarṣasya buddhijanmāhetutvaṃ sambhavati । kāryeṇa hi tasyāstitvam anumīyate । tad abhāve kutas tasyāvagatiḥ jaiminīyaiḥ kriyānumeyeṣyate, kiṃ punar atīndriyāṇām indriyāṇām । kathaṃ ca bhinnavibhaktiviśeṣaṇaṃ samānādhikaraṇaṃ syāt samprayoge buddhijanmeti । atha vyadhikaraṇaṃ viśeṣaṇaṃ rājeva puruṣasya, tadā samprayoga eva buddhijanmano viśeṣaṇaṃ syād ity asāram etat ॥

<I,175>

[I,175,i]

kiṃ cetyādinā yad akṣaṃ prati na vartate, na tat pratyakṣam, abhimatāpratyakṣavat । tathā ca yathoktā sāmagrīti vyāpakābhāvam āha । saṃskāravān iti saṃskārasahitaḥ ॥

{1.40c–1.41b}

[I,175,ii]

manaindriyasannikarṣa indriyārthasannikarṣaś cākṣaṃ prati vartata ity ataḥ saivety āha — yo 'pi hi kalpayed iti । tasyābhiprāyaḥ — indriyasannikarṣa eva jñānasyāsādhāraṇaṃ kāraṇam । ataḥ sa eva yato buddhijanmety atra sarvanāmnā hetutvena parāmṛṣṭaḥ । tasya cākṣaṃ prati vṛtteḥ pratyakṣavyapadeśo yujyata iti । tasyāpi dviṣṭhatvād iti । indriyaviṣayavartitvād dviṣṭhatvam । anena ca tasya nendriyam evāsādhāraṇaṃ kāraṇam iti darśitam । tathā hi dviṣṭhatvāt tasya yathendriyāntaraṃ na kāraṇam, evaṃ viṣayāntaram api । yathā ca viṣayasyānyenān indriyeṇāpi yogaḥ, evam indriyasyāpy anyenāviṣayeṇāpīty aviśeṣaḥ । asādhāraṇena ca loke vyapadeśo dṛṣṭa ity uktaṃ prāk । tato nendriyeṇaiva vyapadeṣṭavyam ity āha — akalpaneyam iti ॥

[I,175,iii]

yato yan niścaya ityādi । yato buddhijanma, tat pratyakṣam ity asyedaṃ bhāṣyam । etad uktaṃ bhavati — yata indriyādisamprayogān niścayajñānaṃ jāyate <I,176> gaurevāyam ityādi, tat pratyakṣam iti । tad apy ayuktam iti, indriyādisamprayogād asambhavād evaṃvidhajñānasya । katham ity āha — gotvādiyogād ityādi । caśabdo hetau । yasmād gotvādiviśeṣaṇasambandhād artho gotvāditvena niścīyate, na cendriyadhiyo viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayojane sāmarthyam, ato 'sambhavo lakṣaṇasyety ayuktam ॥

[I,176,i]

tvan matyeti । yataḥ pareṇa gotvādayas tadāśrayaś ca dravyaṃ vastutvenābhyupetam, atas tadviśeṣayatendriyabuddher āśakyeta । anusandhāne tu viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayor vastusator api nendriyadhiyaḥ śaktiḥ । tathā hi gandho rūpīndriyaviṣayo dravyaṃ ca paramatena, tathāpi na tayoḥ parasparānusandhāne tasyāḥ sāmarthyam abhyupeyate । surabhi dravyam iti hi yadi cakṣurvijñānam etat, na gandhaviṣayam । atha ghnāṇavijñānam, dravyaviṣayatvānupapattiḥ । svamatena tu jātidravyayor apy asattvād asadālocanam iti darśanāya tvan matyety uktam ॥

[I,176,ii]

nanu ca kaṇabhukparīkṣāyām ukta evāyam arthaḥ — viṣayālocanārthatvān na sandhānaṃ viśeṣaṇair iti । tat kiṃ punar kutaḥ । tasyaiva spaṣṭatarīkaraṇāya svasaṃvedyam ityādinān antaraṃ vakṣyamāṇena nyāyena ॥

<I,177>

[I,177,i]

syād etat — vināpi sambandhena niścayo bhaviṣyatīty āha — na cetyādi । tasmān mānasa iti । yasmād evam indriyajo na yujyata ity abhiprāyaḥ । abhedopacāro viśeṣaṇābhidhānarūpeṇa viśeṣyābhidheyapratipattiḥ । abhidhānābhidheyayoś ceti grahaṇaṃ dṛṣṭāntārtham । yad abhedopacārajñānam, tan mānasam abhidhānābhidheyābhedopacāravikalpavat । tathā ca gaurevāyam ityādijñānam । svabhāvaḥ ॥

[I,177,ii]

kiṃ kāraṇam iti vyāptim asambhāvayan pṛcchati । svasaṃvedyaṃ hītyādinā hetum āha । etac ca dharmiṇo 'nekarūpasyety atrāntare vyākhyātam ॥

[I,177,iii]

asādhāraṇeneti । sādhāraṇasya kvacid anupayogād ity uktam । tad etenānirdeśyam eva svalakṣaṇam indriyadhiyo viṣayaḥ, na nirdeśyaṃ sāmānyam । ato na tenābhedopacāraṃ kartuṃ sā samartheti sūcitam । yo yasyāviṣayaḥ, na sa tenābhedopacāraṃ kartuṃ samarthaḥ । tad yathā cakṣurvijñānaṃ śabdena । aviṣayaś ca gotvādisāmanyam indriyabudheḥ । vyāpakaviruddhaḥ । tataś ca mānasam evedam iti sthitam ॥

{1.41cd}

[I,177,iv]

atha punar ity asiddhatām āśaṅkate । sarvatheti jñeyatvādyākāreṇāpīty arthaḥ । tatra ko doṣa ity āha — sarvathetyādi । sarvathārthavijñāne sthitā sarvaprakāreṇārthādhigame vartamānā satī na pratyakṣadhīr bhaved iti sambandhaḥ । na pratyakṣa<I,178>śabdavācyā syād ity arthaḥ । kuta etad ity āha — pratyakṣaśabdo hītyādi । yato bhāṣyakāram atena pratyakṣaśabdastriṣv eva vartate । pramāṇe mukhya iti sannikarṣe pratyakṣapramitatvād iti prasthapramite prasthopacāravat । jñāna iti phale । akṣaṃ prati vṛtter ity anena sādharmyeṇa pramāṇatulyatvāt pratyakṣopacāro yuktaḥ, yathā siṃho māṇavaka iti ॥

[I,178,i]

yadi cetyādinā sarvathārthavijñāne sthitety etad vyācaṣṭe, setyādinā tu na pratyakṣadhīr bhaved ity etat । indriyanirapekṣeti sāmānyabuddhīnām atītādāv api bhāvād andhādīnāṃ ca । abhedopacārapravṛtteti । abhedopacārabuddhayo 'py evam prakārā eva । asatāpi vābhedopacāraṃ kurvanti, yathā pradhānayaḥ sāṅkhyapuruṣo 'yam iti । na caivaṃvidham indriyādisannikarṣajaṃ jñānam iṣyate । pratipāditaṃ ca — na sāmānyam indriyadhiyo viṣaya iti । nākṣaparatantrā syād iti । sāmarthyāt pratyakṣaśabdābhidhānaṃ pratīti gamyate । tathā hi pratyakṣaśabdābhidheyatā pratipādyatvena prastutā । avaśyaṃ caitad evaṃ vijñeyam । anyathe<I,179>ndriyanirapekṣākṣaparatantrā ceti virodhaḥ syāt । tad etad uktaṃ bhavati — jñānasyotpattāv akṣapāratantryaṃ pratyakṣasādharmyāt pratyakṣopacāro vā pratyakṣaśruteḥ pravṛttinimittam । asati tasmin sā na pravartata iti । yasyā naimittikyāḥ śruter yatra nimittaṃ nāsti, na sā tatra pravartate । tad yathā daṇḍiśrutiḥ । nāsti ca nimittaṃ pratyakṣaśruter yathokte jñāne । kāraṇābhāvaḥ ॥

[I,179,i]

sarvathā cetyādinā doṣāntaram āha । guṇatvādīnāṃ sāmānyadharmāṇāṃ rūpaśabdādau sarvatra bhāvād yathā cakṣuṣā grāhyatvam, tathā śrotrādibhir apītīndriyāntaraviṣaye 'pīndriyāntaraṃ pravartate । tato 'nekendriyakalpanāyā vaiyarthyaṃ syāt ॥

{1.42bcd}

[I,179,ii]

phalam anyan na labhyata iti । adhigamo hi jñānasya phalam । sa cet pramāṇam, phalāntarābhāvaḥ । na ca hānopādānopekṣābuddhayaḥ phalam iti kalpayituṃ yuktam, udakādismṛtyantaritatvāt । vyavahitāvyavahiyoś cāvyava<I,180>hitam eva phalaṃ nyāyyam । bhinnaviṣayatvāc cāyuktaṃ tāsāṃ phalatvam । pratyakṣaṃ hi rūpādisvalakṣaṇaviṣayam, tāstu hānādikriyāviṣayāḥ ॥

{1.43}

[I,180,i]

buddheś cetyādi । buddhijanma sūtre pratyakṣam uktam । tac ca buddher anyad anyad vā syāt । tatra yady anyad iṣyate, tad eva pramāṇaṃ syāt । janma ca kaṇabhujām ātmani svakāraṇe buddheḥ samavāyaḥ sattāguṇatvabuddhitvasamavāyo vā jñāne kārye । mīmāṃsakair api tanmatam evāśritam । sa vā yasmād bhāṣyakṛto matena samavāyaḥ pratyakṣaṃ prāpnoti । na ca yuktaṃ tasya pratyakṣatvam, arthavyabhicārāt । tathā hi nityatvād arthābhāve 'pi so 'sti । yad arthavyabhicāri, na tat pratyakṣam, mithyājñānavat । tathā ca samavāyaḥ । viruddhavyāptaḥ । atha vṛttikāram atena yato buddhijanma tat pratyakṣam, evam api nityatvāt samavāyo na kutaścid utpadyata iti nirviṣayaṃ lakṣaṇam । tasmād ubhayathāpi yadi sūtrakāramatena yadi vṛttikāramatena । atha vā yadi svakāraṇe kāryasya samavāyo buddher janmeṣṭam, yadi sattādīnāṃ jñāne kārye samavāyaḥ, ubhayathāpi pratyakṣatvaṃ na yujyate ॥

<I,181>

[I,181,i]

athetyādi । ananyatve buddhir eva janmeti janmagrahaṇaṃ matadvaye 'py apārthakam ॥

[I,181,ii]

nanu ca janmagrahaṇasya prayojanam uktam — jāyamānāvasthāyā eva buddheḥ prāmāṇyajñāpanārtham iti । tad ayuktam uktam । tathā hi kṣaṇikatvenottarakāle 'navasthānād abuddher jāyamānāyā eva prāmāṇyam, nordhvam ity uktam । tadā ca buddhabhāvād eva prāmāṇyābhāva iti kiṃ janmagrahaṇena । atha janmottarakālam asti buddhiḥ, evam apy aviśiṣṭatvāt tasyāḥ prāgvat tadāpi prāmāṇyam anivāryam iti kiṃ janmagrahaṇena । buddhiviśiṣṭasya tu janmano 'kṣaṃ pratyavṛtteḥ pūrvoktāc ca kāraṇāt pratyakṣatvābhāvaḥ ॥

{1.44}

[I,181,iii]

sarve tīrthyā ātmānāṃ pramātāram icchanti । atas taṃ vicārayitum āha — buddhijanmanītyādi । ihaiva kiṃ vicārayatīti cet, kva punar vicārārambhe nedaṃ codyam avatarati । api ceha lakṣaṇavākye puruṣasyeti vacanād ātmādhikṛta iti yuktam atraiva vicārayitum । pūrvāvasthāṃ vikṛtyety apramātravasthopamardenety arthaḥ । <I,182> evaṃ saty anitya iti । yad vikāri, tad anityam, ghaṭavat । tathā cātmā । svabhāvaḥ prasaṅgaḥ ॥

[I,182,i]

athāvikṛtir ityādinā yo yadāpramātravasthāyā aviśiṣṭaḥ, na tadā pramātā, yathā sa eva pumān prāk । yathoktaś ca buddhyutpāde 'pi sa iti viruddhavyāptaṃ prasaṅgam āha । anenaiva ca nityapramāṇanivṛttaye pramāṇabhūtāyety atra yad bhūtagrahaṇam, tatra yuktiḥ sūcitā । vakṣyamāṇasya ca svabhāvahetor vyāptisiddhau । evaṃ tu ślokaḥ paṭhitavyaḥ —
	vastuno 'rthakriyākāle vikṛtir yady anityatā /
	na cet sāsti na tadvastu sarvasāmarthyavarjitam //
iti ॥

[I,182,ii]

prathamaḥ paricchedaḥ samāptaḥ ॥

<II,1>

{2.1}

[II,1,i]

dve eva pramāṇe pratyakṣamanumānaṃ cetyuktam । tatra pratyakṣaṃ vyutpāditam । samprati prāptāvasaramanumānaṃ vyutpādayitumāha — anumānaṃ dvidhetyādi । svārtham, yena svayaṃ pratyeti । parārtham, yena parān pratyāyayati ॥

[II,1,ii]

nanu parārthasya lakṣaṇaṃ pṛthagavācyameva । gamakalakṣaṇavidhānenaiva hi pratipipādayiṣorvacanānukramo darśita eva, anyathābhidhāne gamakadharmādyotanāt । na hi ye yathā yamarthaṃ vidanti vacanajñāḥ, te tatpratipādane punarupadeśāntaramapekṣante ॥

[II,1,iii]

satyametat । tathāpi bālavyutpādanārtho 'yamārambhaḥ । yathāvastu pratipādyamānā api hyanyathā nigadanto dṛṣṭāḥ upayogino 'pyavinābhāvasyāvacanādanupayogināmapi ca sādhyopanayanigamanānāṃ prayogāt ॥

[II,1,iv]

trirūpāditi hetau pañcamī abhighātāc chabda iti yathā । atha vā lyablope yathā prāsādamāruhya prekṣate prāsādāt prekṣate । tathā trirūpaṃ liṅgaṃ dṛṣṭvārthadarśanam — trirūpāl liṅgato 'rthadṛgiti ॥

<II,2>

[II,2,i]

nanu trirūpagrahaṇamanarthakam atrirūpasyāliṅgatvāt । kiṃ ca līno 'rtho liṅgyate 'neneti liṅgam । tac ca trairūpyaṃ vinā na sambhavati । ato 'pi gatārthatvāt trirūpāditi na vācyam ॥

[II,2,ii]

naiṣa doṣaḥ । atrirūpamapi kecil liṅgamicchanti । atas tadvipratipattinivṛttaye trirūpagrahaṇam ॥

[II,2,iii]

tatrāhrīka āha —
	anyathānupapannatvaṃ yasyāsau heturiṣyate /
	ekalakṣaṇakaḥ so 'rthaś caturlakṣaṇako na vā //
iti । anyatheti sādhyena vinetyarthaḥ । anupapannatvamaklṛptirasambhavaḥ । nanu cāvinābhāvitvamevedaṃ syāt । netyahrīkaḥ । avinābhāvitvaṃ hi sādhyād bahiriṣyate anyathānupapannatvaṃ tu dharmiṇyeva sādhya eveti । ślokamapyāha —
	vinā sādhyādadṛṣṭasya dṛṣṭānte hetuteṣyate /
	parairmayā punardharmiṇyasambhūṣṇorvināmunā //
<II,3>
iti । etac caikameva rūpam । sati va trairūpye 'nyathānupapannatvaṃ caturthaṃ rūpameṣṭavyam । trairūpyamātre hi sa deśāntaragataḥ śyāmaḥ caitraputratvādityasyāpi hetutvaṃ syād iti ॥

[II,3,i]

tatra yaduktam — avinābhāvitvaṃ hi paraiḥ sādhyādbahiriṣyata iti, eṣo 'dhyāropaḥ । sarvopasaṃhāreṇa hi yatra yatra sādhanadharmaḥ tatra tatra sādhyadharma ityaṣā vyāptiravinābhāvitvam । ataḥ sādhye 'pi tadiṣyata eva । yadi ca sādhyadharmiṇyeva yaḥ sādhyadharmeṇāvinābhāvī sa heturiṣyate evaṃ sati yasya bahirapi sādhyenāvinābhāvas tasya hetutvaṃ na syāt । vyabhicāryapi ca hetuḥ syāt tasyāpi dharmiṇyanyathānupapannatvasya sambhavāt । tasmādayuktametat । ata evāsyāyuktatvān na caturlakṣaṇo heturupapadyate ॥

[II,3,ii]

yat punaruktam — trairūpyamātre hi sa syāmaḥ caitraputratvādityasyāpi hetutvaṃ syāditi tadayuktam । svabhāvakāryānupalambhaviśe<II,4>ṣāṇāmeva hi trairūpyamupapadyate nānyeṣām । na cāyaṃ teṣvantarbhavati । tata kutaḥ sa prasaṅgaḥ ॥

[II,4,i]

anyas tu dvirūpo heturiti darśayannāha —
	ajñāto dharmiṇo dharmo dharme sanneva yatra hi /
	jñāyate jñāpyate caiṣa heturvidhiniṣedhavān //
iti । ajñāto dharmo jijñāsito 'nityatvādir dharmiṇaḥ śabdāderyatra jñāyate kṛtakatvādau dharme । jñātatvaṃ sāmarthyalabhyam । sanneveti pramātrā ghaṭādiṣu svayaṃ smaryate paro va smāryate parārthānumāne । sanneva nāsannityetau vidhiniṣedhau yasya staḥ sa vidhiniṣedhavānhetuḥ । etena dharmidharmatvaṃ satsādhyadharmatvaṃ cetyetad dvairūpyamuktam ॥

[II,4,ii]

atra sādhyadharmo yatra sanneva nāsanniti bruvatā tadevānvayavyatirekavattvamuktaṃ bhavati yasmādevaṃ sa tatra sanneva bhavati yadi tadabhāve heturna bhavatyeva । tataś ca trairupyamevākārāntareṇoktamiti na dvirūpo hetuḥ ॥

<II,5>

[II,5,i]

ṣaḍlakṣaṇo heturityaparaḥ । trīṇi caitāni — abādhitaviṣayatvaṃ vivakṣitaikasaṅkhyatvaṃ jñātatvaṃ ceti । tatrābādhitaviṣayatvaṃ tāvan na rūpāntaram bādhāvinābhāvayorvirodhāt । avinābhāvo hi hetoḥ sādhyadharme satyeva bhāvaḥ । kathaṃ ca sa tallakṣaṇo dharmiṇi hetuḥ syāt na cātra sādhyadharmo bhavet । ten na bādhāvinābhāvayoḥ sahabhāvaḥ । tena nābādhitaviṣayatvaṃ rūpāntaram ॥

[II,5,ii]

vyavacchedyābhāvād vivakṣitaikasaṅkhyatvamapi na lakṣaṇāntaratvena vācyam । tad viruddhāvyabhicāriṇo hetutvaprasaṅganivṛttyarthamucyate । svalakṣaṇayuktayoś ca hetvorekatra virodhinorupanipāte viruddhāvyabhicāritvaṃ bhavati । na ca yathoktalakṣaṇānāṃ kāryasvabhāvānupalambhānāṃ pratyanīko hetuḥ sambhavati । kathaṃ hi nāma ekaḥ svasādhyabhāva eva bhāvāt tenāvyabhicārī tatraiva cānyo 'pi tadbādhakasya bhāva eva bhāvād viruddhas tena sambhavet । api ca sa heturyadi svabhāvata eva taddharmabhāvī tadārthāntaropanipāte 'pi kathamanyathā syāt । na hi <II,6> vastūnāṃ svabhāvānyathābhāvasya viruddhasvabhāvadvayasya ca sambhavaḥ । atha svabhāvato 'taddharmabhāvī evaṃ satyanyadāpi na sādhanaṃ kasyacit । tasmāt svabhāvata eva svasādhyāvinābhāvino yathoktalakṣaṇasya hetos tallakṣaṇaḥ pratiheturna sambhavatītyalakṣaṇamekasaṅkhyāvivakṣā । viruddhāvyabhicāryavacanaprasaṅga iti cet vastubalapravṛttaṃ liṅgaṃ pratīṣṭatvādadoṣaḥ । viṣayaś cāsya parastān nivedayiṣyate ॥

[II,6,i]

jñānaṃ punaraliṅgadharmaḥ । kathaṃ liṅgasya lakṣaṇaṃ syāt । kiṃrūpāl liṅgādarthaḥ pratipattavya iti cintāyāṃ pratipatturavisaṃvādakasya rūpamucyate yaddarśanādayaṃ sādhanāsādhane pravivecya tasyeṣṭārthasādhanapratyayāt pravartate । tatra yadasya liṅgasyātmarūpam tal lakṣaṇam na pararūpam pratipattijanmanyupayogamātrāt tallakṣaṇatve 'tiprasaṅgāt । evaṃ hi prameyapuruṣādīnāmapi tallakṣaṇatvaṃ syāt । na hi teṣvapyasatsu liṅgini <II,7> jñānaṃ bhavati । tasmāj jñānamapi na liṅgalakṣaṇameṣṭavyamiti sthitametat — trirūpa eva heturiti ॥

[II,7,i]

pūrvavat phalamiti । yathā pratyakṣe dvidhā phalamuktaṃ viṣayasaṃvittiḥ svasaṃvittiś ca tathehāpi pratyakṣavadavyatiriktamanumānasyādhigamātmakaṃ phalamiti bruvatānumānamapyadhigamasvabhāvamityuktaṃ bhavati ॥

[II,7,ii]

ataḥ pṛcchati — yadi dvayamapītyādi । arthas tu rūpaṃ cātulyametayoriti । tuśabdo 'vadhāraṇārthaḥ — etadeva dvayamatulyam adhigamarūpatā tu tulyeti । nanu cādhigamas tayo rūpam । tac cedabhinnam, tat kimanyadrūpam yaducyate — rūpaṃ cātulyametayoriti । yat tadviṣayasārūpyaṃ pramāṇaṃ vyavasthāpitam tadatulyamityuktam । tathā hi — tat pratyakṣasya spaṣṭam aspaṣṭaṃ tvanumānasya ॥

[II,7,iii]

viṣayo hītyādi । viṣayaśabdenātrālambanaṃ vivakṣitam na tu prāmāṇyasya viṣayaḥ । anumānasyāpi hyavisaṃvādalakṣaṇaṃ prāmāṇyaṃ vastuviṣayameva । tasmādālambanabhedāt pramāṇayorviṣayabhedamāha । kathaṃ punarālambanabhedaḥ । pratibhāsasya bhinnatvāt । na hi tāvekasya vilakṣaṇāvākārau yujyete । bhinna iti cābhinnapratiṣedha eva draṣṭavyaḥ na tu nā<II,8>nāviṣayatā anumānavikalpasya nirviṣayatvāt । tac ca anumānasya sammato yo viṣayaḥ tasya tattvato 'pariniṣpannatvāt ॥

[II,8,i]

tadākāraviśeṣāc ceti । taditi pratyakṣānumānayorviṣayaḥ parāmṛśyate । tasyākāraḥ svabhāvaḥ ākriyate paricchidyata iti kṛtvā । tadākārasya viśeṣo bheda ityarthaḥ । viśeṣagrahaṇaṃ cāviśeṣapratiṣedhapratipādanaparaṃ veditavyam । na tu nānāsvabhāvatānena pratipadyate, sāmānyasya vikalpitatvenāsattvāt । tadetat sūcitaṃ bhavati — yasmāt pratyakṣasya bahirviṣayo 'sti yatas tasya spaṣṭo viṣayapratibhāso bhavati na tvanumānasya yas tu tasyāsphuṭo viṣayākāraḥ sa svabījabalādeva jāyate tasmāt pratyakṣānumānayoryathoktaṃ svarūpaṃ bhinnamiti । atha vā pratyakṣasya svalakṣaṇaṃ sākṣāt spaṣṭasvākārajanakaṃ prameyaṃ svarūpeṇa anumānasya tu tadeva pāramparyeṇāsphuṭaviṣayākārajanakaṃ pararūpeṇa prameyam । pratyakṣasyāpi pararūpeṇetyapare । tadevaṃ yataḥ pratyakṣānumānayorbhinno viṣayaḥ atas tatsvabhāvaviśeṣāt spaṣṭāspaṣṭaviṣayākāratayā svarūpamapi bhinnamiti ॥

<II,9>

{2.2}

[II,9,i]

atha kasmāditi । kiṃ kāraṇaṃ svārthaparārthabhedenānumānameva dvidhā bhidyate na tu pratyakṣamityavadhāraṇena darśayati । etaduktaṃ bhavatisvayaṃ pratyakṣīkṛtasyārthasya parāvabodhanāya yad vacanam tat parārthaṃ pratyakṣaṃ dvitīyaṃ kasmān neṣyata iti ॥

[II,9,ii]

yasmādityādi । anumānasya hi sāmānyaṃ viṣayaḥ । tatra ca yādṛśamanumānamātmanaḥ tādṛśameva parasantāne vācā kriyata iti yuktaṃ tasya dvaividhyam । pratyakṣasya tu svalakṣaṇaṃ viṣayaḥ । na ca tatra yādṛśamātmanaḥ pratyakṣajñānam tādṛk śabdena santānāntare janayituṃ śakyate tasyānirdeśyatvāt । anyathāndhādīnāmapi śabdāt tathāvighameva sphuṭapratibhāsi jñānaṃ syāt । kasmāt tadanirdeśyamityāhagrāhyabhedāditi । pratyakṣasya hyasādhāraṇaṃ grāhyam । na ca tac chakyate nirdeṣṭum tasya pūrvamadṛṣṭatvāt । anumānasya tu tadviparītam । tasmāt tasyaiva grāhyaṃ nirdeśyam na pratyakṣasya ॥

[II,9,iii]

svātmavadityanenaitat sūcayati — pratyakṣānumānayoḥ svarūpaṃ bhinnam । pratyātmavedyametat sarvasya । na cābhinnaviṣayatve svaviṣayākāramanukurvatos tadupapadyate । tasmād yathā tayoḥ svarūpaṃ bhinnam, <II,10> tathā viṣayabhedo 'pi draṣṭavyaḥ । tato nānumānavat pratyakṣasya viṣayo nirdeśya iti ॥

[II,10,i]

anye tvāhuḥ - vṛttabhaṅgabhayādatra yat paścād vaktavyam tat pūrvamuktam । tasmādevamatha grantho vijñeyaḥ — kasmādanumānameva dvidhā bhidyate na pratyakṣamiti pṛṣṭe kāraṇamāha — grāhyabhedādityādi । yadi grāhyabhedādanumānaṃ dvighā bhidyate evaṃ sati pratyakṣamapi dvidhā bhidyetetyāha — svalakṣaṇamanirdeśyamiti । etaduktaṃ bhavati — īdṛśamidaṃ pratyakṣānumānayorgrāhyamiṣyate yatraikaṃ nirdeśyamanyadanirdeśyamiti । tasmādanumānameva dvidhā bhidyate yasya viṣayo vācā parasmai pratipādayituṃ śakyate na tu pratyakṣamiti ॥

[II,10,ii]

nanu cārthas tu rūpaṃ cātulyametayorityanena prāgeva pramāṇayorviṣayabhedaḥ pratipāditas tadbhedāc ca svarūpabhedaḥ । tat kimidamupanyastam — bhinnaṃ hi pratyakṣānumānayoḥ svātmavad grāhyamityādi । pūrvamanyārtho 'yamartha uktaḥ idānīmanyārtha ityadoṣaḥ ॥

[II,10,iii]

yadi cetyādinā svalakṣaṇasyānirdeśyatvaṃ pratipādayati । sa tenaiva śabdenānumeyaḥ syāditi sa eva pratyakṣagrāhyo 'rthas tataḥ śabdāt <II,11> pratīyetetyarthaḥ । na caivam । mā bhūdandhāderapi pratyakṣeṇaiva tasyārthasya darśanamiti । paras tu jāḍyādimaṃ doṣamanavagacchan svayamabhyupagatapramāṇaikaviṣayatvasya dṛṣṭānuvidhāyitāṃ darśayanniṣṭamevaṃ me taditi nanu cetyādinā sūcayati । sparśo hi pratyakṣasyārthaḥ । sa eva ca rūpeṇānumīyata iti manyate । kadāciditi yadā sparśa indriyeṇa na spṛśyate, tadetyarthaḥ । na tu yathā pratyakṣamiti । pratyakṣaṃ hi bhedāntaravimarśavivekena pratiṣṭhitenaiva rūpeṇa sparśaṃ paricchinatti anumānaṃ tu smārtākṛṣṭapūrvānusandhānataḥ — so 'yaṃ mayā pūrvamanena rūpeṇa saha prāgupalabdha iti sparśasāmānyamasparśavyāvṛttam । tad yatheti pūrvadṛṣṭānusandhāne dṛṣṭāntamāha । yathā rūpaṃ na pratyakṣato gṛhyata ityeva svalakṣaṇākāreṇa liṅgaṃ bhavati viśeṣasyānanvayāt api tu sāmānyākāreṇaiva pūrvadṛṣṭānusaṃhitena tathā na sparśaḥ pūrvapratyakṣeṇa gṛhīta ityeva svalakṣaṇato 'numeyaḥ kiṃ tu sāmānyākāreṇaivānumānayogyeneti darśayati ॥

<II,12>

[II,12,i]

kathaṃ dṛṣṭādivyavahāra iti । yadi yathānubhūtamācakṣate evaṃvyavahārā āryā yujyante । tvanmatena tu svalakṣaṇamupalabhyānyadeva kathayatāṃ vyavahārā anāryāḥ syuḥ । tataś cābhyupetabādhā ॥

[II,12,ii]

dṛṣṭamityādinaitat kathayati - darśanādikriyānimittā dṛṣṭādiśabdāḥ । te ca sati svasminnimitte āryaiḥ prayujyante nāsatītyāryā vyavahārā abhyupeyante na tu svalakṣaṇābhidhānāditi nābhyupetabādheti ॥

[II,12,iii]

yat tarhītyādi । śāstravirodhamāha । nanu ca naiva cakṣurvijñānānubhūta eva kṣaṇo manovijñānenānubhūyate । kiṃ tarhi । kṣaṇāntaramityuktaṃ prāk । tat kathamevamuktam । naiṣa doṣaḥ । cakṣurvijñānānubhūtamevārtham iti svalakṣaṇopalakṣaṇaparametat svalakṣaṇameveti yāvat । tulyajātīyatvāc ca pūrvottarayoḥ kṣaṇayorabhedavivakṣayaivamabhihitaṃ syāt । atha vānuśabdo 'yaṃ sahārthe vartate bhūtaśabdo 'pyutpanne । tataś ca cakṣurvijñānena sahotpannamevārthaṃ vijānātītyayamatrārtha ityadoṣaḥ । yadi yat <II,13> tanmanovijñānānubhūtaṃ svalakṣaṇam tadanirdeśyam kathaṃ mano nīlaṃ ca vijānāti nīlamiti cāviṣṭābhilāpaṃ tadeva । tatrāpīti śāstre ।

{2.3}

[II,13,i]

ākārāntaravirdeśyanāmajñatvādityādi । svalakṣaṇākārādākārāntaraṃ sāmānyākāraḥ । tena nirdeśyam na svalakṣaṇena । tasya nāma nīlamitīyaṃ sañjñā । tac ca vijānāti na kevalaṃ svalakṣaṇam । tasmād dvidhā śāstre mana iṣyate ॥

[II,13,ii]

anīlavyudāseneti tamākārāntaraṃ darśayati । vyavahartṝṇāmabhiprāyānurodhādanīlavyudāsenetyuktam । te hi tattvādhyavasāyena vyavaharantītyuktametat । anyathā parasparavyāhatametat syāt । tathā hiyadyākārāntareṇa mano nirdiśati na tarhi tena cakṣurvijñānānubhūtameva nirdiṣṭaṃ bhavati । atha tadeva svalakṣaṇaṃ nirdiśati na nāmākārāntareṇeti ॥

[II,13,iii]

asāmānye 'pīti । apiśabdāt sāmānye 'pyanityatvādau ॥

[II,13,iv]

vāyvādisvabhāva iti । ādiśabdenākāśādayo 'pratyakṣā gṛhyante । yathāheti । kaṇādaḥ । asya sūtrasya sambandhaḥ — kṣitija<II,14>lānanavadagrahaṇāt sparśamātraṃ vāyuriti pareṇākte tatparihārāyāha — adṛṣṭasyāpi liṅgataḥ samadhigamaṃ kariṣyāmaḥ । kiṃ punas tasya liṅgamiti । taducyate — sparśaś ca । na ca dṛṣṭānāṃ sparśa ityadṛṣṭaliṅgo vāyuriti । sparśaś ca samupalabhyate śītoṣṇatvaviśeṣarahitaḥ । caśabdāc chabdadhṛtikampāś ca । nirvṛkṣakṣupe deśe śukaśukāśabdaḥ samupalabhyate tṛṇādināṃ ca dhṛtiḥ । teṣāṃ dravyāntareṇāsati pratibandhe gurutvāt pātaḥ syāt । sthitiś ca viyati lakṣyate । latādīnāṃ ca kampaḥ । na cāyaṃ dṛṣṭānāṃ kṣityādīnām । caśabdān na cādṛṣṭānāmākāśādināma । ato dṛṣṭādṛṣṭeṣvadṛṣṭatvāt sparśaviśeṣo 'dṛṣṭaḥ । so 'sya liṅgamityadṛṣṭaliṅgo vāyuḥ । na cāsau pūrvaṃ dṛṣṭaḥ tatprathamataḥ sparśaviśeṣeṇa grahaṇādityasāmānyaviṣayamanumānam ॥

[II,14,i]

na tatsāmānyasūcanāditi । tacchabdena sparśa eva sambadhyate, na tu vāyuḥ ॥

<II,15>

[II,15,i]

ata evāha — na hi tad vāyvādiṣvityādi । sparśasya sāmānyamāśritatvaṃ guṇotvena sūcyate । yo guṇaḥ sa āśritaḥ gandhavat । guṇaśa ca sparśaḥ । svabhāvaḥ ॥

[II,15,ii]

atha vā tacchabdena vāyureva sambadhyata iti darśayannāha — na vā vāyvādisvabhāveṣvityādi । asyārthaḥ — yo guṇaḥ sa dravyāśritaḥ, gandhavat । guṇaś ca sparśa iti svabhāvaḥ । sparśasya guṇatvād dravyāśritatve 'numite dravyatvamātramarthataḥ sidhyati । tad yathā cakṣurādīnāṃ pārārthye siddhe paro 'pyarthataḥ sidhyatītyabhiprāyaḥ ॥

[II,15,iii]

pariśeṣāditi । pariśeṣasiddhiranumānameva liṅgajatvāditi manyate । yathāhetyādi । nāyaṃ sparśaḥ pṛthivyāḥ gandhādyasahacāritvāt । nāptejasoḥ anuṣṇāśītatvāt । nāpyākāśādīnāmadṛṣṭānām । teṣāṃ hi sparśavattvād ghaṭādīnāṃ tatra pratighātaḥ syāt । na manasaḥ anumeyaguṇatvāt । aṇutvamekatvaṃ cāsyānumeyau guṇau । ayaṃ tu pratyakṣaḥ । na ca nirāśrayo guṇaḥ samasti । tasmāt pariśeṣād vāyorevāyaṃ sparśa ityeṣā pariśeṣasiddhiḥ ॥

<II,16>

[II,16,i]

na tatsattvāsiddheriti । tacchabdena vāyuḥ sambadhyate । yasmādnyeṣāṃ yasyāsambhavaḥ tatra siddhasattāke tasyāstitvaṃ sambhāvyate । yasya tu sattvamevāsiddham kathaṃ tatra pariśeṣāt so 'stīti sambhāvyate । na hi — yadānyena tatra sannihitena puruṣeṇedaṃ kāryaṃ na kṛtamiti sambhāvyate tadā vandhyāsutena pariśeṣāt kṛtametaditi yuktaṃ sambhāvayitum । teṣveva tu kenedaṃ kṛtamiti saṃśayo bhavati ॥

[II,16,ii]

pratiṣedhatulyatvāc ceti । siddhe 'pi tasya sattve pratiṣedhasya tulyatvān na yuktamanumānam । yathaivāyaṃ sparśaḥ pṛthivyādiṣu na dṛṣṭacara iti teṣāṃ na bhavati tathā vāyāvapi prāṅna dṛṣṭa iti tasyāpi mā bhūt । kathaṃ tarhi vāyoḥ pariśeṣasiddhirityāha — siddhe hītyādi । yathotpattimatāṃ ghaṭādīnāṃ sattvaṃ siddham tathā yadi vāyvādīnāṃ jijñāsitānāṃ sattvaṃ siddhaṃ bhavati evaṃ sati hetoḥ siddhatvaṃ labhyate nānyathā । pratiṣedhāsambhave citi । siddhe 'pi teṣāṃ sattve yadi sa dharmaḥ pramāṇena bādhyate 'gnāviva śaityam evamapyasiddha eva hetuḥ syāt viparyayāt tu siddha ityevaṃ yathā hetoḥ siddhatvaṃ janyate tathā darśitam । guṇaviśeṣasambandhāditi । guṇaviśeṣo dharmaviśeṣo hetutvenābhimataḥ । tasya sambandhaḥ sādhyenāvinābhāvaḥ । guṇasāmānyamujjhitveti dharmasāmā<II,17>nyaṃ vyabhicāri hitvā । guṇaviśeṣeṇeti yathoktena sādhyadharmiṇi siddhasattākenānvayavyatirekavatā dharmeṇa । dravyaviśeṣānumānaṃ kriyata iti pariśeṣād vāyuranumīyata ityarthaḥ । tatrāpi sāmānyākāreṇeti veditavyam na tu svarūpeṇa yasmāt prāgevānumānasya svalakṣaṇaviṣayatvaṃ niṣiddham । viśeṣagrahaṇaṃ tu pṛthivyādidravyanirāsārtham । tatrāyaṃ prayogaḥ — yo yataḥ siddhasattākādanyeṣāṃ na sambhāvyate vastudharmas tatra ca pramāṇenābādhitaḥ sa tasya bhavati । tad yathotpattimadbhyaḥ siddhasattākebhyo 'nyeṣāmasambhāvyamānamanityatvaṃ vastudharmas tatra pramāṇenābādhitaṃ bhavati । vāyoḥ siddhasattākādanyeṣāṃ na sambhāvyate 'nuṣṇāśītasparśo vastudharmas tatra ca pramāṇenābādhita iti svabhāvaḥ । evaṃ sparśasya pariśeṣād vāyusambandhitve siddhe vāyuḥ kvacid deśaviśeṣe kālaviśeṣe vā sidhyati । tvanmatena tveṣāṃ pariśeṣasiddhirna bhavatīti darśayannāha — sattvaṃ tvasiddhamityādi । yasmāt sattvamasiddhaṃ tulyaś ca pṛthivyādibhiḥ pratiṣedhaḥ tasmādguṇaviśeṣābhāvaḥ trairūpyavato dharmasyābhāva ityarthaḥ । tato guṇaviśeṣābhāvāt tatra <II,18> kuto 'numānam । naiva । evaṃ tāvad dṛṣṭādṛṣṭebhyaḥ pratiṣedhamabhyupetyānumānābhāva uktaḥ ॥

[II,18,i]

samprati pratiṣedha evāyukta iti darśayannāha — yadyadarśanamātreṇetyādi । mātragrahaṇenopalabdhilakṣaṇaprāptasya yadadarśanam tata evābhāvaḥ sidhyatīti sūcayati । nanūpalabdhilakṣaṇaprāpteḥ sparśasya yukta eva pratiṣedhaḥ । na yuktaḥ dṛśyatatsvabhāvamātrāpratiṣedhāt । pṛthivyādisāmānyaṃ gṛhītvā bhavān pratiṣedhamāha । tatra ca tūlopalapallavādiṣu tadbhāve 'pi sparśabhedadarśanāt kvacid viśeṣasyāpi sambhavāc chaṅkayā bhāvyamiti sarvatrādarśanamātreṇāyuktaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ ॥

[II,18,ii]

adṛṣṭebhyo 'pi na yukta iti darśannāha — na hyadṛṣṭebhya ityādi । hiśabdaḥ samuccaya'vadhāraṇe vā । amurtimatāmanabhighātāditi । abhighātasya vāyaṃ pratiṣedhaḥ syāt tadviparītasya vā vastuno vidhiḥ । yadi pratiṣedhaḥ abhighātasparśaviśeṣayoḥ kāryakāraṇabhāvo vyāpyavyāpakabhāvo vā vācyaḥ yato hetuvyāpakāveva nivartamānau svapratibaddhe kāryavyāpye nivartayataḥ anyathātiprasaṅgāt । kāryakāraṇavyāpyavyāpakabhāvau ca na sidhyataḥ vināpyabhighātena sparśaviśeṣasya bhāvādarthāntaratvāc ca । athāmūrtimatāmanabhighātādityanenānabhi<II,19>ghātākhyaṃ vastvevocyate paryudāsavṛttyā tasya tarhi vyomādhibhiḥ sambandhaḥ sādhyaḥ sparśaviśeṣeṇa ca virodhaḥ । anyathā kathaṃ tadasambaddhamaviruddhaṃ ca tenaitat tatra bādhata atiprasaṅgo vā ॥

[II,19,i]

tatra tāvat sambandho na sidhyati । tathā hi — teṣu tasya vṛttirvā sambandhaḥ syāt tajjanyatā vā । na tāvad vṛttiḥ sidhyati teṣāmatīndriyatvāt । n hyatīndriyeṣu kasyacid vṛttirupalabhyate । na ca vinopalambhenātredaṃ vartata iti śakyate niścetum । nāpi tajjanyatā sidhyati vyatirekāsiddheḥ । na hyanvayamātrāt kāraṇasya sāmarthyaṃ gamyate api tu vyatirekādapi । sa ceha nāsti nityatvāt sarvagatatvāc ca vyomādināṃ tadabhāve tadabhāvāsambhavāt । tadevamanabhighātākhyamākāśādisambandhi vastveva na sidhyati ॥

[II,19,ii]

kutaḥ punas tasya sparśaviśeṣeṇa virodhaḥ । tathā hi — ātapādiṣu ghaṭādināmanabhighāto 'sti । atha ca te sparśavantaḥ । tasmān na tataḥ pratiṣedhaḥ sidhyati ॥

[II,19,iii]

guṇānumeyatvāc ceti । tatpuruṣo 'yam । manasi ca guṇopajanitavyatirekanibandhanā ṣaṣṭhī nānumeyāpekṣā । manaso guṇānāmanumeyatvāditi vākyārthaḥ । guṇasya guṇāpekṣāyā nityatvāt  sāmarthyābhāvadoṣo 'pi nāsti । ayamapyahetuḥ avirodhāt । tathā hi — yathātmano <II,20> vibhutvaṃ nāma guṇo 'numeyaḥ atha ca sukhādayaḥ pratyakṣāḥ tathā manaso 'pyaṇutvamekatvaṃ cānumeyametadguṇadvayaṃ syāt ayaṃ ca sparśaḥ pratyakṣo guṇaḥ syāditi na kaścid virodhaḥ ॥

[II,20,i]

idānīṃ yadatra yuktam tat pratipādayitumāha — kiṃ tarhītyādi । caśabdo 'vadhāraṇārthaḥ । kathaṃ punar — dṛṣṭeṣu ca dṛṣṭatvādityetaduktam, yāvatā sa sparśaviśeṣo dṛṣṭeṣvapi naiva dṛṣṭaḥ ॥

[II,20,ii]

naiṣa doṣaḥ । dṛṣṭeṣu tāvat sparśasāmānyaṃ sambhavadviśeṣaṃ dṛṣṭam । adṛṣṭeṣu tu tasyāpi darśanaṃ nāsti । yo yatra dṛṣṭasāmānyaḥ sa tatra sambhavati । yathāmalakeṣu madhuro rasaḥ । dṛṣṭasāmānyaś ca dṛṣṭeṣu sparśaviśeṣaḥ । atha vā yo yatra dṛṣṭaḥ sa tatra sambhavadviśeṣaḥ । yathāmalakeṣu rasaḥ । dṛṣṭaś ca sparśo dṛṣṭeṣviti svabhāvau । ubhayatra cābādhake satīti viśeṣaṇaṃ draṣṭavyam । vāyvādau tu sadvyavahārapratiṣedhāyānupalambho vācyaḥ । yadyevaṃ niścayena bhavitavyam — atraivāyaṃ sambhavatīti । saṃśayas tu dṛṣṭaḥ । tasmānnāyaṃ dṛṣṭeṣu sambhavatītyata āha — teṣāṃ cetyādi । anekatvāt saṃśayaḥ na tu tatrāsambhavādityarthaḥ ॥

[II,20,iii]

tairapi vāyorānumānikatvaṃ nirastamiti darśayannāha — āptasañjñāvidhānenetyādi । na vāyorānumānikatvamityatrādhyāhāryam । dravyasāmānyānumāne satīti । sparśena guṇena dravyāśritenāsti kimapi <II,21> dravyam yadayamāśrita iti dravyamātrānumānam  tat parityajya । āptasañjñāprāmāṇyāditi । yasmāt kṣīṇadoṣairnavaiva dravyasañjñāvihitāḥ tatra pṛthivyādiṣvaṣṭāsu dravyeṣvaṣṭau sañjñā niveśitāḥ, vāyusañjñaivāvaśiṣyate na cānyad dravyamasti daśamam tasmād yasyāyaṃ sparśaḥ sa vāyurityevaṃ pṛthivyādibhyo 'nyasya daśamāder dravyasya pṛthivyādeś cānyasya pratiṣedhena vāyusattvamavagacchati ॥

{2.4}

[II,21,i]

na bhedasyāpi sambhavāditi । śābdasya pramāṇāntaratvanirākaraṇāya pramāṇāntaravādī tāvaduttaraṃ dāyikaḥ svayaṃ tūttaratra dāsyati । prasiddhivaśeneti । sapakṣavipakṣayoḥ sadasattve śrotuḥ siddhe iti dṛṣṭāntānabhidhānam । dṛṣṭāntagrahaṇamavayavopalakṣaṇārtham avayavānāmanupadeśāditi yāvat । tadetaduktaṃ bhavati — yadanupadiṣṭāvayavam, tadanumānād bhinnam pratyakṣavat । tathā ca śābdamiti svabhāvaḥ ॥

[II,21,ii]

evamapīti । vyabhicāramāha । dṛṣṭāntasyaikasyeti । śeṣāvayavāpekṣayā dṛṣṭāntasyaikatvam na tu dṛṣṭāntāpekṣayā । tataś cāyamarthaḥ — yaddṛṣṭāntasyaivānabhidhānamiti । dvayorveti । vāśabdaś cārthe vartamāno 'nuktasamuccayaṃ karoti trayāṇāṃ caturṇāṃ pañcānāṃ cetyarthaḥ । tena <II,22> yadāpi sādhāraṇaṃ hetuṃ karoti tadāpi svārthānumānenānekānto bhavati । śābdaprasaṅga iti । parasya śābdamanumānād bhinnaṃ pratītam, tena śābdavat prasaṅgaḥ anumānād bhinnatvaprasaṅga ityarthaḥ । yathābhūtaṃ śābdam tathābhūtaṃ tadapi prāpnotīti yāvat । vināpi hi vatinā tadartho gamyata ityuktaprāyam ॥

[II,22,i]

anye tvāhurityādi । śabdo hi svarūpeṇābhinnarūpamevārthaṃ pratyāyayati na tvevaṃ dhūmādayaḥ । na hi dhūmādagniṃ pratiyan pratyāyayanvā dhūmarūpeṇa pratyeti pratyāyayati vā । kathamarthe 'numānamiti । arthasyānekarūpatvāt । tatra kiṃ svarūpeṇa so 'rtho gamyata uta sāmānyarūpeṇa । sarvathaivānupapattiṃ manyate । tathā hi — yadi vṛkṣādayaḥ śabdāḥ sattvādibhiḥ sāmānyākārairvṛkṣādikamarthaṃ pratipādayeyuḥ, sarvaśabdānāmekārthatā prasajyeta sāmānyākārāṇāmanekārthasādhāraṇatvāt । atha viśeṣarūpeṇa tadayuktam asādhāraṇasya rūpasya pratipādayitumaśakyatvāditi sarvathā śabdārthatvābhāvaḥ । vṛkṣaśabdābhidheyo 'nyo 'rthe na bhavatīti । yathaiva tava śabdārtho 'nyāpoḍhaḥ sāmā<II,23>nyam tathā mamāpi । etāvāṃs tu viśeṣaḥ - mayā tac chabdākāroparaktaṃ pratīyata ityabhyupagatamiti darśayati । vṛkṣaśabdābhidheyo yo 'rthaḥ, so 'nyo ghaṭādirna bhavati । anyaśabdārthābhāvenātra vṛkṣaśabdābhidheyo bhāgo lakṣyate । etaduktaṃ bhavati — arthāntaravyāvṛttyupalakṣito yo vastuno bhāgaḥ sa eva vṛkṣaśabdasyārtha iti tenaiva tasya sārūpyāt । na tu sattvādibhiḥ sādhāraṇairākārairasādhāraṇena vā rūpeṇeti manyate ॥

[II,23,i]

anyeṣāṃ pāṭho vṛkṣaśabdābhidheyo 'nyārtho na bhavatīti । vṛkṣaśabdārtho yaḥ sa śabdāntarasyārtho na bhavati । paryāyaśabdānāmekārthatvenānanyatvamevetyabhiprāyaḥ । atrāpi vṛkṣaśabdārthasya śabdāntarānabhidheyatāṃ darśayatā śabdāntarārthavyāvṛttyupalakṣitaṃ vṛkṣatvamātraṃ vṛkṣaśabdasyārtha ityuktaṃ bhavatīti sa evārthaḥ ॥

[II,23,ii]

nanu ca dravyaśabdenāpi śākhādimānarthaḥ pratyāyyate । na cāsau tadrūpaḥ । tataś cāsārupye 'pyabhidheyatvadarśanān na śabdasārūpyeṇārthapratyāyanamityata āha — yadyapītyādi । apiśabdena dravyaśabdo dravyabhedānāṃ vyabhicārādavācaka eva । abhyupetya tūttaramucyata ityarthamāviṣkaroti । rūpāntaramākārāntaram tasyaiva vastunaḥ kaścid bhāgaḥ । tena ca saha dravyaśabdasya sārupyamastyevetyabhiprāyaḥ । tat <II,24> punā rūpāntaramadravyanivṛttyopalakṣyata iti darśayitumidamuktamadravyanivṛttyeti ॥

[II,24,i]

nanu cetyādi । na kevalaṃ dravyaśabdenādravyanivṛttyupalakṣitaṃ vastuno rūpāntaraṃ dravyaśabdasārupyaprāptiyogyaṃ gamyate api tu vṛkṣaśabdenāpi । tathā hi — sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ dṛśyate — dravyaṃ vṛkṣa iti । na hi bhinnārthayos tadupapadyate । na ca tena saha tasya sārūpyamiṣyate । tataḥ sa eva doṣaḥ asārūpye 'pi śabdārthatvadarśanāt । nābhidhānasya sārūpyeṇārthābhidhānamityabhiprāyaḥ ॥

[II,24,ii]

arthāt na śabdāditi । vṛkṣaśabdārthādevādravyanivṛttyavinābhāvinaḥ sā pratīyate । mūḍhas tu śabdādeva gamyata iti manyate । sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ tu viśeṣasahitasya viśeṣe vartamānatvāt । na tu vṛkṣaśabdenādravyanivṛttirabhidhīyate । yadi vṛkṣādipadānyevetyādi । subantānyeva padāni yadi śabdanibandhane pramāṇa ucyeran na syād doṣaḥ । tathā hi — teṣāṃ pariniṣpannarūpo 'rtha idaṃ taditi pratyavamarśayogyo buddhau sanniviśata iti tena sahābhedopacāraḥ sambhavati śabdasya । na tu nāmapadānyeva pariniṣpannārthābhidhāyīnyucyante । kiṃ <II,25> tarhi । taṅantānyapi yadāha — ākhyātaśabdairapītyādi । ākhyātaśabdaiḥ pacati paṭhatītyevamādibhiraliṅgāsaṅkhyā pūrvāparībhūtāvayavā pariniṣpannasvarūpā kriyocyate । na ca tathāvidhasyārthasyedaṃ tadityagṛhītasya buddyā śakyo 'bhedopacāraḥ kartum । nāpi pariniṣpannarūpaḥ śabdātmā śādyamānākāratāṃ pratipadyate ॥

[II,25,i]

yeṣāṃ ca vākyameva śabda iti । tenārthasya śabdanāt । yadi vākyameva śabdaḥ padānāmupādānaṃ kimarthamityāha — tadadhigamopāyaś cetyādi । tatsamudāyātmakatvāt yathā varṇāḥ padānāmiti manyate । teṣāṃ nāstītyādi । vākyārtho hi bāhyo vā syāt sādhyasādhanasambandhātmā sādhanaśaktiniveśānugṛhītā niravayavā kriyā vā āntaro va pratibhālakṣaṇaḥ ॥

[II,25,ii]

trayamapi caitadasattvabhūtamidaṃ taditi pratyavamarśātikrāntam । na ca tathābhūtenārthena so 'yamityabhedopacāraḥ śakyaḥ kartumiti ॥

[II,25,iii]

viśeṣaleśamiti । dṛṣṭāntānabhidhānaṃ śabdena cābhedopacāro viśeṣaleśaḥ ॥

<II,26>

[II,26,i]

yadi tarhi na bhidyate tvayā cāgamikatvaṃ vāyvādīnāṃ pratipādayatā svalakṣaṇaviṣayatvaṃ śābdasya pratipāditam evaṃ satyāgamānumānayorabhedāt siddhiṃ svalakṣaṇaviṣayatvamityāha — tatra śabdavinirmuktamityādi । tatreti śāstre śāstranimittamityarthaḥ । etaduktaṃ bhavati — bhavatāṃ svalakṣaṇaviṣayaṃ śāstramityabhyupagamaḥ । tato yadetadamumānaṃ sparśaś ca । na ca dṛṣṭānāṃ sparśa ityādinopanyastam etad yuṣmacchāstrādeva nimittādasvalakṣaṇaviṣayamuktam । āgamikatvaṃ bhavatāmeva prasiddhaṃ bruvatā na tu svaprasiddhimiti kiṃ sandhāyaivamuktamityāha — śabdaminirmuktaṃ liṅgamabhisandhāyeti । śabdenāgamākhyena tyaktametal liṅgaṃ sparśākhyam । tannirapekṣa eva sa yasmād vāyoḥ sattāṃ sādhayati । tadevaṃ tvadabhyupagataśāstravaśādakiñcitkaraṃ liṅgamabhipretya tajjamanumānaṃ mayedamasvalakṣaṇaviṣayamuktam na punaḥ svayamāgamikatvaṃ vāyvādīnāmicchatetyacodyam । evaṃ tarhi śābdamapi yathā svalakṣaṇaviṣayaṃ na bhavati pratipādyatāmityataḥ pratipādayitumāha — śābdamapi tvityādi । sambandhābhāva iti saṅketakāle । śabdārthasambandhā<II,27>bhijño hi saṅketakālānubhūtārthasāmānyameva pratipadyate śabdāt na svalakṣaṇam tasya pūrvamadṛṣṭatvāt । prayogakāle viśeṣaviṣayatvāśaṅkā na bhavatyeva । saṅketakāle tu pratyakṣaṃ svalakṣaṇamiti sambhavati tadviṣayatvāśaṅkā । ataḥ sambandhābhāva ityāha ॥

[II,27,i]

dṛṣṭārthaṃ yatrārthaḥ pratyakṣeṇa dṛśyate adṛṣṭārthaṃ viparyayāt । dṛṣṭārthe sañjñāvyutpattiriti । yathāyaṃ panasa ityatra sambandhavyutpattireva bhavati nānumānam arthasya pratyakṣatvāt । adṛṣṭārthe svargādāvarthavikalpamātramiti । na hi svargādiśabdāḥ svargādīnāṃ saṅketakāle 'nyadā vā svalakṣaṇaṃ buddhāvarpayanti anatīndriyatvaprasaṅgāt । kevalaṃ tatpratipādanābhiprāyaiḥ prayuktāḥ śrotaryapratibhāsamānatatsvabhāvamarthabimbamarpayantyasti kaścit surādhivāsaviśeṣa ityevamādikam । na caivaṃ svalakṣaṇaṃ pratipannaṃ bhavati pratipāditaṃ vā svargādiśravaṇe tadanubhāvināmiva pratibhāsabhedaprasaṅgāt । apratipadyamāno 'pi ca tatsvabhāvaṃ tathābhūta eva vikalpapratibimbe tadadhyavasāyī santuṣyati

<II,28>

[II,28,i]

tathābhūtatvādeva śabdārthapratipatteḥ । atra ca sambandhābhāva ityetannāpekṣyate । kiṃ tu dṛṣṭārtheṣveva । tatra hi dṛṣṭatvād viśeṣasya tasyaiva vācyatāśaṅkyeta । tatas tannivṛttyarthamuktam — sañjñāvyutpattiriti ॥

[II,28,ii]

kathaṃ tarhi tasyānumānatvamiti । api nāmāgamāt puruṣopayoginamarthamatīndriyaṃ niścitya yathārhamanutiṣṭhannāsādayeyamityāgamo mṛgyate । tataś cedarthavikalpamātraṃ bhavati na viśiṣṭārthapratītiḥ, tasyānumānatvameva hīyata ityabhiprāyaḥ । nanu ca yathānāptaprayuktānāṃ śabdānāṃ vivakṣālakṣaṇaṃ yadarthamātraṃ tadvacanādevānumānatvam na tu bāhyasyārthasyābhidhānāt tathāptaprayuktānāmapi syādityata āha — na hītyādi । evaṃ manyate — nāptavacaso vivakṣāmātre prāmāṇyameṣṭavyam, api tu bāhye 'pyarthe । anyathā kas tasyānāptavacanād viśeṣaḥ syāt । tasmānnāptaprayuktaiḥ svargādiśabdairarthamātramucyate । kiṃ tarhi । laukikaśabdāsādhāraṇo bāhyo 'pyartha iti ॥

{2.5}

[II,28,iii]

na svalakṣaṇavacanādāgamānāmanumānatvam । kiṃ tarhi । tathāvidham arthavikalpamātramupajanayatāṃ sāmānyākāreṇārthaprakāśanāt tatra cā<II,29>visaṃvādāditi darśayannāha — āptavādāvisaṃvādasāmānyādityādi । āptavacaso 'tyantaparokṣārthaviṣayasyetareṇa pratyakṣānumānadṛṣṭārthaviṣayeṇāptavacanenāvisaṃvādasāmānyādanumānatvamiti vākyārthaḥ ॥

[II,29,i]

nanu ca śabdānāmartheṣvapratibandhāt puruṣātiśayasya na niścetumaśakyatvādbāhye 'rthe prāmāṇyamevāyuktam । satyametat । ayaṃ punaratrābhiprāyaḥ — nāyaṃ puruṣo 'nāśrityāgamaprāmāṇyamāsituṃ śaktaḥ atyakṣaphalānāṃ keṣāñcinmahānuśaṃsāpāyaśravaṇāt tadbhāve virodhādarśanāc ca । tat sati pravartitavye varamevaṃ pravṛttiriti । ataḥ parīkṣayā prāmāṇyamāha । tatra puruṣārthasya śakyasya ca tadupāyasya yat pratipādanasamartham tac chāstraṃ parīkṣārhamiti tadeva parīkṣyeta anyatrāvadhānasyaivāyuktatvāt । tad yadi na visaṃvādabhāgbhavati pravartamānaḥ śobheta ॥

<II,30>

[II,30,i]

āptavacanaṃ gṛhītvetyādi । āptavacanaṃ gṛhītvāvisaṃvādādhigamahetuṃ tasyānumānatvamuktam । kasmāt punas tasyānumānatvamarthāvisaṃvādatulyatvāditi vyākhyeyam । kaḥ punarasyāvisaṃvādaḥ । pratyakṣābhimatānāṃ tathābhāvo 'tathābhimatānāṃ cāpratyakṣatā । tathānumānaviṣayābhimatānāṃ tathābhāvo 'tathābhūtānāṃ cānanumeyatā । seyaṃ śakyaparicchedāśeṣaviṣayapariśuddhiravisaṃvādaḥ । tatsāmānyamanumīyate pratyakṣānumānāgamye 'pyartha āptavacanatvamupalabhya — yadāptavacanam tadavisaṃvādi tadanyāptavacanavat । āptavacanaṃ cātyantaparokṣaviṣayaṃ kiñcid vacanam । svabhāvaḥ । tataś ca svalakṣaṇamaviṣayīkurvatāmapyāgamānāṃ na tadanyaśabdavad vivakṣāmātre prāmāṇyam । kiṃ tarhi arthe 'pi ॥

[II,30,ii]

atha vānyathāptavacanasyāvisaṃvādād anumānatvamucyate — heyopādeyatadupāyānāṃ tadupadiṣṭānāmavaiparītyamavisaṃvādaḥ । tathāsya puruṣārthopayogino 'nuṣṭhānārhasyāvisaṃvādād viṣayāntare 'pi tathātvopagamo na vipralambhāya anuparodhān niṣprayojanavitathābhidhānavaiphalyāc ca vaktuḥ ॥

<II,31>

[II,31,i]

tadetadagatyobhayathāpyanumānatvamāgamasyopavarṇitam — varamāgamāt pravṛttāvevaṃ pravṛttīriti । na khalvevamanumānamanapāyam anāntarīyakatvādarthaiḥ śabdānāmiti ॥

[II,31,ii]

atra cāptavacanaṃ gṛhītvāvisaṃvādo 'numīyate । anumite tasmin paścāt tata evāvisaṃvādādāptavacaso 'numānatvaṃ bhavati । anumānaśabdaś cātra liṅge vartate anumīyate 'neneti kṛtvānumitikāraṇatvād vā । avisaṃvādaḥ punarāptavacaso 'rthakāryatvāt । tat punaḥ pratipatturabhiprāyānurodhāt na tu vastuvaśāt ॥

[II,31,iii]

tathā hyāhetyanena svamataṃ śāstrāntareṇa saṃsyandayati । āptāḥ pratyakṣataḥ svargādīnāṃ svabhāvaṃ gṛhītvā sañjñāṃ praṇayanti । upalakṣaṇamātraṃ ca sañjñākarma veditavyam । sarvameva hi te 'rthadarśanapūrvakeveva vyāharanti । anyathāptā eva na syuḥ । tasmāt teṣāṃ sarvameva vaco 'visaṃvādi । ataś cānumānamiti ॥

[II,31,iv]

anayā diśeti । pradhānādibhiradṛṣṭasambandhatvāt talliṅgānāmāgamikā eva pradhānādaya iti pūrvānusāreṇa vācyam ॥

<II,32>

[II,32,i]

anumeye 'tha tattulya iti । athaśabdaḥ samuccayārthaḥ tattulye cetyarthaḥ । upalakṣaṇaṃ cānvayasya tattulye saddhāvo veditavyaḥ । yathā kākād dadhi rakṣyatāmityatra kākaḥ sarvasya śvāderupaghātakasya । etaduktaṃ bhavati — anvayaś ca dvitīyaṃ rūpamiti । evaṃ ca śrāvaṇatvasyāpyanityatve hetos trairūpyaṃ pratipāditaṃ bhavati na tvanyathā । na hi tasya tattulye saddhāvo 'sti । anvayas tu vidyate । anvayo hi nāma liṅge liṅgino bhāva eva । sa cāsti śrāvaṇatvasya । tathā hi — yatra śrāvaṇatvam tatrānityatvaṃ bhavatyeva । anyathā śrāvaṇatvameva nopapadyata iti pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ ॥

[II,32,ii]

nāstitāsatītyatrāsacchabdena na kevalaṃ tattulyābhāva ucyate, api tu tato 'nyas tadviruddhaś ca tadākāravivekāditi veditavyam । vyatirekopalakṣaṇaṃ vāsati nāstitvaṃ draṣṭavyam । vyatirekaś ca tṛtīyaṃ rūpamiti vākyārthaḥ ।

<II,33>

[II,33,i]

iha kevalayordharmadharmiṇoḥ siddhatvādanumeyatvaṃ nopapadyate । samudāyo 'pi yāvaddharmo na sidhyati tāvan na sambhavatyeva । na hyasanniviṣṭena buddhau dharmaṇa viśiṣṭo dharmī yujyate । siddhe tu dharmiṇi paścāt samudāyo jāyate । tadā cāsya sādhyatvaṃ nivartate siddhatvāt । tasmādanumeye hetoḥ sattvaṃ na sambhavatyeveti kasyacic codyamāśaṅkyāha — anumeyo hītyādi । atra yadyapi dharmaśabdaḥ sāmānyavācī tathāpi sādhanādhikārād yadarthaṃ sādhanamanviṣyate pratyāsattes tatraiva vartate । kaḥ punarasau । jijñāsito viśeṣalakṣaṇo dharmaḥ । na hyajijñāsite dharmiṇo dharme kaścit prakṣāvān sādhanaṃ pratyāhriyate । tasmāt siddhisattāke dharmiṇi yatrākṛṣṭaṃ sādhanam sa eva jijñāsito dharmo dharmaśabdena pratyāyyate । tena viśiṣṭo 'rthāntarād vyavacchinna ityarthaḥ । tataś cāyamevārtho bhavati — jijñāsitaviśeṣo dharmī iti । tathā hiyo yena jijñāsitena viśiṣṭo bhavati tasyāsau jijñāsito viśeṣo bhavati । samudāyaḥ sādhya ityapi vacanaṃ jijñāsitadharmāpekṣayaiva veditavyam ॥

<II,34>

[II,34,i]

uttarakālasiddhibhājā dharmeṇa pratinirdiśyate dharmaviśiṣṭo dharmīti । na tu liṅgadarśanakāle dharmaviśiṣṭatvamasti asaṃviditatvāddharmasyetyapare । jñāpakasya hetoradhikārāj jñānamarthākṣiptamiti niścityāha — tatra darśanamityādi । tatretyanumeye । pratyakṣata iti dhūmādeḥ । sadhūmaṃ hi pradeśamarthāntaraviviktarūpamasādhāraṇātmanā dṛṣṭavataḥ pratyakṣeṇa tadbalenaiva yathādṛṣṭabhedaviṣayaṃ niścitaṃ sa evāyamiti smārtaṃ liṅgajñānamuttarakālamutpadyate । na ca tat pramāṇam anadhigatārthakriyāyogyavastvanadhigamāt । ādyameva tu pramāṇam ato viparyayāt etallakṣaṇatvāt pramāṇasya । kuta etat । vastvadhiṣṭhānatvāt pramāṇavyavasthāyāḥ । etadapi kutaḥ । arthakriyāyogyaviṣayatvādarthipravṛtteḥ । etena dharmidharmādivikalpasyāprāmāṇyaṃ veditavyam । tataś ca ye codayanti — liṅgādijñānasya pratyakṣānumānānantarbhāvāt pramāṇāntaratvaṃ prāpnotīti te jāḍyamevātmanaḥ khyāpayanti ॥

[II,34,ii]

anumānato veti kṛtakatvādeḥ kādācitkatvādinā liṅgenānumīyamānatvāt । uttarakālamiti pratyekamabhisambadhyate — pratyakṣata uttarakālamanumānato vottarakālamiti । anumānaśabdaś cātra liṅgajñāne vartate । yathoktam — tadetat sākṣāt pāramparyeṇa vānumitikā<II,35>raṇatvādubhayamapyanumānaṃ karaṇaṃ kārakaṃ kṛtveti । dharmasya sāmānyarūpeṇeti । sāmānyarūpagrahaṇamasādhāraṇarūpanirāsārtham tenānumānāsambhavāt । na ca tat pratyakṣādipṛṣṭhabhāvinā viṣayīkartuṃ śakyate jñānena tasya savikalpakatvād vikalpānāṃ ca sāmānyaviṣayatvāt ॥

[II,35,i]

tajjātīye ceti । atrāpi sāmānyarūpeṇeti sambandhanīyam । nanu dharmiviśiṣṭasyānyatra vṛttivirodho 'viśeṣaṇe vā nānumeyadharmatā syāt । na ayogavyavacchedena viśeṣaṇāt yathā caitro dhanurdhara iti । yadi tarhi sādhanadharmasya viśeṣo 'numānānumeyavyavahāraṃ pratyanupayogīti sāmānyameva liṅgaṃ parigṛhyate sādhyadharmasyāpi tadeva grāhyam । na hi tasyāpi viśeṣas tatropayujyate ।  sāmānyasādhane ca siddhasādhyatā syāt । naiṣa doṣaḥ । sāmānyameva sādhyamayogavyavacchedena । na ca siddhasādhanam ayogavyavacchedasyāsiddheḥ ॥

[II,35,ii]

ekadeśagrahaṇena sapakṣāvyāpino 'pi hetutvaṃ darśayati । kuta etaditi । anumeyatattulyayos tulye sadbhāvavacana ekatra sarvatra sadbhāvo 'nyatraikadeśe 'pītyetat kuto hetorlabhyata iti pṛcchati । <II,36> vyavacchedaphalatvād vākyānāmiṣṭataś cāvadhāraṇādetal labhyata ityāha — tattulya evetyādi । anenānyayogavyavacchedenātrāvadhāraṇamāśritam yathā pārtho dhanurdhara iti darśayati । yadyevaṃ sādhyadharmiṇyavṛttiriti cet na anyaniṣedhārthatvāt । tatra vṛttau labdhāyāṃ samuccīyamānāvadhāraṇamanyad vyavacchinatti,
	naraṃ ca nārāyaṇameva cādau svataḥ sutau dvau janayāṃ babhūva
iti yathā ॥

[II,36,i]

na tarhi vaktavyamiti । ata evāvadhāraṇāt tadarthasya gatatvāditi manyate । etat punarityādi । niyamyate 'neneti niyamaḥ । sādharmyavān vaidharmyavāṃś ca prayoga ucyate । prayogavākyena hi pramāṇaṃ prakāśayatā kimayaṃ nitya uta neti pareṣāṃ saṃśayadolārūḍhā buddhiranitya evāyamityarthāntarād vyavacchidyānitya eva vyavasthāpyate । tasmāt prayogo niyamaḥ । tadarthaṃ tṛtīyaṃ rūpaṃ vaktavyam । anvayavyatirekayorniścitavyāptikamekamapi rūpaṃ prayuktamarthād dvitīyaṃ gamayatītyekasyāpi prayogaḥ syāditi । dvirūpaṃ tarhi liṅgaṃ prāptam । na anva<II,37>yavyatirekayoḥ pṛthagrūpatvāt । te tvekenāpi vākyena śakye darśayitumiti prayogasamāsa ucyate na rūpasamāsaḥ । tathā hyuktam — arthāpattyā vānyatareṇobhayapradarśanāditi ॥

[II,37,i]

syādetat — asati nāstitā nopapadyata eva asato 'dhikaraṇatvādyayogāt । śaktiprabhāvitāni hi kārakāṇi asataś ca sarvasāmarthyavirahādityata āha — asatveva nāstiteti । nipāto bhinnakramaḥ । asati nāstitaivetyevaṃ draṣṭavyaḥ । atha vā yathānyāsamevāstu ॥

[II,37,ii]
